me long gi rgya dpe zhig gtad nas/ cung zad khro tshul bcas/ khyod snying rul/ tshe 'dir chu 'di las brgal mi nus/ 'on kyang phyi mar dka' ba med par thar bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes
zer ro/ /drug par/ bsam yas mchims phu'i kun mkhyen dri med 'od zer gyi gdung 'bum yin rgyu de'i 'khris nas phar phyin pa na/ se ba'i phung po me tog rgyas pa zhig gi
khrod nas rje bla ma dhI kA sha'i zhabs kyi phyag bris yin pa'i shog dril zhig rnyed/ stod cha der tshig 'ga' zhig 'dug kyang brjed/ gsham der snyan brgyud 'chi med bcud
len zur du bris pa 'di ji lta ba bzhin gda'/ der sems spro snang gis tshar kha shas klog pa blo la gsal ba byung / de mtshams rje bla ma dhI kA sha'i zhabs mjal/ 'di ltar
'dug ces zhus pas/ re zhig ci yang mi gsung / dar cig na/ de 'bar ba'i snyan brgyud zab shos shig yin/ ngas tsA rir 'gro dus bris pa yin ces phebs/ de rjes tsam du rdo rje
'dzin dbang bA gindra mjal bar 'phros zhus pas/ dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur dang bcas thod phreng rgyan ldan zhig gnang nas/ dam tshig gtsang ba yin 'dug /ces dang / dam tshig
'di ni 'da' bar dka'/ /de bas srog bzhin gces par zungs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i snang ba byung / bdun par/ lha ldan sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang du slebs pa na/ nang skor du
phyin par/ rang gi lag tu 'bras dkar gyis khengs pa'i rin po che'i za ma tog zhig 'dug pa nas 'thor bzhin du phyin pas/ sa la chags rim bzhin du me tog dkar po re re lam
lam skyes/ spro snang bcas jo bo rin po che'i mdun du slebs/ der mar me brgya kong zhig spar chog byas 'dug pa'i 'khris der ngo mi 'tshal ba'i mi zhig gis/ sku zhabs kyi
grub

rtags khyad par 'phags/ da mar me 'di rnams la thugs smon gnang na rang 'bar du yong / de byung na smon lam gang btab myur du 'grub zer bar/ mar me la dmod btsugs te me tog
'thor bas rang 'bar du byung / der phan bde 'byung ba'i sogs dang / 'jig rten bde zhing sogs kyi smon lab btab pas/ da ci'i de na re/ rang don du'ang smon lam re mdzod zer
bar/ phar ltos dpon med tshul ltos g.yog med cing / /'dul rgyu'i dgra med bskyang rgyu'i gnyen med par/ /dben pa'i gnas su rang sems 'dul ba dang / /rlabs chen rgyal sras
spyod pa mthar phyin shog /ces btab pas yi rangs pa'i rnam 'gyur ston to/ /brgyad par/ btsun pa bgres song zhig gis glegs bam chen po zhig gtad 'di phreng ba skor gsum
gyi don 'grel grub chen mi tra dzo kis mdzad pa de yin zer/ zhal phyes pas/ thog ma der srid spel dang / de 'og byis pa la 'jug pa'i sgo dang / sman dpyad sogs nas/ mthar
dus 'khor las gsungs pa'i bcud len sogs yod pa/ dpe tshan shin tu mang ba/ bo dong pa'i de nyid 'dus chen gyi snying po bsdus pa lta bu zhig 'dug /de tsam na lung yod
med dpyod pa'i snang ba shar ma thag /rje bla ma wA gindra dang mjal/ lung yod kyang brgyud pa nges 'drongs mi 'dug gsungs/ cung zad na mdun gyi nam mkhar slob dpon rin po
che dang / grub chen mi tra gang yin ma 'tshal ba zhig byin gyis rlob rlob ltar bzhugs pa'i 'phror gnyid sad do/ /dgu par/ mi zhig gis bsam yas nas bskur ba yin zer rgya
ma chen po zhig sprad/ kha phye bas gnam lcags rdo rje dngos gtsang khyad mtshar zhig 'dug /der mi des/ 'di las cung chung ba zhig yod pa ma

hA sandhi par phul bas thugs mnyes po rang byung song / 'di na nyin nas sku zhabs rang la 'bul snyam yang / thugs bca' gnang gi med dam snyam pas gzhag /da lan thugs bca' gnang
ba 'dra zer bas phul ba lags zer ba'i 'phror bzhad mo mang du 'chor ba zhig byung ngo / /bcu par/ rang nyid skye yul yin snyam pa'i sman ljongs nyams dga' ba zhig tu
slebs par/ bdud rtsi ril bur 'gro ba'i sngo sman rnams tshol ba'i 'dun pas phyin par phal cher zhig rnyed/ slar phyin pas a ru ra'i nags tshal tho re ba zhig tu slebs/ de
na sman gyi drang srong yin zer ba'i dge slong bgres po skra dang sma ra dkar po can zhig 'dug pas/ sngo sman mang po'i ngos 'dzin dang / sman sbyor kha shas gsungs/ de
la yul 'di rgya bal gyi sa cha zhig yin 'dra bas ji skad zer ba lags zhus par/ bde mchog gi gnas khyad par can yin/ sku rang byon kyang bzhugs pas mjal du 'dong zhes khrid/
khang bzang cung zad gog pa zhig gi sgo phye ba'i nang du/ mtsho nag ngam pa zhig gi dbus su bde mchog gi sku blos mi 'khyud pa'i chen po zhig mjal/ zil bsam gyis mi
khyab pas re zhig brgyal ba snyam byed do/ /bcu gcig par/ srod khra 'brug tu slebs/ paN chen nags rin gyi sku de mjal bas/ cung zad na sku dngos su song / phyag gis reg cing
/ khyod kyis dbang ji tsam thob gsungs/ thob tshul rags pa zhus pas/ skal bzang dang dam nyams gnyis ka mang du bsags 'dug phebs/ spyir sngags kyi dam tshig srung shin
tu dka' na'ang rtsa ba che rigs dang 'gal ba cher mi bdog zhus pas/ gnad ma go ba mtshangs che/ tha mal gyi snang zhen dang bcas pas dbang tshig 'chad nyan

tsam la'ang ltung ba char bzhin 'babs gsungs/ 'o na dbang gtan nas mi zhu ba legs sam zhus pa/ de 'dra ga la yin/ rdzas ldog so sor phye dgos pa yin mod gsungs pas/ bod snga
phyi'i sngags kyi phyag len yangs dog dang / jo bo rjes/ so sor thar pa'i nyes pas gtan nas ma gos sogs dang / 'jam dbyangs bla mas/ rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa ni/ /sogs
la go ba khyad par can skye ba snyam byed pa byung / der nyid kyi padma tshe khrid de gnang dgos zhus pas/ dpe brlag nas med gsungs/ thugs nas gnang bas khyab lags sam
zhus par/ gdams ngag dgos na dbang bskur ba dgos pa yin mod gsung ba'i 'phror sku rang du song ngo / /tho rangs/ phreng ba'i skor la 'bel gtam mang du bgyis kyang brjed/
dran pa zhig la/ abha yas/ rgyud sde so sor ma phyes zer ba mi bden te/ rgyud sde phyi nang gnyis su phye zhing / nang la'ang khyad chos ma 'dres par bshad pa'i phyir/ de
la'ang rgyu mtshan yod de/ lam dang 'bras bu dngos btags ldog pa dang bcas pa'i dbye ba dang / bslab pa gsum rdzogs pa'i dbang du byas pa'i phyir/ 'on kyang phyag len la
gnyis ka gnang ste/ ma nges pa'i dbang rnon dang / bla med kho nar nges pa'i dbang rnon dag gi ched du'o/ /de lta mod kyi da lta'i phyag len ltar na'ang don gyis bla med
du 'gyur te/ thog ma nas de'i dbang bskur ba tsam gyis rgyud bde stong chen po'i ngo bor bsdoms zin pa'i phyir ro/ /zhes sogs rgyu mtshan dang bcas te smra ba zhig byung
ngo / /zhes bka' stsal pa ltar ya mtshan pa'i mnal nyams khyad par can dang bcas gsan par mdzad do/ /phan bde bzang po las kyang rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang

bskur phal cher dang / 'jam nag /gza' yum/ gshed dmar rnams kyi rjes gnang / ngag dbang lhun grub las/ kun rig dbang / seng gdong / gur drag /seng ge sgra rnams kyi rjes gnang
/ tshe rta zung 'brel dbang / tshul khrims dpal bzang las seng ge sgra/ gshed dmar sogs kyi rjes gnang / kun dga' bsam 'grub las rnam 'joms rjes gnang dang / tshe rta
zung 'brel/ chos grags las rnam 'joms rjes gnang / ngag dbang bkra shis las tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi dbang / rnam 'dren dam pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho las tshe dpag
lha dgu'i dbang 'chi bslu dang 'brel ba/ ri khrod ma/ tshe rta zung 'brel sogs gsan/ dpal ldan phrin las las kye rdor rgyu lam/ ba ri brgya rtsa/ snar thang brgya rtsa/
/sgrol ma bar chad kun sel rnams kyi rjes gnang sogs dang / tshe rta zung 'brel/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ byams pa bstan 'dzin rnam rgyal las zhu chen
pa'i bcu gcig zhal gyi smyung gnas lung / bla ma ngag dbang grags pa las rab gnas dpal 'byor rgya mtsho'i lung / ngag gi dbang po las 'jam dpal shes rab 'khor lo dang
/ gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang lung bcas gsan/ rdo rje slob dpon bsod nams phun tshogs las dus 'khor bu lugs dbang rdzogs pa/ brgyud 'debs/ sgrub dkyil lung / rdo rje
shugs/ sna tshogs yum/ rdo rje khyung khra rnams kyi rjes gnang / rnam sras ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang bcas/ chos rje dge legs rgyal mtshan las sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis/
'chi 'joms/ nyi sbas sgrol ma nyer gcig /tshe dpag dkar po/ khro mo sme brtsegs/ bcu

gcig zhal/ mi 'khrugs pa rnams gsan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa ngag dbang bzang po las/ thugs rje chen po phyag chen zung 'jug /tshe dpag med sprul sku/ bde mchog bong zhal can/ dgra
nag /rigs gsum spyi dbang sogs/ dpal ldan don grub las/ bcu gcig zhal/ thugs chen skyer sgang lugs/ 'jig byed dpa' gcig /bir srung / phrin las rab rgyas las thang lugs
tshe dbang / de'i yig cha'i lung / zhabs drung byams pa kun dga' dpal bzang las sa ru pa'i lugs gcod skor yongs rdzogs kyi smin grol gsan/ 'jam dbyangs blo gsal las tshe
dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra'i dbang / gsang 'dus spyan ras gzigs dbang / 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i dbang / 'jigs byed rwa pod kyi lung / ngor chen bka' 'bum pod bzhi/ zhu
chen bka' 'bum pod brgyad kyi lung sogs gsan/ nA lendra'i gzim 'og mchog sprul rin po che byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'dzin snyan grags zhal snga nas dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed/
de'i brgyud 'debs lung / blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral/ de'i don 'grel grags pa/ sa paN/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags/ kun dga' legs rin bcas kyis mdzad pa'i khrid lung /
grub chen mi tra'i tshe dpag dkar po'i rjes gnang / de'i brgyud 'debs/ sgrub skor/ rjes gnang bcas kyi yig cha'i lung / sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrags kyi rjes gnang dang
khrid lung / sgrub thabs kyi lung / dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ bo dong lugs kyi dbyangs can dkar mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ bo dong pas mdzad pa'i de'i
sgrub thabs tshig lhug /gegs sel/ sbyin sreg /bstod pa dang bcas

pa'i lung sogs dbyangs can ma'i skor gyi rjes gnang bklag lung mang du gsan/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang / sa lugs thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum gyi rjes gnang lung bcas/
thugs rje chen po tshem bu lugs kyi khrid/ yig cha skor du ma'i lung / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs/ rta mgrin pad dbyug can gyi lung / rta mgrin zla rgyal lugs
kyi rjes gnang / khyung nag 'byung po 'ur 'ded kyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ o rgyan rin po che la brten pa'i bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga grub gnyis 'dod 'jo'i bsam 'phel/ o
rgyan bstod pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi dmigs rim khyer bde bcas kyi lung / lcam dral lha gsum gyi rjes gnang / nyid mdzad mgon po'i bla mchod dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi
brgyud 'debs/ sgrub thabs/ smon lam gyi lung sogs zab chos mang du gsan/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor mas mngon sum rjes su bzung ba mkhas shing grub pa'i rdo rje slob dpon
chen po dpal zhwa lu ri sbugs mchog sprul rin po che rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong gi zhal snga nas snga phyir bka' chos rgya mtsho gsan pa'i zegs ma tsam bkod par/
sems tsam lugs kyi sems bskyed/ rigs byed ma'i rjes gnang phyi sgrub thun mong ba/ dzaM dmar rjes gnang lung bcas/ mgon po beng dmar rjes gnang lung bcas/ gtor chog lung
/ phyag rdor 'byung 'dul sems dpa' sum brtsegs kyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ thub dbang 'od zer dri med lha bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i
dbang / don yod zhags pa lha mang gi dbang chen/ dbang chog gi lung / dpal rdo rje dbyings rtsa ba'i lugs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi dbang bskur chen mo sngon dngos rjes tshang
/ dkyil chog

sogs kyi lung bcas/ dpal rdo rje rtse mo rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang bka' bcu tham pa tshang ba/ mtshan brjod rnal 'byor rgyud du bkral pa 'jam dpal gsang ldan gyi
dbang chen/ shAkya seng ge gtsug tor dgu pa'i dbang / rnam 'joms dkar po lha bcu dgu ma'i dbang / phyag rdor 'gro bzang lugs kyi dbang chen/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin
rlabs rgyas pa tshar lugs ltar/ nyid gsung rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga /gegs sel sogs kyi lung / dpal mchog rdor sems/ mi 'khrugs bcu gsum ma/ 'jigs byed dpa'
gcig rnams kyi lung / ni gu'i skor rje nyid kyi chog khrigs tshang ma'i dbang byin rlabs/ su kha'i byin rlabs/ rtsa khrid/ stan gcig ma/ lhan thabs rnams kyi khrid lung
/ su kha'i khrid/ phyag chen gwa'u ma'i byin rlabs khrid dang bcas pa/ yig cha'i lung / bde mchog dril bu pa'i dbang / bde mchog mai tri bcu gsum ma'i dbang / bde mchog sdom
'byung gi dbang / bde mchog spyan ras gzigs padma drwa ba'i dbang / bde mchog lwa ba bcu gsum ma'i dbang / ma hA mA yA'i dbang / bde mchog sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi
dbang / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gdan bzhi yab bka'i dbang / gsang 'dus 'jam rdor dbang / gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug dbang / gshin rje gdong drug gi dbang / dpal dus
kyi 'khor lo bu lugs kyi dbang bskur chen mo sngon dngos rjes tshang / grub thob tshe sgrub kyi dbang / jo nang khrid brgya'i gsung khrid/ pod dbang / lung bcas/ thugs rje
chen po tshem bu dmar khrid kyi gsung bshad sngon 'gro nas brtsams mthar chags su rgyas spros bcas/ bde mchog dril bu lugs kyi bskyed rdzogs kyi zab khrid/ ti phu'i tshe
sgrub zhal shes ma'i zhal

khrid/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid/ mi tra lugs kyi thugs chen yi ge bzhi pa'i byin rlabs/ rdzogs rim phyag chen sems nyid ngal gso'i khrid/ tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi
tshe'i nyams khrid zab mo zhag bdun dang / 'ba' ra ba'i tshe khrid rin chen gter mdzod sogs kyi lung / byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba/ tshe sgrub bu ston gong
khug ma'i khrid lung / lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi pod gzhung / bu ston yo ga'i chos 'byung rnal 'byor rgyud kyi rgya mtshor 'jug pa'i gru gzings/ bu ston rin po che'i
rdor dbyings mchod phreng / rje nyid mdzad dbang gis sdom rigs pa'i 'phrul 'byed/ lam 'bras pod nag ma/ rje nyid mdzad rnal 'byor ma'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ chos nyid dngos
bstan gyi zin bris sogs/ zhwa lu pa'i gdan rabs glegs bam/ sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ tshar lugs bla ma'i rnam thar skor las/ bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa/ tshar chen rje/ mkhyen brtse/ mang thos klu sgrub/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen
bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rta ra ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ zhwa lu mkhan chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ nyid mdzad sa skya pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa bcas kyi rnam thar de dag gi ljags lung sogs sgrub thabs/ khrid zin/ las tshogs sogs kyi bklags lung rab
tu mang po gsan no/ /gong dkar po ta la pa mkhan chen rin po che bstan 'dzin tshul khrims mdun nas/ dpal mchog dang po 'jig

rten las 'das pa dang 'jig rten pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu bzhi rdul tshon gyis bzhengs pa'i steng nas dbang skur yongs su rdzogs pa sngon dngos rjes tshang dang / sa lugs yang dag
lha dgu'i dbang rdzogs par gsan/ brag sgom zhabs drung ma hA paNDi ta dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas bka' chos mang du gsan pa las/ gsang
bde 'jigs gsum sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ bde mchog sngags btu'i lung / dbyangs can dmar mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ 'jam bzhad gnyis pa'i yi dam sgrub skor nas/ 'jam dkar/
dmar ser/ phag dkar/ gdugs dkar 'don thabs/ rnam 'joms bum chog bcas kyi lung / dri med 'od/ rdo rje snying 'grel/ rgyan 'jug /rgyan 'grel don gsal/ zhwa lu'i chos spyod
las chu gtor ma gtogs tshang ba/ blo sbyong chen mo/ lam rim zin bris bcas kyi lung / rje rin po che'i yon tan gzhir gyur ma/ rin chen gsum gyi gtam/ phyag rdor stod 'grel/
nag po gzhung drug /dril bu skor gsum/ lU hi pa'i sgrub thabs che ba/ phreng ba skor gsum/ rgya mtsho/ sgron gsal/ mdor byas/ mdo bsre/ rnam gzhag rim pa/ dkyil chog nyi
shu pa/ byang chub sems 'grel/ rim lnga/ zung 'jug gsal ba/ klu sgrub bstod tshogs/ dpag bsam 'khri shing / mdo kun btus/ bskal bzang rgyan phreng / skyes rabs so bzhi
pa/ bslab btus/ spyod 'jug /byang sa/ ched du brjod pa'i tshoms/ byams chos phyi ma bzhi/ rigs tshogs drug /tshad ma mdo/ rnam 'grel sogs sde bdun/ so thar mdo/ 'dul ba
mdo rtsa/ sum brgya pa/ me tog phreng rgyud/ 'od ldan/

mngon pa mdzod/ kun btus/ dbu ma bzhi brgya pa/ 'jug pa rang 'grel/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ snar thang brgya rtsa/ rin spungs skor gsum/ blo sbyong brgya rtsa/ thogs
med bka' 'bum/ snyan brgyud chen mo/ bla ma lnga bcu pa/ rtsa ltung dang sbom po'i rtsa ba/ spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan pa'i 'dul ba'i sdom tshig /dge tshul slong byang
sngags bcas kyi phyir bcos/ gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa rnams legs par gsan/ gzhan yang rje rin po che'i lam gyi gtso bo rnam gsum gyi lung / bka'
gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang / rnam snang mngon byang gi dbang / de'i sgrub dkyil sogs kyi lung / gshed dmar bcu gsum ma'i dbang / dril bu lha lnga'i dbang / sgrub
dkyil lung / dril bu lus dkyil dbang / de'i sgrub skor sogs kyi lung / phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi dbang / u tsarYa dang / sems dpa' sum brtsegs kyi rjes gnang / 'jigs byed
dug dbang / rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i yi dam sgrub skor nas spyan ras gzigs dang / sgrol dkar rjes gnang / byang chub sems dpa'i nor bu'i phreng bcas kyi lung / bka'
gdams glegs bam rin po che yongs rdzogs/ bka' gdams thor bu/ po to ba'i chig lab ring mo/ /byang chub 'od kyi zhal gdams/ ding ri brgyad cu/ ang yig bdun cu pa/ tho lcogs
drug pa/ nag tsho'i jo bstod brgyad cu pa/ man ngag lhan thabs/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa ngag dbang brtson 'grus kyi 'jam dkar/ dbyangs can dkar mo/
srad brgyud lugs kyi ri khrod ma rigs gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ so so'i las sbyor dang bcas pa'i lung / stag phu ba'i rnal 'byor ma'i bskyed

rdzogs chen mo baiDUr zhun ma'i them skas/ thu'u bkAn pas mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor ma'i bskyed rdzogs kyi dmigs rim shin tu zab pa bde chen bcud kyi snying po/ paN chen dpal ldan
ye shes kyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa srid gsum 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu'i 'grel chen rdo rje gsum gyi snang ba zhes khri gung thang pas bkod pa'i glegs bam bcas kyi lung / blo
sbyong nyi ma'i 'od zer/ yongs 'dzin rin po che'i don bdun ma/ blo sbyong tshig rkang brgyad ma/ tshem bu dmar khrid bcas kyi khrid/ bka' gdams chos 'byung chen mo'i lung
bcas/ gso dpyad rgyud bzhi/ sa paN tshig gter/ sdeb sbyor rin 'byung / me tog chun po/ snyan ngag me long / sgra ka lA pa/ dbyangs can sgra mdo rtsa 'grel bcas kyi lung
sogs dbang rjes gnang bklag lung / zhal khrid sogs shin tu rgya chen gsan no/ /dga' ldan khri rin po che 'jam dpal tshul khrims las bla ma'i rnal 'byor dga' ldan lha brgya
ma'i khrid lung / shar rtse grags pa bstan dar las 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i snying po dang / byang rtse blo bzang mkhas grub las yon tan gzhir gyur ma sogs kyi lung / rwa
sgreng khri chen rin po che las lam gyi gtso bo rnam gsum gyi lung / mchog sprul blo bzang mthu stobs las tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / bya spyod spyi'i cho ga'i lung
/ dbu ma'i lta khrid skor gyi gsung bshad/ ka chen nor bu don grub las paN chen dpal yes kyis mdzad pa'i dug dbang bskur tshul/ rigs byed ma'i bstod lung / sgrub thabs brgya
rtsa'i rgya gzhung gi lung bcas gsan/ lha btsun 'jam pa'i rdo rje ye shes don grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas/ thub pa dam tshig gsum bkod
lha lnga/ sman bla zhe bdun ma/ gdugs dkar

lha mang / rnam 'joms mthing ga lha bco lnga/ gza' yum lha bcu bzhi/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ 'jigs byed skyo lugs zhe dgu ma/ dge lugs 'jigs byed dpa' gcig /'brug lugs ras chung
tshe dpag med nang sgrub zhi ba lha mang / gsang sgrub khro bo lha mang / ngam rdzong lugs kyi bde mchog lus dkyil/ stag lung pa'i dgyes rdor dznyA na lugs/ kye rdor
ting 'dzin dbang bzhi/ khros nag lha lnga rnams kyi dbang chen/ khro phu lo tsA'i man ngag brgya rtsa 'bring po'i lung / gtum mo zhag bdun/ zhag gsum ma/ rlung / chu/ me
tog bcas kyi bcud len/ rde'u'i bcud len bcas pa'i phyag khrid lung bcas/ ma ning ha 'don gyi khrid/ ding ri brgyad cu pa/ dam pa'i mkhyud dpyad dkar nag khra gsum/ 'jigs
byed nag po'i dug srung / grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe khrid/ 'ba' ra ba'i yig cha tshang ma/ khyung po'i mgur brgyad/ sgrol dkar/ 'jam dbyangs smra seng / 'jam dpal nag po/
/seng gdong sngon mo gong dkar lugs/ dbyangs can dkar mo rnams las sngar ma gsan pa'i yig cha ci rigs kyi lung sogs gsan/ dpe chos rin chen spungs pa/ gtam rgyud rin chen
phreng mdzes/ man ngag rin chen spungs pa rnams ngag dbang legs grub las gsan/ mchog sprul ye shes thub bstan rgya mtsho las thig le bcu drug gi rgyun khyer dbang khrid
gtsos rjes gnang dang lung 'ga' tsam gsan/ ser byes rab 'byams pa dge bshes ye shes gong 'phel las nag tsho'i jo bstod brgyad cu pa/ 'brom gyi jo bstod sum cu pa/ 'brom
gyi lha chos mi chos gnad phreng / lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi zhal gdams/ 'chad ka ba'i don bdun ma'i

rtsa tshig /blo sbyong thun gcig ma/ chos gsum dri len dang rgyal sras lag len/ rgya ma spyan snga ba'i blo sbyong bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs kha che'i snying gtam bcu
gsum ma rnams kyi lung / byang sems ra sgreng ba'i blo sbyong byang sems chu rgyun/ po to ba'i man ngag beu bum sngon po/ bka' gdams gsar rnying gi chos 'byung chen mo
sogs gsan/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen rab 'byams pa grags pa lhun grub las spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi blo sbyong chos kyi sgo 'byed/ 'jam mgon byams pa phun tshogs las
lam rim 'jam dpal zhal lung gi khrid dang sems bskyed/ lam rim bsdus don khrid lung bcas/ bkra shis lhun po'i ka chen rnam rgyal rgyal mtshan las pa ri brgya rtsa'i rgya
gzhung yongs rdzogs kyi lung / ka chen rin po che blo bzang dge legs kun khyab las paN chen na bza' ba'i be bum dgos 'dod kun 'byung lung bcas gsan pa'i tshul 'dir mdo
tsam mo/ /o rgyan smin grol gling gi khri chen rin po che 'gyur med sangs rgyas kun dga'i zhal snga nas/ bka' ma'i yang dag lha dgu so lugs kyi dbang / nyid mdzad dong sprugs
kyi sbyin sreg lung / nyang gter drag dmar pod rags rim/ thugs rje chen po 'gro 'dul phal cher tshang ba/ chos dbang bla ma gsang 'dus dbang yongs rdzogs/ lung rags
rim/ thugs chen yang snying 'dus pa'i dbang / lung 'ga' re/ phur pa spu gri'i dpang lung cha tshang / las 'brel phyag rdor gtum po'i skor 'ga' re/ pad gling tshe khrid rdo
rje phreng ba'i skor 'ga' zhig gi lung / rig 'dzin thugs thig dbang / tshe dbang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs char 'bebs khrid lung / rdor sems dbang / rtsa khrid
bcas/ rje btsun rin po che 'gyur med phrin las

chos sgron las snga phyir dbang lung khrid gsum mang du gsan pa las/ gtso bor bla ma yang tig yid bzhin nor bu'i dbang lung khrid gsum cha tshang / thugs chen rgyal po lugs
kyi lung khrid/ nyang gter gtum mo zhag bdun ma'i dbang khrid 'brel ma lung bcas/ chos dbang rin po che'i zhal gdams 'ga' re/ ra shag mdos bcu stod smad 'phyang bcas/ thang
lugs tshe rta zung 'brel/ pad gling nag po skor gsum/ man ngag gter phran/ nyi zla sangs rgyas 'pho ba 'jag tshugs ma'i khrid lung / snyan brgyud ma bcas/ dkon mchog
spyi 'dus rtsa dbang / tshe dbang / bshar khrid bcas/ thugs tig rtsa dbang / tshe dbang / rtsa khrid bcas/ lo chen rin po che'i rtsa khrid ngo sprod/ rtsa dbang dang tshe
dbang mtshams sbyor bcas kyi lung / rdor sems dbang / rtsa khrid/ rmi lam dang / 'pho khrid/ lo chen rin po che'i gsung tshang ma'i lung / rin rnam lhan thabs mdzes rgyan
bcas/ a ti'i rtsal dbang / khrid/ lung tshang ma/ drag dmar dbang gsum dregs pa'i srog dbang bcas/ rin rnam bsnyen yig /zhi sbyin/ tshe sgrub/ mi 'gyur dpal sgron gyi lha
khrid/ dmigs rim bcas kyi lung / dregs 'joms lung / thugs rje chen po'i rtsa dbang / mchog dbang / gtor dbang / gar tshe/ gsang ye/ lha chen bcas/ rtsa khrid/ gtum mo'i
shar khrid/ pod rags rim/ lo chen gyi rtsa khrid snying po stan cig ma/ au Di yA na'i gar tshe'i bsnyen yig /khyung ras pa'i nang sgrub gsal byed zung 'jug rnam rol dang
/ gsang sgrub gsal byed/ lha chen bsnyen yig sogs kyi lung / lo chen gyis mdzad pa'i chos spyod phyi ma las 'ga' zhig dang / nang gi chos

spyod/ thun drug /smyung gnas cho ga /klu chog /zhi byed skor cha tshang / gcod dbang dang / khrid lung / g.ya' bzang ba'i lugs kyi gza' bcos gsal byed bcas kyi lung / nyid
mdzad gsang snying bshad rgyun gsol 'debs spyi don dang 'brel ba/ a nu yo ga lung bdun gyi 'chad tshul/ nyang gter khros nag rgyun khyer/ bsnyen yig /thugs chen bder 'dus
sngon 'gro'i khrid yig /thun mong sngon 'gro'i zin bris/ gtum mo'i gsol 'debs/ rdor sems 'pho khrid/ gter gsar skor gyi brgyud 'debs/ lha btsun pa'i gcod yul dpa' bo'i
thol glu'i zin bris snang srid rang grol rnams dang / lo chen rin po che'i rgyud chog /padma dbang rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i rgyud 'chad thabs kyi zin bris lung sogs gsan/ dge
slong dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'gyur med phun tshogs zhal snga nas rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che yongs su rdzogs pa gsal dag snyan gsum dang ldan pa'i sgo nas blo kha tshims
par thob pas mi lus tsam po ba thob pa 'di don cung zad dang ldan par gyur snyam rnam pa kun tu rjes su dran to/ /zhes gsungs/ dge slong sngags rab slob dpon 'gyur med
don grub las/ lo chen rin po ches mdzad pa'i so thar las chog /gzhi gsum/ sdom gsum rnam nges/ gsang bdag dgongs rgyan/ chos spyod tshang ba bcas gsan/ dge slong dge ba'i
bshes gnyen sngags rab 'gyur med bstan 'phel las/ gter chen rin po che'i gsung rab glegs bam bcu gsum yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gter gsar skor gter gzhung cha tshang
gi lung bcas gsan/ rgyal sras gzhan phan mtha' yas las/ gu ru tshe brtan rgyal mtshan gyi gter ma rta mgrin brgya rtsa dang / nyid mdzad grub mtha'

ris med gsol 'debs kyi lung / klong sde rna brgyud rdo rje zam pa'i dbang lung khrid/ sems sde a don bco brgyad kyi dbang lung khrid/ kun byed don khrid/ gnubs kyi shog dril
bcu/ 'bri gung chos grags gshin rje'i be bum nag por gnubs kyi gong khug brgya rtsar mtshan gsol ba/ rta mgrin yang khros rtsa dbang tshe dbang / bka' srung srog gtad bcas/
pusti yongs rdzogs kyi nang tshan kha shas ma gtogs tshang ma sogs bka' chos khyad 'phags rab tu mang ba gsan/ rdzogs chen mkhan rin po che padma dam chos 'od zer ram
padma badzra'i zhal snga nas/ snga 'gyur bka' ma'i phrin chog phyogs bsdus glegs bam dgu'i lung yongs rdzogs/ mkhyen brtse'i bka' 'bum lung yongs rdzogs/ rdzogs chen rgyud

/ kha thun dbang / rong phur dbang / rog phur dbang / dong sprugs zhi khro rigs bsdus 'gro ba kun sgrol dang / rigs bsdus padma brgya ldan gyi dbang / bka' brgyad rdzong

cha lag /rnam dag dbang gi chu rgyun/ srung ba'i sdom/ zhal shes phyag len/ 'khor lo khyung gsum bcas/ bum chung / bzang po grags pa'i 'khor lo 'bar ba'i rtsa ba/ brda don

'bebs skor

bcas/ dri med rdo rje'i za yig nor bu'i bang mdzod/ mnga' ris paN chen gyi yon tan gter mdzod/ legs ldan rje'i bla ma sku gsum dang / nam mkha' zas za/ byang bdag tshe sgrub
sku gsum rigs 'dus/ drag po karma gu ru'i dbang lung chog bsgrigs bcas cha tshang / dag snang mdos chog snang srid spyi skong / ba mkhal ba'i gsol 'debs bar chad lam sel/

gcud 'khor dpe'u ris dang sbrags pa/ gu ru jo tshe'i sha brgya zan brgya/ sna nam thub rgyal gto bcos brgya rtsa/ zur mkhar a jo bal po'i bsod nams glang po stobs skyed/
zangs gling dbang phyug gtad hrul/ rad gling yang zlog dang gtad hrul/ a tsA' ra dmar po'i ser srung / gter ston tshe ring rdo rje'i spyi ti'i skor gyi dbang lung tshang
ba/ gter ston dri med lhun po'i don tig dang / zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi zab tig chos dbyings rang gsal brgyud pa'i chu bo gnyis 'dres las phyi ma gtso bor byas pa'i dbang

mang bka' brgyud las byon pa'i bde mchog snyan brgyud chen mo'i dbang dang byin rlabs thams cad/ 'khor lo lnga'i gzhung pod tshang ma'i lung / chos skyong ma mgon zhal sbyor
dbang chen/ phyag bzhi pa'i dbang che chung / ma mgon 'khor lnga tshe ring ma sogs kyi rjes gnang / jo nang rin 'byung dang / rje dgu pa dbang phyug rdo rje'i zhi phreng
drag phreng chos skyong glog phreng bcas kyi rjes gnang / rang byung ba'i zab mo nang don/ rnam shes ye shes/ snying po bstan pa rnams kyi bshad lung / mar mi dwags
gsum byin rlabs/ phyag chen khrid rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang nA ro chos drug sogs kyi khrid lung / shangs lugs rgyud sde lnga'i dbang chen/ bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang dang
khrid/ ni gu chos drug jo nang lugs kyi byin rlabs rnams dang khrid/ zur mang dang gnas mdo lugs kyi gcod dbang gcod khrid/ grub chen brgyad cu'i byin rlabs jo nang nas
brgyud pa/ gzhan yang rjes gnang gi rigs/ gong smos rnams kyi yig cha dang chags med gsung skor gtsor gyur lung gi rnam grangs shin tu mang por phul/ rnying ma'i skor
la rnying ma rgyud 'bum spar pod nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bklag lung / rnying ma bka' ma drag dmar 'o bran lugs/ bka' brgyad rdzong 'phrang / rong lugs phur pa/ rog phur lha nag
/gdong drug nag po/

gsang rdzogs thugs kyi sgrub pa/ gshin rje gshed kha thun nag po/ gshed dmar ru mtshon dmar po rnams kyi dbang / de dag gi gzhung pod tshang ma'i lung / dong sprugs zhi khro
khrom dkrugs dang padma brgya ldan gyi dbang / gter ma'i phyogs la nyang gter bka' brgyad bder 'dus gzhung pod dgu'i lung / chos dbang gsang rdzogs kyi dbang chen/ don
dbang / gzhung pod bzhi'i lung / byang gter bka' brgyad rang shar/ rig 'dzin gdung sgrub/ thugs sgrub drag po rtsal/ thugs rje chen po/ rdzogs chen dgongs pa zang thal/ phur
pa che mchog dang spu gri/ bstan srung yongs rdzogs lha chen sogs kyi dbang dang lung yongs rdzogs/ mkha' 'gro snying thig dang mkha' 'gro yang tig dbang lung / kun mkhyen
klong chen pa'i mdzod bdun dang ngal gso skor gsum rjes 'brel dang bcas pa'i lung / zhang khrom tshe bdag lcags 'dra dang lcags sdig gi dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ ra
shag ma mo sgang shar gzhung pod lung / sangs gling bla ma dgongs 'dus pod bcu gsum/ thugs rje chen po phyi rgyal po lugs/ nang nor bu lugs/ gsang ba mi tra'i bla med lugs
bcas pod gsum/ phur pa thugs kyi nying khu/ 'jam dpal dkar dmar nag gsum/ khyung gsang ba yang khol sogs kyi dbang lung yongs rdzogs/ kar gling zhi khro'i dbang dang gzhung
pod lung / zhig gling gter chos rnams dang 'ja' tshon snying po'i gter chos pod drug tu grags pa rnams kyi dbang yongs rdzogs/ stag sham yi dam dgongs 'dus gtsor gyur
gter chos phal mo che'i dbang / chos gling gter chos/ yongs dge mi 'gyur rdo rje'i gter chos che chung lnga/ rol rdor

mtsho brag gnyis kyi skor tshang ma'i dbang lung gis mtshon gter ma'i phyogs che phra shin tu mang ba rnams dang / rang rtsom bstan bcos shes bya kun khyab rtsa 'grel bshad
lung gi tshul du gsan par bzhed pa sogs rang rtsom rigs phal mo che'ang bkas gnang ma thag pa nas dgyes pa skong ba'i slad du gus pa chen pos 'bul bar bgyis pa'o/ /de dag
rnams kyang gsan tho bzhugs rigs las rags bsdus tsam bkod pa ste gsan tho gang bzhugs rnams bkod na yig tshogs ha cang che ba dang phal cher tho yig kyang ma bzhugs pas
zhib par ma 'tshal lo/ /de ltar rgya mtsho chen po la chu klung bye ba 'bum phrag snyed sdud kyang bri ba dang gang ba nam yang med pa bzhin chos kyi rgya mtsho chen po
'dis ni dam pa'i chos kyi chu klung nam yang ngoms pa med par gsol ba'i rnam thar 'di gcig pu'ang da lta'i gang zag sus kyang cha tsam bskrun nus pa ma mchis so/ /lnga pa
de ltar gsan pa'i don thugs nyams su bzhes te mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan gyis 'phags pa'i tshul ni/ deng sang snyigs ma'i mthar mchog dman thams cad gal chung chos la
byed pa'i dus ngan shar bas da ltar sangs rgyas pa'i chos khur po gcig las kyang khe grags zang zing dngos po phra mo tsam snying gi dkyil du 'chang ba dang / ri bong cal
sgrog gi rjes su rgyug pa dang blo chung dran mang 'ga' zhig gis zhus zhus thob thob mang po byas kyang dpe cha ldeb gcig mi bzhengs/ don sne gcig nyams su mi len/ phal
mo ches ni rang nyid dka' las gang yang mi dgos/ chos la zhu rten mi dgos/ phyin chad khas len dam bca' mi dgos pa'i chu chen nas chu bcus pa lta bu zhig byed du yod na zhu
ba skad dang / de'ang chos zhus shing nyan pa'i drin brtsi

bla ma la byed pa'i skabs 'dir/ rje bla ma 'di ni dngul chu sa la pho yang rdul dang ma 'dres pa ltar ngan pa'i mig ltos kyis nam yang ma bslad par/ sku chung ngu nas bla ma
tshul bzhin bsten pa dang dam chos tshul bzhin du tshol ba'i rnam par thar pa lhan skyes su mnga' bas dbus gtsang nas lho mon tshun chad kyi gnas rten rnams mjal ba dang
/ rnam 'dren dam pa rnams las chos gsan du phebs pa na'ang nye gnas dam pa tshul khrims rgya mtsho dang dpon slob gnyis kho na bya btang kun tu rgyu'i ngang tshul gyis
phebs/ skabs rer zhabs phyags kyang med par zhabs rjen kho nas gshegs pas mtshon dka' ba du ma spyad de gnas rten rnams la phyag mchod tshogs skong smon lam mthil phyin pa
gnang / bla ma rnams la dngos po rgya mi che rung spus nam gtsang ba'i phyag rten ci 'byor pa re dang bcas chos dang gdams ngag thugs kha ma rdzogs par 'tsho chas 'byor
min dang yun ring thung la mi gzigs par gsan/ phyis su bzhed pa med kyang 'byor pa 'bad med lhun grub tu 'byung ba'i skabs su ni nyin re bzhin yang maNDal gyi rten dngos
gtsang ba re dang dbang chos grub pa'i skabs su zhabs brtan dang 'brel bar dngos po gang bzang gi 'bul ba sbom mtho ba re mdzad pa sogs mdor na ci mdzad thams cad mdo rgyud
nas bshad pa'i chos mthun gyi mdzad pa 'ba' zhig lhur bzhes pa ste/ rin chen bang mdzod las/ skyon bral yon tan rdzogs pa'i bla ma ni/ /snyigs ma'i dus na sangs rgyas
dngos dang mtshungs/ /rab dwangs sri zhus gus pas spyi bos bsten/ /ces pa ltar sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams tshul de bzhin du bsten par mdzad pa dang / sa'i snying po'i
mdo las/ gcig tu dad cing gus pas

chos nyan gyis/ /'di la 'phya zhing skur ba mi bya'o/ /chos smra ba la mchod par bya ba ni/ /sangs rgyas 'dra bar de la 'du shes skyed/ /ces gsungs pa ltar chos smra ba'i bshes
gnyen thams cad la de bzhin gus par mdzad pa dang / rgyan stug po bkod pa'i mdo las/ 'jam dpal gang na chos smra ba 'dug gam/ de mthong na mtshams med pa lnga byang
bar 'gyur ro/ /chos smra ba de la'ang mchod par bya ste/ gal te chos smra ba des mtshams med pa lnga spyod kyang de la sems 'khrugs par mi bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don thugs
la bzhag nas phal pa ltar snang ba rnams la'ang gus pa dang bcas pas gdams ngag sna re yin kyang gsan par mdzad cing / gang gsan pa'i rigs thams cad g.yas chung du mi
bzhag par phyag dpe 'dri ba dang / gsar rnying rgyud sde rnams kyi dkyil thang / gter ma la sogs pa'i tsaka li bzhengs pa dang / dbang chas/ mchod pa'i yo byad thams cad
la phyag rdzas gang yod phangs med du btang nas/ gzhan gyis dper 'os pa sha stag bzhengs pa sogs bla ma dam pa rnams mnyes shing bstan pa la phan pa'i mdzad pa kho na lhur
bzhes pas sa lam gyi yon tan zhar byung du rdzogs pa gzhir bzhag /lo legs na phub ma zhar la 'byung ba ltar gnas skabs kyi dpal dang 'byor pa thams cad kyang lo re bzhin
je rgyas su 'gyur ba ste/ ye shes rgya mtsho las/ gang gis bla ma'i bya ba la/ /mkhas pa'i skal ldan gang yin de/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad la/ /bskal pa bye ba
drug 'bum du/ /phyag byas pas ni 'di don che/ /bla mas bsgo ba bzhin bsgrubs na/ /'dod pa thams cad 'grub pa dang / /bsod nams dpag tu med pa 'thob/ /rang gi rdzas dang yo
byad

kyis/ /bla ma gnyes par sus byas na/ /'dis ni khams gsum 'khor ba las/ /sprul sku'i zhing du dbugs dbyung ste/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i sar gshegs so/ /zhes gsungs pa nyid mngon
du gyur pa'o/ /gang zhig gsan pa de dag thams cad kyang ming rkyang tsam ma yin par grub mtha' so so'i bshad pa'i rnam grangs/ lta sgom gyi 'jog mtshams/ bskyed rdzogs so
so'i zab gnad/ cho ga dang man ngag gi phyag len phra mo tshun chad rang rang gi lugs srol ma 'dres par gsal bar mkhyen cing de ltar phyag len du'ang bstar bar mdzad do/
/de dag kyang / ji skad du/ dam pas khas 'che mang po mi byed la/ gal te dka' bas khas ni blangs gyur na/ /rdo la ri mo bris pa ji bzhin du/ /shi yang gzhan du byed par
mi 'gyur ro/ /zhes dang / blun po chu yi ri mo 'dra/ /gang zhig byas pa de myur 'jig /mkhas pa rdo yi ri mo 'dra/ /shin tu phra ba'ang brtan par gnas/ /zhes pa ltar rig
pa'i gnas dang mdo rgyud la gsan bsam mdzad pa'i don go sku na gzhon pa'i skabs su 'chad spel gyis slob ma bskyangs/ phyis su rtsa ba'i gzhung dang 'grel ba phal mo che par
du bzhengs nas chos sbyin 'dzad pa med pa'i sgo 'phar phyes/ mdo rgyud kyi gzhung rnams kyang snod dang ldan cing skabs su babs pa na zhib mor bshad/ gtso bor gsang sngags
kyi bskyed rdzogs zab mo rnams la nyams bzhes chad pa med par mdzad de/ dgung lo nyer bzhi pa chu mo yos kyi lor mkhan rin po che 'jam dpal bzang po dang lhan cig mdo
khams su phebs nas rdzong sar bkra shis lha rtse'i gzims gshags su bzhugs stan 'jags nas lo bzhi tsam la/ ngor lugs kyi phyag bzhes ltar kye rdor gzhi bsnyen sngon

dngos rjes tshang zla ba brgyad kyi khongs su bsgrub/ bya rgyud rigs gsum spyi/ spyod rgyud rnam snang mngon byang / rnal 'byor rgyud rdo rje dbyings rnams la las rung gi ljags
bsnyen btang / cha mthun rgyud kun rig zla ba drug gi khongs su bsnyen pa rgyas pa/ gzhan yang rnam 'joms/ gdugs dkar gyis mtshon pa'i phran tshogs kyi ljags bzlas kyang
mang du mdzad/ dgung lo nyer dgu pa sa sprel lor mkhan rin po che dang lhan cig bod du phebs nas lo gsum tsam bzhugs/ lcags phag dgung lo so gsum par phyir phebs nas
gsar ma'i phyogs nas dus kyi 'khor lo gtsos pa'i rgyud sde che phra/ mkha' spyod ma sogs mkha' 'gro'i rigs/ gur zhal sogs chos srung / gzhan yang sgrub thabs mang po'i rnal
'byor gyi rim pa la bzhugs nas ljags bzlas du ma mdzad/ rnying ma'i phyogs su gter kha gsar rnying gi gu ru'i thugs sgrub zhi drag che phra/ thugs rje chen po'i rigs/
tshogs chen 'dus pa dang sgyu 'phrul zhi khro/ bka' brgyad lugs srol bcu dgu tsam dang phur pa lugs srol de tsam/ gsar rnying gi tshe sgrub rigs brgya rtsa re zung rnams
la bsnyen bzlas dang / tshogs skong bshags nar ma/ yar mar gyi tshes bcu dang dus chen rigs la tshogs dang mchod pa shin tu rgyas pa/ rgyun du mar me'i phreng ba gtsor byas
pa'i mchod pa'i phreng ba tshar du dngar ba rnam grangs du ma bshams nas bsags sbyong spel ba'i rim pa phal pa'i blos 'khyud par dka' ba kho na gnang / khyad par du'ang
de kho na nyid nges par bstan pa'i mdo las/ shA ri'i bu gang gis bskal pa gcig gi bar du nyan pa bas/ gang gis se gol gtogs pa'i yun tsam cig de kho na nyid kyi ting nge
'dzin la mnyam par bzhag na bsod

nams mang du 'phel lo/ /shA ri'i bu de lta bas na de kho na nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin 'di gzhan la nan gyis gdams par bya'o/ /zhes dang / mdo sde rgyan las/ de ltas rnal 'byor
can gyi sgom pa gang yin de ni don med min/ /de ltar bde bar gshegs kyi bstan pa gang yin de yang don med min/ /gal te thos pa tsam gyis don mthong 'gyur na sgom pa don
med 'gyur/ /gal te ma thos par yang sgom la 'jug na bstan pa don med 'gyur/ /ces gsungs pa'i don thugs la bcangs nas/ spyir dgung lo chung ngu'i dus nas skyes thob kyi stobs
kyis mtshan bcas rtsa rlung thig le'i rnal 'byor 'bad rtsol chung ngus 'grub pa dang / nyin mtshan gyi rtags bcu dang srid pa gsum gyi stong gzugs rkyen chung ngu la
brten nas shar ba dang / 'od gsal gyi snang ba sku dang thig le'i 'char sgo ci rigs pa 'byung ba dang / chos nyid kyi bden pa phyin ci ma log pa gzigs pas sems 'dzin dang
byung gnas 'gro gsum gyi rtsad gcod sogs rim gyis pa'i lam la brten ma dgos par rang bzhin lhun grub ngang bzhag chen po'i lta sgom gyi lhums su tshud kyang gdul bya rim
skyes dang blo rigs tha dad pa rnams drang ba'i slad dang / smin grol gyi rim pa zab mo gsan pa'i gsham du/ slob dpon gyis de nyid nyams su len dgos par gdams pa ni/ slob
bus gtso bos ji ltar bka' stsal pa sogs kyi khas len zhu ba'i srol mchis pa rnams kyang rjes su bsgrub cing gsan pa rnams chud zos su mi btang ba'i phyir/ gsung ngag rin
po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa/ mkha' spyod ma'i rdzogs rim gyi dmigs rkang sogs kyang tshar re ma chag pa dang / lo gsum bcad rgya'i khongs su jo nang rje btsun kun
dga' grol mchog

gis bsgrigs pa'i zab khrid brgya dang brgyad pa nyid rtsa bar bzung / sgom don zhib mo so so'i khungs su gyur pa'i khrid yig rnams dang sbyar te dam tshig rdo rje'i sgom bzlas
sogs kyis rgyud sbyang ba sngon du btang nas/ thog mar bla ma sa skya pa'i zhen pa bzhi bral nas bzung / bram pa kun dga' bzang po'i phyag rdzogs nor bu mthong grol gyi
bar rnams la/ mdo dang thun mong ba'i lam rim zhen pa bzhi bral/ bka' gdams lam rim/ blo sbyong don bdun ma/ dmar khrid rigs gsum sogs dang / rgyud sde so so'i rdzogs
rim dus 'khor sbyor drug /kye rdor lam 'bras/ bde mchog lU dril nag gsum sogs dang / rgyud ste thun mong gi rdzogs rim nA ro dang ni gu'i chos drug /dwags po lugs kyi phyag
chen rnams gtso bor mdzad cing zhag grangs mang ba dang / gzhan thams cad kyang chad lus gcig kyang med par nyams bzhes mthar phyin par mdzad/ rnying ma'i phyogs su sems
sde lugs gsum/ klong sde rna brgyud rdo rje zam pa/ bi ma dang mkha' 'gro snying thig /gter ma'i phyogs nas klong chen snying thig gtso bor gyur pa'i zab khrid rnams dang
/ sems nyid ngal gso sogs khro phu lugs kyi khrid/ zhag bdun ma rnams sogs bo dong lugs kyi khrid sogs mdor na khrid tshul gsan tshad shar sgom re tsam ma mdzad pa gang
yang med pas nyams dang rtogs pa'i yon tan nyin re bzhin yang gong 'phel du gyur/ mdor na snga rjes lo grangs bcu gsum tsam du bskyed rdzogs kho na la brtson par mdzad
pas snga phyir grub pa'i mtshan ma mngon du gyur pa'ang ci rigs par bstan yod par snang ba las mthong thos su gyur pa ni/ lcags zam chu bo ri'i tshe chu phug tu tshe rta
zung 'brel sgom bzlas

mdzad pa'i skabs tshe chu kar yol gang glo bur du babs/ yar klung tshe chu 'bum pa la phyag mchod mdzad pa na'ang de mtshungs dang / lha ldan jo bo rang byon lnga ldan la phyag
mchod mdzad skabs ring bsrel kha shas phyag tu phebs/ dpal spungs gling stod nas bdag cag 'dus pa rnams la nyang gter khros nag gi dbang gnang skabs dbang rten thod
pa reg tu mi btub pa tsam gyi drod 'bar/ byang rdza rgyud ma mo thang du rdzogs chen dpal sprul nas rdo 'bum la rab gnas zhus par tshes bco lnga zhig la mchod pa shoms shig
gsungs nas rdzong sar bzhugs gnas nas dgongs gtad mdzad pas nyin lam bdun brgyad kyi bar chod pa'i rdo 'bum der rab gnas kyi me tog char babs pa bzhin byung ba der gnas
phal mo ches dad rten du'ang thob/ phyis su tshe sgrub lo gsum tsam chags med mdzad skabs tshe chang rgyun bzhag de dbyar mi rul/ dgun mi 'kheng / kha dog ser smug shin
tu ska ba'i nyams can/ dbus nas gyen du phyur ba la dri ro gang gis kyang mtshon du med pa'i ya mtshan can du gyur/ dad skal ldan pa rnams kyis thog mar mjal skabs thang
stong rgyal po sogs sku'i rnam pa tha dad du mthong ba dang / gang zag bzang po zhig la 'phags ma'i snying thig gi dbang bskur gnang ba'i skabs spyan bdun po bkra hrig yod
pa mjal bas dad pa'i shugs kyis shes pa brgyal thabs su song ba sogs mang / dngos nyams mnal lam ci rigs par dag snang zhal gzigs rgyun chad med par 'byung yang dad ldan
blo thub la zur tsam re las gtan nas mi gsung / gzhan pas mthong snang byung tshul zhus pa la'ang rlung khams ldang ba'i mis mi rigs mi mthong ba ci yod/ de 'dra la blo
gtad ci'ang med tshul gyis nga

rgyal gcog pa kho na mdzad/ skabs rer zur tsam gsungs pa la sangs rgyas byang sems/ rig 'dzin mkha' 'gro'i tshogs las chos gsan pa dang / tshig don gyi sgro 'dogs bcad pa dang
/ rdo rje'i sngags rgyud mang po sgrogs pa dang / rdo rje'i glu snyan cing don zab pa len pa sogs chos kyi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin brnyes pa'i ngo mtshar 'byams klas
shing / snga phyir kla klo dang / dam sri gdug pa can tshar bcad pa'i mtshan ma'ang mang du gzigs/ dag snang gi rigs cung zad 'og tu 'chad par 'gyur la/ 'dir yang cung zad
smos na gtsang du phebs skabs dpal sa skya'i gdan sar sa chen phug tu 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi ril bu sgrub pa zhag bdun mdzad grub pa'i tho rangs khar/ mdun gyi gzhi
steng du 'od dmar ser gyi gong bu che ba zhig gi nang du utpal sngon po kha bye ma thag pa can yun cig gsal ba'i mthar thugs kar thim pa zhig byung / de phyin blo gros kyi
spobs pa je 'phel du song nas su la ci zhig 'chad kyang thogs pa med pa byung gsungs/ phyis me yos zla ba gsum pa'i tshes lnga la a lo zhe dgar khyim bdag cig rtsar bzhugs
pa'i mnal lam du bzhugs khri mthon po zhig gi khar mkhan rin po che byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin dang lhan cig tu bzhugs/ mkhan chen rin po ches 'thor nas mdzad de
'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bkra shis tshigs bcad brgya phrag mang po gsung ba zhig byung bas/ de'i thog ma'i tshigs bcad/ lha dbang lha yi longs spyod chen pos
brjid/ /mi dbang mi yi 'byor pa chen pos mtho/ /klu dbang klu yi nor bu chen pos phyug /'jig rten chen po gsum gyi bkra shis shog /ge sar mngon shes rdzu 'phrul 'gran zla
med/ /zhal lu dpa' rgod snying stobs

'gran zla med/ /khro thung 'phrul dang bkra lag 'gran zla med/ /'gran med mi pho gsum gyi bkra shis shog /rgya bzas rgya yi rten mchog thabs kyis drangs/ /bal bzas bal po'i
mchod sdong brdzongs su thob/ /'brug mos 'brug ltar grags pa'i gtam rgyud bzhag /ya mtshan bud med gsum gyi bkra shis shog /ces pa 'phral du 'dri bar mdzad nas de ka'i khyim
du blan/ de rjes phyogs de'i gar byon sar bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad ngo mtshar ba mang du mdzad/ kho bo'i sgrub khang sogs la'ang bkra shis rtags brgyad/ rdzas brgyad/
rgyal srid dang sbyar ba sogs mang du gnang ba rnams kyang rten 'brel gyi sgo khyad par can zhig yod par mngon/ yang phyogs de'i sbyin bdag ni sa mda' tshang la bzhugs
pa'i mnal lam du/ kla klo'i zhags pa byung zer ma thag tu dru gu 'dra ba zhig hril gyis byung nas sku lus dkris te nam mkhar khyer song bas cung zad thugs zhad pa'i rnam
pa byung ma thag /mgon po phyag bzhi pa byung nas gri gug gis bcad song bas sa thog tu rdo rje legs pa 'dug pas sku lus pang du btegs nas/ he he/ mgo mtho sa la btags/ rke
phra sa nas chad zer dpes/ byad thag mgon pos bcad pa bzang ste nga med na sa thog tuu 'o brgyal byas ang song zer ba dang mnal sad/ 'di skor du gar phebs kyi ri rnams
zang thal du gzigs shing gnas ri rnams la rtsa gsum lha tshogs ci gnas/ gter kha du yod thams cad sgrib med du gzigs pa zhig byung 'dug /'og gsang rnam du'ang khyugs tsam
smos pa ltar/ khyad par dpal 'byor sgang du bzhugs pa'i nub gcig stod 'bras mo ljongs/ bar padma bkod/ smad g.yu lung gangs ra yan

chad kyi gnas kyi bkod pa dang gter kha gang yod sogs me long gi gzugs brnyan bzhin sgrib med ma 'dres gsal bar gzigs/ de skabs mchog gyur gling pa bod du byon pas mon yul
dkar mo brag gi kha byang yang byang snying byang gnad byang bcas gcig tu bsdoms pa mar me'i 'od la bris te bod du bskur rtsis mdzad kyang rjes sor mtsho rgyal gyi lung bstan
de byung phyin de phyogs 'phros tsam yang mi gnang zhing yi ge de'ang bskur mdzad ma song bas de phyogs kyi rten 'brel thams cad bod spyi'i bsod nams kyis ma chun pa
la dgongs par snang / sngar phan rje nyid la gter kha bzhugs pa'i sgros tsam sus kyang mthong thos med pa la sde dge'i rgyal khab kyi nye skor rdo kho mar gter chen mchog
gling dang zhal rgyas bzhugs pa'i skabs/ 'phags ma'i snying thig thog mar spel ba sogs kyi nub cig mnal lam du/ nyid kyi ma yum de skra dar dmar gyis rgyab tu mdud/ gos
chen gos gyon/ par bu 'dzer bus bsdams pa zhig thogs nas byung ste/ nged kyi grogs mo gser gyi rna cha can bya ba des gsang 'os pa rnams dam med la bsgrags pa'i nyes pas
mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis bsgral nas sha khrag tshogs 'khor byas/ snying 'di red zer nas par bu kha phye nas snying rlon pa 'phar 'dar phri li li byed ba zhig 'dug pa de
la skrag sngangs lta bus sku lus 'dar phri li li byas nas mnal sad/ phyir nyin kyang de nam dran dus snying tsha shar 'gro ba zhig byung bas dus su ma babs par gsang ba bsgrags
pa 'di nyen che 'dug gsungs/ yang smin gling pa'i gter byon rdor sems kyi cho ga gtang ba'i skabs shig mnal lam du/ rdor sems sku dngos lta bu zhig la sku smad du
ring bsrel grangs med pa 'byar nas 'dug pa mjal bar/ gzhan

zhig la 'di ci red dris par/ khyed rang gis rdor sems sgo nas dbang dang byang chog byas pa rnams red zer gsungs/ 'dis ni de 'dra'i 'brel ldan rnams rdo rje sems dpa'i go 'phang
du rnam par grol bar thob par brda'i sgo nas lung du bstan par snang / sgrol ston 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal mtshan sogs las chos dbang gter byon thugs rje chen po
'khor ba dong sprugs kyi smin grol gsan grub pa'i rjes lam dus kyi nyams bzhes cung zad re mdzad skabs mnal lam du phyag mthil du de bzhin gshegs pa'i ring bsrel zhig snang
ba la/ 'khor ba dong sprugs kyi gzungs ring gsungs nas zhal phu btab pas ring bsrel grangs med pa skad cig la 'phel ba thugs shin tu dgyes pa zhig byung gsungs/ 'di ni
thugs rje chen po'i gdung 'dzin grangs med 'byung ba'i ltas su snang / sde dge ma yum chos dbyings bzang mo sogs la mkha' 'gro yang tig gi dbang lung khrid gsum gnang ba'i
skabs su yang tig gi dag snang khyad par can gzigs kyang zhib par ma nges/ bsam yas mchims phur phebs pa'i snang ba la kun mkhyen klong chen rab 'byams mjal nas snying
tig ya bzhi nye brgyud tshul du gsan par 'dug /mkha' spyod rdo rje rnal 'byor ma bla ma brgyud pa dang bcas pa byin gyis brlabs shing rjes su bzung ba dang / nyid las mkha'
spyod ma'i chos 'brel thob pa rnams kyang rim par byin rlabs thob pa'i ltas kyang gzigs/ rnal 'byor ma grub pa'i rtags su spyir bshad pa'i lus la bde ba/ ngag la nus
pa/ sems la rtogs pa ste 'bar ba rnam pa gsum/ nyin mo mi/ mtshan mo lha 'dre/ nang nub zas nor te 'du ba rnam pa gsum rnams ni thams cad kyi mthun snang du grub pa der
gda'/ skabs shig sku lus kyi nang du

rtsa gsum 'khor lo bzhi'i gnas lugs rnams gdos bcas kyis ma bsgribs par gsal bar gzigs shing / lan gcig 'khor lo 'og ma rnams skam/ mgrin pa 'ol tsam dang spyi bo rang mal
du yod pa'ang gzigs par gsungs pa 'di ni lam gyi mngon rtogs ches mthon por phebs pa'i don du snang ngo / /'dzam nang padma shel phug tu gter gsar thugs sgrub yid bzhin nor
bu'i tshogs skong mdzad skabs khrom mang du 'dus pa la khrom dbang zhig phug pa der mdzad par bzhed pa la dam can dngos su 'ongs nas/ 'dir mi nyi shu las mang ba gtan
nas btsud mi nyan zhus pas khrom dbang rgyab tu mdzad/ gter lhung padma shel rir mchog gling dang phran bcas yod skabs phyi dro zhig la sku ngal ba'i tshul gyis cung zad
bsnyal nas bzhugs song ba'i rjes/ da lta 'og gi pha waM 'gram 'dir rdo rje legs pa byung nas g.yas kyi rdo rje yar gyi brag la bstan/ mig zur gyis mar gyi sgrub phug 'di
la bltas song bas 'di gnyis la gter kha re re yod par 'dug gsungs pa de la brten nas phyir nyin yar mar nas mchog gling dang rje nyid bcas kyis gter kha re re thon song /
lar dus rgyun dam can/ g.yu sgron ma/ sha za kha mo che rnams ni grib ma ltar 'grogs shing legs nyes kyi lung bstan pa dang ci bcol ba'i phrin las sgrub pa yin 'dug /lcags
sprel lor kho bos yang khrod sgrub sder rdor sems sku brnyan bzhengs pa'i nang gzhug la ched du gsol ba btab pa ltar/ zla gam dbang phug tu bzhugs skabs rdo rje g.yu sgron
ma la phrin las bcol bas/ rin po che asma garbha las grub pa'i rdor sems sku brnyan rgyal po dzaH'i thugs dam rten khyad par 'phags pa phul 'dug pa bka' drin du stsal
bas da lta sku brnyan gyi thugs

kar ye shes sems dpa'i tshul du bzhugs pa lags/ rab byung bco lnga pa thog mar tshes pa me yos zla ba bcu gcig pa'i dga' ba dang por yang khrod sgrub khang 'dir rab gnas bka'
drin stsal ba'i nub dag snang mu med pa shar/ skabs shig ri bo lta bu'i mchod rten chen po'i zhig gi phyogs bzhir sgo bzhi/ nang du mdzod lnga yod pa'i mdzod re re bzhin
chos gter gyis gtams pa la paN grub dang mkha' 'gro mang pos brda sprad/ rje nyid nas kyang gzigs pa btsal bas de dag la don gang yod thugs la nges shing de'i srung ma
chos srung khyad par ba bzhi yod pa dang / rgyal chen be har nas kyang thugs yus pa'i tshul gyis/ nged la slob dpon padmas bod yul gyi gtsug lag khang ci yod gnyer gtad
pa yin kyang khyed rang rnams kyis gsol mchod tsam mi byed pa'i thog 'drer ba lta zhig 'dug pas gnod pa skyel na ri rab tsam yang thal bar byed nus kyang khyed rang rnams
slob dpon padma'i rjes 'jug red pas nged kyis de'i dam tshig la brtsis pa yin/ da zhag glo bur mi bde ba kha shas byung ba de rnams nged kyis rtags tsam bstan pa yin zer
ba byung / mchod rten de'i don khyod la mdzod lngar grags pa zhig tshang dgos par 'dug pas shes bya kun khyab de'i phyogs gtogs bcas thun mongs shes bya'i mdzod/ gsar rnying
gi rgyud sde'i skor rnams thun min sngags kyi mdzod/ gter chos gsar rnying gi chog bsgrigs rnams rin chen gter gyi mdzod/ sgrub brgyud shing rta brgyad kyi smin grol
rnams zab mo gdams ngag gi mdzod/ sa gter dgongs gter gang byung gsang ba thun mong min pa'i mdzod kyi brdar bzhag nas de snga 'go bzhag grub pa rnams rim par mtha' 'dus
grub pa dang / de snga med rigs

de lta bu'i 'grigs shing byung na dgos pa gnad don che bar 'dug cing / be har la'ang gsol kha re tsam gtan nas chag mi nyan par 'dug ces bka' phebs pas mgon khang du sku lnga'i
gsol kha ldeb gcig tsam bton pa dang / de nas da lta'i bar du mdzod bzhi po rnams bla ma'i bka' lung sor bzhag gis dbang lung gi rgyun btsal 'os pa rnams gsar du btsal/
gsar bsgrigs dgos rigs dge sbyong yang gcog nas de la 'bad 'bungs bton/ dpe gsar bzhengs dang spar du 'khod pa'i rtsa ba byas/ dbang lung khrid bcas rgyun yang yang spel
ba'i rgyu mtshan kyang de la brten pa lags/ tshes bcu gnyis pa'i snga dror 'tshubs slong chen pos thugs khams ma bde bas mun pa'i nang du bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar byang
shar phyogs ngos/ srid pa'i rgyal mo e ka dzA Ti sku mdog phyag mtshan sogs sngags srung ma spyi dang 'dra ba la/ tshem khrab lta bu kha dog ljang gu g.yu 'od 'bar ba zhig
mnabs pa/ 'jigs zil dang bcas pa ja sbyor tsam mngon sum gzigs/ mun mthongs bsal nas kyang de ltar 'char ba de yis/ e chos dbyings gdod nas sogs kyi gsol mchod stsal
ba de nyid yi ger btab nas tshar gcig gsungs pas 'ja' yal ba ltar song gsungs/ de'i tshes nyer gnyis nub mor 'od gsal gyi ngang la rje nyid lha sa'i bar skor du byon pa na
bud med mi las 'das pa'i gzi brjid mdzes sdug chas rgyan phun sum tshogs pa zhig gis rgya man lta bu'i me tog dmar po'i sdong po chen pos bum pa bkang ba thogs nas byung
ba dang 'phrad/ phan tshun ma bu lta bu'i dgyes pa chen po'i ngang gsung gleng 'ga' zhig mdzad pa'i mthar 'grogs nas jo bo rin po che'i mdun du phyin te lhan cig bod khams

bde ba'i smon lam mang po mdzad/ bud med de la khyed su yin dris pas khyed rang rnams kyis dus rgyun 'bod pa'i ye shes mtsho rgyal bya ba de yin gsungs/ 'o na bod khams bde
ba'i thabs ci drag zhus pas/ lung bstan mang du gsungs/ bod 'dir nang 'khrugs zhig ma byung na re zhig skyon med/ 'on kyang lo gsum gyi nang tshun nang 'khrugs zhig 'byung
bas de la brten nas kla klos nyen che/ lar khyed rang rnams nas bya dgos nges de ci'ang mi byed/ khyed kyis ma mtha' na'ang lo brgyad kyi skabs la kho mos yang phur sgrub
thabs byin pa de tsam yang rang bzhin gal chung bskyur ba de'ang ma legs sogs gsungs nas bar snang thams cad Da ma ru'i sgra shar shar gyis gang ba bcas mkha' la gshegs/
de'i phyir nyin dgung lo brgyad par mkha' 'gro mtsho rgyal gyis stsul ba'i yang phur sbrags ma'i sgrub thabs phab pa'i yi ge pa kho bos zhus/ nyi zlog dang 'grigs pas
gtor zlog kyang gnang bar mdzad do/ /zla ba bcu gcig pa phyi ma'i tshes lnga nub rmang lam du/ dpal spungs byang 'dren rab grub nas phur pa'i bris thang ri mo sogs gsar
nyams can ha cang khyad mtshar mi che ba zhig khur nas 'di shin tu rtsa chen yin pas rab gnas zhig zhu zer/ 'di de tsam gyi rnying nyams bca' kha sogs mi 'dug pas na ma ci
che gsungs pas/ 'di ni spang mi rabs bcu gsum gyi thugs dam rten so so la gsung byon pa'i rtsa chen yin zer ma thag /kho bo der 'dug pas gru tshugs shig byas song bar rdzogs
chen mkhan po pad rdor lta bur gnas 'gyur bas skad che snyan 'brug sgra lta bus/ oM badzra kI li kI la sogs dzab dbyangs sa g.yo ba lta bu byas pa dang lhan cig phur
sku de rdo rje gzhon nu dngos su

bzhengs nas byon te/ rje nyid dang kho bo grogs dan de bcas gsum la phyag tha ma'i phur pa mgo la bzhag ste byin rlabs mdzad ma thag mnal sad/ snang ba thams cad rdo rje gzhon
nu'i sku dang sngags sgras mer mer sh-ig shig byed pa mngon sum du yun ring byung gsungs/ yang / de skabs shig gi mtshan mor gsal snang du/ rje nyid khyams yangs pa zhig
na khri mthon por bzhugs 'dug pa la/ dril bu lta bu'i sgra rgyun ring byung ba'i rjes su bud med gzugs bong che la mtshar sdug gzi brjid dang ldan pa mo btsun bzang mo'i
chas can zhig byung nas gos chen gos gnyis/ 'go snam gos gnyis/ ther phrug sogs dang / bzang gos gcod ldan sngon po kha bzhi bcu rtsa gsum yod pa'i yug gcig phul nas
phyag dbang zhus/ gus pa chen pos/ dus rgyun nyid kyi gsung thos pa tsam gyis kyang dga' bde mi bzod pa skye/ sku mdun 'ong snyam yang 'gol po zhig ma byung / da res li thang
du phyin pa'i yar lam sku mdun ched du bcar ba yin zer ba la/ khyed su yin gsungs pas/ sman btsun rdo rje dbyar mo bsil yin zer/ 'o na khyed li thang du ci'i don du
phyin dris pas der grogs mo zhig yod pas gtugs sar phyin zer/ da gang du 'gro dris pas zil khrom du 'gro zer/ zil khrom la rten gnas gang yin dris pas phyag mdzod nor bu
bzang po rtsar yin zer/ skabs der grogs mo bde chen chos sgron 'dra ba zhig gis ba men rwa co zhos bkang ba zhig phul nas/ 'di la dus phyis mi bde ba zhig byung ba de la
phan pa'i byin rlabs mdzad dgos zer/ mi bde ba ci byung dris pas sman btsun des rgyab ston pa na sgal tshigs re re bzhin 'dzer nag 'dra bas gang bar 'dug /zho de bzhes pas

bde ba tshad med pa zhig skyes pa dang mnyam du sman btsun des sku la khril gyis 'khril byung bas/ dge slong la bud med kyis 'khyud pa gzhan gyis mthong na shin tu ngo tsha
snyam nas gnong bag 'char ba'i skabs der gsang gnas 'phrad pas gsang rtsa padma'i snal ma lta bu lte ba la thug par brkyangs byung bas bde ba'i ngang tu rtog pa gzhan nub
nas sku lus ri bo chen po lta bur song ba la rtsi shing nags tshal thams cad dpa' bo dpa' mo'i rang bzhin can gyis rdo rje'i rgyud dang sngags kyi sgra mu med pa zhig sgrog
pa shar ba'i ngang du gsal snang de 'gags so/ /rgyal zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi dga' ba gsum par kho bo nas brtan bzhugs phul ba'i sta gon gyi nub mor mnal lam du sde
dge sa dbang dpal ldan 'chi med rtag pa'i rdo rje nyid rje nyid kyi 'khris su byis pa chung ngu'i ngang tshul gyis brtse gdung dang bcas te bzhugs 'dug pa/ re zhig nas bzhengs
te brkyang phyag gsum 'tshal ba dang sbrags/ rje nyid la sku chung ngu zhig dang / shog dril zhig sprad nas sku 'di khong gis khro khog stod kyi brag sked cig nas rnyed
pa khyed la phul ba yin/ yi ge 'di zhabs brtan rtsom phud yin ces gsungs pa phyag tu blangs nas mjal bas/ sku ni smad snying zho sha la/ stod klu 'jim gyi rnam pa rdo
rje 'chang sked yan chod shin tu gsal ba zhig 'dug /yi ge kha phye bas/ rdo rje 'chang chen rdo rje'i rig pa 'dzin/ /'jam dpal gzhon nu 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gter/
/pad sdong las 'khrungs padma'i rgyal tshab che/ /bskal brgyar 'tsho gzhes skal bzang grub gyur cig /ces snang / de 'phros rje nyid nas khyed kyi sku 'di gter ma yin rgyu
red pas 'di mnyam shog ser i 'dug gsungs pas/ shog ser chung ngu zhig 'dug ste

nged nas klog mi shes gsungs/ nged la ston dang klog i shes lta gsungs pas bstan byung bar/ shog ser chung ngu sbrang bu'i 'dab ma lta bu shel ltar dwangs pa brda yig cha shas

nas gsang ba bshad bya ba/ /bha ga chos kyi 'byung gnas che/ /gru gsum nyams dga'i gnas mchog tu/ /gsang ba'i bdag por rab bzhugs te/ /zhes sogs dang / sngags/ oM badzra
satwa tsaNDa ma hA ro Sha Na radznyA pa ya ti rangga pa ya sogs yod pa/ mtshan la dpyad na gsar ma dang / rgyud sde 'og ma'i sngags rgyud lta bu/ mchod brjod la brtags
na rnying ma/ brjod bya bla med kyi rgyud yin pa zhig tu snang gsungs pas phyir nyin rang nas brtsams pa'i zhabs brtan gyi dbur dag snang shlo ka de'ang bsabs pas rten 'byung
shin tu dge bar gyur/ me glang zla ba dang po'i tshes nyi shu nyin rje nyid dang rdor brag mkhan po sogs la byang gter dgongs pa zang thal gyi dbang bgyis pa'i mtshan
mor rje bla ma'i gsal snang du/ zang zang lha brag yin snyam byang kha ri chen po kha shas phyogs phyogs su yod pa/ de nang rig cig la brag mi che ba gdong gyen rgyug yod
pa zhig gi mdun rab byung chas sba dbyug bcas pheb pa/ rig 'dzin rgod ldem yin zer ba'i sngags pa zil can/ spyan gru gsum rnam pa/ dbu skra thor cog che tsam yod pa/ phyag
tu thod phreng bsnams pa zhig de nas byon byung ba de'i zhal nas/ dgongs pa zang thal dbang de de 'dra byed bskur rgyu min/ khrid sbrel dgos gsungs/ khams phyogs su
dbang lung rgyun ma chad tsam las khrid

rgyun mi 'dug zhus/ nga yis dgongs pa gtad pa yin/ khrid rgyun byed chog /tshig rgyun zhig kyang lo gsum nang thob 'ong gsungs/ zang thal 'di dbang khrid sbrel dus sngar lo
gsum dgos pa sogs zhib cha chen po dgos pa'i phyag srol 'dug tshul zhus pa/ de mi skyon/ bstan pa spyi'i babs dang mthun par gter chos rnams la'ang 'bras bu'i dus/ sgrub
pa'i dus/ lung gi dus/ rtags tsam 'dzin pa'i dus rnams su yod pa la 'di'ang mnga' ris paN chen sku mched yan chad chos 'dir zhugs nas tshul bzhin bsgrubs tshad 'bras bu
ma thob pa gcig kyang ma byung / de nas sgrub pa'i dus yin/ tshad ldan byed mkhan kha shas 'bras bu thob pa'ang byung / deng sang lung gi dus yin pas spyi 'gre ltar byed
chog /lar khyed rang la byang gter 'di'i bag chags chen po yod pa gsungs/ nged nas byang gter 'di la gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i dad pa yod/ da zhag bag chags 'dra ba thar thor
yang 'dug zhus pas/ 'o de ka yin gsungs/ da lta yang tig gces sgron khrid cig 'chad skabs yin kyang sngar lha ri gzim phug nas khrid lung mdor bsdus zhig las ma thob pas
ci red 'gro na zhus pas/ de'ang nga yis dgongs pa gtod pa yin pas khrid dngos red 'gro gsung 'phror sad/ gter chen mchog gyur gling pas thog mar mjal ba'i skabs bar chad
sel ba'i rten 'brel du chos dbang phur pa spu gri'i dbang gnang ba'i rjes nas phyis kyi bar du gter bzhes pa la bar chad med par ci 'dod chog pa mngon sum gyis grub pa
byung song / de rjes zhig tu byin rlabs 'bebs pa'i slad du dpal chen yang dag gi dbang gnang ba'i skabs/ gter chen

nyid kyis rje bla ma dpal he ru ka'i skur dngos su gzigs pa'i mos gus kyi rkyen gyis thugs ka nas 'od zer mthing nag gi gong bu hU~M yig gis mtshan pa byung ste spyi bo nas
zhugs sku lus la thim pas byin phebs pa'i nyams bzod med du skyes/ des rtsa mdud grol bas de phyin chad shog ser 'bebs pa la thogs pa med pa dang tshig don thams cad rim
bzhin je legs je zab tu gyur pa byung 'dug /bar skabs zhig 'di skor phebs nas khro khog sogs su dgon pa 'debs par rtsom pa'i dbyar thog bsnyun khams mang po zhig bzhes pa
la skyabs 'jug zhus pa'i skabs sku rim du sgrub pa zhig mdzad pa'i nub gcig mnal lam du/ thang yangs pa zhig tu chos rgyal bla ri yin zer ba'i ri chen po zhig la me 'bar
ba'i 'od kyis phyogs thams cad khyab pa'i mus su rlung 'tshubs chen po zhig langs pas ri bo me dang bcas pa gar song med par gtor song ba zhig byung gsungs pa ni phyis
'byung gi lung bstan du snang / phyis zhig gi mnal lam du gu ru'i sku tshab shin tu legs pa zhig phyag tu 'dug pa zhig nas thal ba ltar gyur pa la da ni de 'dra thon thabs
med dgongs pa'i thugs 'gyod chen po skyes pa zhig byung gsungs pa'i rjes yun ring ma 'gor bar gter chen de nyid gshegs song / yang lan cig 'od gsal snang bar dpal chu bo
ri'i yar rgyab thang dkyil du gur dkar po phub pa zhig snang ba la/ der su 'dug blta dgos dgongs nas phebs pas/ der mnga' ris rig 'dzin legs ldan rdo rje nyid sngags pa'i
cha lugs can du bzhugs 'dug pa la gus 'dud mdzad nas 'dir phebs don ci yin zhus par/ sngon gu ru chos dbang gis la yag gu ru lha khang gi sgo gong du sbas pa phal cher
mnga' ri paN chen gyis bton/ 'dir

khyod la lung byed du 'ong ba yin gsungs/ drang srong dri med zhi ba kun tu dge ba'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa'i dbang lung yud tsam la gnang nas dpe phyag tu gnang
ba zhig byung / de rjes 'chi med sprul sku nas logti zhi ba'i sgrub thabs zhig mdzad par zhus/ rten 'brel du dgongs te drang srong dri med kun tu dge ba'i sgrub thabs
dbang bskur las tshogs dang bcas pa de gnang / 'di skabs gter gyi 'phros tsam yang mi gsung zhing rje nyid la gter kha bzhugs pa sus kyang ma tshor ba'i skabs yin pas mdzad
byang sogs su rtsom chos lta bur gnang ba las don du 'di'ang yang gter gyi gral yin par snang ngo / /yang rje nyid la snga sor gsol ngan zhig zhu bar byung ba rlung gi

tshe/ baNDi ta la mkha' 'gro mas lung bstan nas de ring nyid nas sdig spyod kyi rgyal po de ma bsgral na nges par sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la 'tshe ba chen po 'byung
