zhing khams dang yul gyi bkod pa gzigs pa'i tshul shin tu mang bar 'dug kyang nges pa can paNDi ta mi pham rgya mtsho la bka' stsal ba ni/ skabs shig khong de zhag skor
zla ba drug gis bgrod dgos pa'i mya ngam gyi thang brgal nas

ri'i phug tu yun ring song nas/ sham bha la chung ba'i gnas sgo lho phyogs gsang ba brag gi ra ba zhes grong khri phrag tsam yod pa/ yul de'i mi rnams bcud len gyi mthus yun
ring 'tsho ba/ padma gling pa'i gter chos dar ba der/ sngon slob dpon padma'i slob brgyud yin pa'i rnal 'byor pa yul skad tong ku bla ma zer ba zhig las rdo rje sems dpa'
rgyan 'khor lnga pa zhes pa'i dbang lung zhus/ bla ma des sham bha la chung ba nas blangs pa tsandan las grub pa'i rdo rje sems dpa'i sku stong phrag mang po bzhugs pa'i
lha khang yang mjal/ des sham bha la chung bar 'gro lam brag phug nas chu 'bab pa sogs bstan/ gnas 'di brag gi ra ba grong khri phrag tsam yod/ 'di nas byang du lam bgrod
dka' bar phyin na sham bha la chung ba g.ya' yi ra ba zhes grong 'bum phrag yod/ bon pos 'ol mo lung zer ba'ang de yin kyang bon po la lo rgyus dag po med/ de na nus
pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa du ma bzhugs yod/ de las kyang phar byang phyogs su phyin na sham bha la che ba gangs kyi ra ba can grong bye ba du ma yod pa dngos yod ces zer
ba lta bu'i nyams byung zhing / der byon lam dang yul de'i bkod pa/ bla ma de'i rnam 'gyur sogs nyin snang lta bur gsal gsal 'di dang 'di 'dra 'dug ces thugs nyams mtshar
snang dang bcas te bka' stsal to zhes thos/ yang skabs shig mnal ltas su/ rje nyid bsam yas kyi pho brang zhig tu rgyal po'i tshul gyis bzhugs nas 'dug /g.yas phyogs yangs
pa zhig tu slob dpon padma pheb lam skas btsugs dgos pa red zer nas sgrom skas bar snang la zug pa zhig mi re zung gis dka' las chen po byed nas btsugs/ de skor mi tshogs
shin tu mang pos 'ur

sgra sgrog cing 'tshubs kyi li li byed kyang shing thung bas yar mi sleb pa dang / lji bas mi theg pa sogs kyis skas dngos la mi phan 'dug /der mi brjid can zhig 'dug pa des
'di rnams kyis slob dpon padma'i phebs skas btsugs pa yin zer 'ur sgra chen po byed pa rer kyang / mchog gyur gling pa dang / kong sprul dang / khyed rang gsum tsam ma
gtogs skas chen 'di tshugs thub pa ni su'ang mi 'dug zer ba zhig byung bas 'di la'ang go rgyu chen po zhig 'dug gsungs/ lar mnal ltas 'di 'dra'ang dgos pa'i dbang gis skabs
rer zur tsam gsung ba ma gtogs rgyun du ni gtan nas bka' gnang ba'i srol mi 'dug go /yang lan cig 'od gsal dag pa'i snang char 'phags yul lta bu'i sa gzhi shin tu rgya
che zhing khod snyoms pa/ spang ljongs ne'u gseng chu mtsho rnams la me tog dkar dmar sna tshogs kyis spras shing shin tu nyams dga' la yid du 'ong ba zhig tu phebs 'dug
par/ rje nyid kyis gser gyi rus sbal zhig la chibs/ zhwa lu mchog sprul blo gsal bstan skyong gis seng ge dkar mo chibs/ rdzogs chen pa gzhan phan mtha' yas kyis glang chen
thal dkar chibs/ gter chen mchog gyur gling pas rgya stag ngar ma chibs/ kho bo padma gar dbang gis g.yu 'brug sngon mo la zhon/ thams cad kyang he ru ka'i cha byad sha
stag byas/ dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dar dang rin chen rus pa'i rgyan ldan shin tu mang po Da dril sogs phyag mtshan sna tshogs thogs pa rnams dang lhan cig rdo rje'i glu len
cing gar bsgyur bas shin tu dgyes pa'i snang ba yun ring mo byung gsungs nas thugs ngo mtshar ba'i tshul mdzad/ 'di dag gi zhon pa las so so'i sprul

gzhi yon tan phrin las sogs dang 'brel ba'i gnad don go rgyu chen po re yod pa yin 'dug pas/ kho bos tshul de lta bu'i bkod pa bris thang zhig bzhengs nas spyan sngar phul
bas thugs dgyes pas rab gnas gnang zhing sku'i nye logs su yun ring bkram par mdzad song / nged la mngon shes med ces dus rgyun du gsungs mod/ deng sang gi lung bstan mkhan
po mi dgos dus thams cad kyi skye ba snga phyi bar gsum dang legs nyes shes pa lta bu'i yi ges srang mdo thams cad khyab cing thig mi thig sna tshogs dang / dgos dus ci'ang
mi mkhyen pa ma yin par/ dus 'gyur chen mo'i skabs sogs gal gnad che dus ci gsungs thams cad thog tu khel bas bla chen dang / mi chen dang / mkhas grub thams cad kyis
yid rton pa'i gnas gcig pur mdzad/ des mtshon mkhas btsun grub pa'i yon tan la shes ldan gzur gnas kun gyis bsngags pa'i gling bu bsgyur/ slob ma dad ldan rnams 'gro khar
da phyin chad 'phrad par dka' gsungs pa dang / da dung rjes nas 'phrad 'ongs gsungs pa rnams kyang de bzhin kho nar gyur/ lan cig dgon stod la me'i dogs pa gyis gsungs
pa dang / lan cig dgon smad du me shor bar 'dug pas ltos shig gsungs pa rnams kyang de skabs kho nar me 'bar bar snang ba rnams so so'i khyim du gnas pas kyang ma mthong
bar lkog gyur gzigs pa sogs 'di 'dra'i rigs kyang mang du 'dug /mdor na spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan dang mngon par rtogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bdag nyid can
yin pas gnas tshul ji bzhin pa brjod nus pa lta ci smos/ phyogs re tsam yang shes pa dang brjod pa'i rngo thogs pa ma yin kyang so skye tha

mal pas ji tsam mthong ba de tsam zhig brjod byar byas pa'o/ /drug pa de la brten nas bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don ji ltar mdzad pa ni/ dgung lo nyer gcig par ngor gyi gdan
sar bzhugs pa'i skabs mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bkas bskul te/ brda sprod gtso bor gyur pa'i rig gnas kyi bslab gra btsugs pas/ thar rtse zhabs drung byams pa kun
dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub sogs ches mkhas pa'i slob ma'ang thon/ gtsang paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa bstan pa'i nyi mas
kyang / gsung bris kyis bsngags shing / dngos su zhal mjal skabs kha btags nang mdzod mgul du gsol/ gser zho lnga phyag tu gtad/ dbu la phyag gis byugs pa dang bcas thar
rtse ma hA paNDi ta zhes gsung gis gzengs bstod pas mtshon/ phyogs der sde dge paNDi ta dang / thar rtse paNDi ta sogs su mkhas pa rnams kyis snyan pa'i dril bsgrags/ blo
gros rgya mtshos zhus pa'i mdo las/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dang chos 'dzin dang / /chos sgrub pa dang srog chags snying rje ba/ /chos bzhi 'di dag yon tan tshad med
de/ /de dag mtha' ni rgyal bas mi gsung ngo / /zhes pa'i chos bzhi po rtag tu thugs dam du bzhes pa las khyad par du gyur pa/ dpal sa skya pa'i gser pod du grags pa lhag
pa'i lha'i sgrub thabs mang po phyogs bsdus kyi rjes gnang / so so'i rgya gzhung gi lung dang bcas par ma chad pa bzhugs pa rnams gzhir bkod/ de dag gi gsal byed yig cha
shin tu gal che ba rnams kyis kha bskangs/ ma tshang ba dang mi gsal ba rnams la gsal byed kyi yig cha gsar du spel/ kar dge sogs lugs srol khungs thub gzhan las

byung ba de mtshungs rnams kyang phyogs su bsdebs te bstan pa'i rgyun gnas pa kho na la dgongs pa gtad nas sgrub thabs kun btus zhes pa'i mtshan gsol ba pusta ka bcu gsar du
bsgrigs nas spar du bkod/ de dag gi dbang lung khrid gsum gyi rgyun gtsang du lan gcig /mdo khams dpal spungs kyi gdan sar zla bzang sprul pa'i sku dang / bdag cag dad
'dus nyi shu skor la lan gcig /rdzong sar dgon du rgyal dbang karma pa bco lnga pa dang / thar rtse mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje sogs la lan gcig /thar rtse zhabs
drung 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dang / khang sar/ phan khang zhabs drung sogs la kha skong gi skor tshar gcig stsal/ byams pas seng ge'i sgra bsgrags pa'i
mdo las/ ganggA'i bye snyed 'jig rten gser dag gis/ /bkang ste gang la sbyin pa byin pa bas/ /dus ngan tshe na tshigs bcad gcig 'chad pa/ /de yi bsod nams ci 'dra snga mar
med/ /ces shin tu snyigs ma'i dus 'dir chos 'chad par 'os pa'i snod tshul dang ldan pa shin tu dkon kyang / bstan pa'i btsas dang gzhan phan lhag pa'i bsam pas drangs te
chos shlo ka gcig 'chad pa la'ang phan yon dpag tu med par gsungs pa ltar/ bstan pa 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen chen po rnams nas bzung / mchog dang bar pa dang dman pa'i 'gro
ba rnams la nam yang sku ngal ba dang thugs skyo dub med par chos kyi sbyin pa bar ma chad du stsal ba ste/ rje nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma gcig pu thar rtse rdo rje 'chang
sku mched nas kyang ngor chen bka' 'bum dang / zhu chen bka' 'bum gyi lung / dri med rnam gnyis kyi dbang bka' sogs gsan bzhes mdzad pas mtshon/ dpal sa skya pa khri

chen bkra shis rin chen/ rje btsun ma rta mgrin dbang mo/ bstan 'dzin dbang mo/ skal bzang chos sgron sogs dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zhal ngo / ngor e waM pa'i mkhan po zhabs
drung phal cher/ zhwa lu mchog sprul/ nA lendra'i gzims 'og rin po che/ yar klung dbon rin po che/ sa skya dga' ldan dpon slob/ ngor dpon slob ngag dbang legs grub/ 'dar
grong chen slob dpon kun dga' 'jam dpal/ sa skyong sde dge'i dbu bla dpal ldan phrin las dang dge 'dun rgya mtsho khu dbon/ shar bla ma mkhas dbang kun dga' dpal ldan sogs
sa ngor tshar gsum gyi phyogs dang / dpal karma pa chen po gong 'og /si tu mchog sprul gong 'og /stag lung ma rin po che/ ri bo che'i rje drung dang zhabs drung no mi han
'phags mchog bcas/ zla bzang rin po che/ dbon sprul sku mched/ mkhas dbang bla ma karma nges don/ bdag cag yan bka' brgyud phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin phal mo che/ sbyor ra
thams cad mkhyen pa/ bsam sdings rdo rje phag mo sogs bo dong / lcags zam nyi ma chos 'phel sogs jo nang gi bstan 'dzin du ma/ dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ lha btsun don
grub rgyal mtshan/ bkra shis lhun po dang / se 'bras kyi mkhas pa mang po/ brag g.yabs no mi han chen po/ li thang mkhan rin po che mkhas mchog byams pa phun tshogs/ hor
khang sar rgyal ba sogs dge lugs phyogs/ rdor smin dpal ri/ lcags zam sogs kyi bla ma dge 'dun mang po/ kaHdpal zhe rdzogs kyi bla ma bla chen ci rigs/ gter chen mchog
gyur gling pa yab sras sogs snga 'gyur rnying ma'i phyogs kyis mtshon grub mtha' ris med pa'i zhal slob dang / bod kyi mi chen bka' mda' rtsis

gsum/ chos rgyal sde dge /gling rgyal po sogs la/ rig gnas 'chad spel ci rigs/ mdo rgyud kyi bshad bka'/ rnying ma/ bka' gdams/ sa ngor tshar gsum gyi lugs/ bka' brgyud/ shangs
chos/ zhi byed/ gcod yul/ dus 'khor gtsor gyur rgyud sde rnams kyi dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid/ lung sogs so so'i 'dod pa dang mthun par
phyogs dang ris med par spel/ rje nyid kyis gsan rigs rnams las bka' 'gyur tsam ma gtogs gzhan tshar re ma 'chad pa med cing / phal cher tshar grangs mang po dang / khyad
par mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid/ klong chen snying thig dbang khrid sogs ni zhu mkhan chad pa med par 'byung ba la thams cad kyi re ba skong bar mdzad/ phyis
su mdo khams chu bzhi sgang drug gi skye bo pho mo phal cher zhal mjal zhu bar 'ong ba rnams la'ang / tshe dbang dang 'pho lung gis mtshon pa'i chos 'brel mos pa dang 'tshams
par khor yug tu gnang / de ltar khams dbus kyi bla chen mi chen mtha' dag gis mngon par btud cing mchod kyang / ngo srung phyogs 'dzin dang / rang gzhan gyi mgo 'dren
zhu rgyu lta bus mtshon 'jig rten chos brgyad ci'ang mi spel bar chos dang mthun pa'i lam du drang tha ler bzhugs te khengs pa dang dregs pa cung zad tsam yang med par
snyom chung kho nas bya btang kun spangs kyi ngang tshul lhur blangs te bzhugs pa ni gcig tu ngo mtshar che bar sems/ lar rje nyid nas grub mtha' gang la'ang mi smod/ dag
snang ris med du sbyangs/ phan tshun bsre ba'ang mi mdzad/ bon po tshun chad kyang dngos brgyud gang rung nas thar pa'i lam stegs su nges pa'i

mos pas drangs te/ bstan pa thams cad la ci phan gyi thugs bskyed bzang po yod pa'i rten 'brel gyis phyogs de'i bon po rnams kyis kyang rang rang gi bla ma zhig dang mtshungs
par bzung ba sogs bstan pa thams cad kyi spyi dpal du bzhugs pa lags/ de la spyir skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'i mdo ni/ dam pa'i tshul dgu'am bcu gnyis
zhes yongs su grags pa ltar na/ mdo sngags rig gnas dang bcas pa mang du gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son/ bsam byung gi rig pas rang gzhan gyi grub mtha'i gnad ma 'dres par
mkhyen/ bsgoms pas nyams dang rtogs pa'i klong brdol/ mkhas pa phyogs re ba ma yin par mdo sngags rigs gnas nas tshig gi brda khyad phran bu yan chad la blo gros chen por
grags pa rnams kyi'ang the tshom sel nus pa mnga'/ btsun po ngo lkog can ma yin par chos dang mdzad spyod zhu dag pher/ bzang po phyogs lhung can ma yin par shin tu drang
po'i thugs bsam rnam par dag pa gser lta bur dpyod ldan kun gyis bsngags/ 'chad pa'i tshe lhag pa'i lha'i byin rlabs zhugs pa lta bus gzhung gang 'chad kyang dpe gzigs
dang thugs bsam sogs la ma ltos par ma Ni 'dren pa bzhin thogs pa med/ rtsod pa na dang po zhal gyis bzhes pa de brgal brtag ji tsam byas kyang lung rig gi sgrub byed dang
gting je zab tu 'gro ba ma gtogs ltag 'og 'gal ba'i snang la ma nges pa mi mnga'/ brtsam pa na tshigs bcad ches mang po sbrel te gsungs na'ang blo 'dzin byang ba lta
bur dpod pa ma gtogs thugs bsam dang zlos skyon sogs med/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyis ji snyed pa'i shes bya thams cad kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid gzigs/ ji lta ba'i gnas
lugs kyi dgongs pa brnyes/

brtse ba'i thugs rje bstan 'gro kun la phyogs lhung med pa'i phan pa 'ba' zhig mnga'/ nus pas kla klo gdug pa'ang zil gyis mnan par rdo rje'i lung gis bsngags na gzhan lta
ci smos so/ /de ltar chos kyi yon tan lta zhog /'jig rten gyi ngos nas kyang rje nyid kyi yab de shin tu blo drang zhing ngo lkog thub pa zhig yod 'dug stabs/ sde dge'i drung
yig chen mo lo nyer drug tsam du mdzad pa'i skabs/ mi bdag khrims ka tsha zhing thugs rtog ha cang rgod pas nyes chad ma byung ba'i sku drag su'ang med mod/ drung yig
dam pa des kha btags kha gang tsam shor ba'i bka' bkyon kyang ma byung bas spyi mi dung gi thor tshugs can zhes thams cad kyis bsngags pa dang / rdo rje 'chang nam mkha'
'chi med/ grub chen kun bzang gzhan phan/ kaHthog ma hA paNDi ta tshe dbang mchog grub sogs kyis kyang skyes bu dam pa zhig dang mtshungs par dngos su bka' gnang ba yi
ger bris pa deng dus kyang yod pas mtshon/ rje nyid kyang de'i rigs las 'khrungs pas thugs gzu bor gnas shing ha cang drang bas/ chos lugs kyi grub mtha'i khas len/ 'jig
rten gyi bsam spyod legs nyes gang la'ang nye ring phyogs cha gtan med par drang po kho nar mkhyen cing / drang po kho nar gsungs pas shes ldan rnams gcig tu mgu/ 'chol bar
spyod pa rnams bag za/ yid srubs kyi mthus brlabs pa'i mi srun rlangs por spyod pa rnams kyis rang mtshangs brtol ba ma bzod pas gshe skur kyang 'debs pa ni/ thig skud
drang por bzhag pa na/ /ya yo can gyi sems la gzan/ /zhes pa ltar snang ngo / /gzhan yang gdul bya/ grong chog /rnyed pas rnyed pa 'tshol ba sogs ched du gtad pa ci'ang
mi mdzad/

dgra 'dul gnyen skyong / tshong so nam nye du'i kha 'dzin sogs mnal lam du'ang mi mnga'/ phebs zhor lta bur gdan 'dren re tsam byung na sus ci byas re ba skong ba las nged
bya btang yin ces bum gog dang / lag pa mgor 'jog pa tsam la'ang srog chad chad kyi tshul 'chos mi mdzad/ rnyed pa gang byung thams cad 'phral byung 'phral dag gi dge rtsar
gtong ba ma gtogs phugs bsris su 'tshag pa dang / grwa 'khor nye du sogs rnam smin la mi 'dzems pa rnams la ngo dgas mtshon gnas min du zho gang yang chud zos su mi gtong
/ nang tshag la nged ban rgan 'chi nye ba yin zhes nges 'byung gi gsung thung ngu kho na las yun ring gi 'tsho rtsis 'di bya 'di byed kyi shom ra mi 'ding / thun mong
gi ngor nges 'byung la bsnyad pa'i ngu cho tshir tshir lta bu'i mngon tshan can mi mdzad/ bla ma rnams la'ang dngos su ha cang gus gus dung dung gi kha gsag gis thugs sna
mi 'brid mod/ lkog tu ming rus bla dwags tshun chad nas brjod pa'i brnyas bcos ma yin par rdo rje 'chang dang / rin po che sogs gsungs pa'i che ba 'ba' zhig pa'i bsngags
pa brjod pa sogs mos gus kyi rnam 'gyur bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad cing / thugs dad 'gyur ldog mi mnga' ba 'di kho na'ang deng sang gi bla ma dang slob ma cher rloms mngon
lkog can sus kyang 'gran du med pa'i rnam thar mchog gcig tu mngon/ spyir yang thugs kyi gting sgam pas sus kyang tshod mi dpog mod/ ltar snang du zhu sa zer sa ci'ang
med pa'i ngan dkyus dang / mkhas pa'i snyems pa dang / grub pa'i spu sud dang / thugs sna thung ngu can ma yin par kun dang mthun pa'i snyems chung dang / thugs chung
ngu mdzangs pa lta bu mdzad/ don du dus 'gyur chen mo'i skabs

sogs su lha chos kyi ngos nas skyes bu dam pa dang / blo gros can dang / mngon shes rdzu 'phrul nus pa can du rloms pa dang / mi chos kyi phyogs nas shes pa yon tan/ pho rgod
ngan g.yo can du brtsi ba stag dang seng ge lta bu thams cad kyis kyang snga bsam phyi mno cung tsam yang med par snying lkog mar lhud de phyi mig mi blta bar 'bros pa'am/
shes bzhin du dgra yi dwangs mar blo gtad ling bskyur mgo bcad dbang bzhag gis rang gzhan thams cad phung la sbyor ba sha stag gi 'khrul 'khor mig 'phrul lta bur bskor
ba dang / zhen pho rus sam/ khrel ngo tsha'am/ 'di phyi las 'bras sogs 'phongs phyis pa'i rdo bzhin dor te 'jig rten na grags pa'i kun rdzob kyi rdza phung ma rabs tha
chad kyi spyod ngan rdo ba'i char gyis rmengs med du bcom pa de lta bu'i skabs su'ang / 'jigs zil rngams zhud ji tsam che rung de tsam gyi thugs stobs lhag par rgyas te
ba spu'i rtse mo tsam yang mi g.yo bar/ pha rol po la skyabs 'tshol ba'am/ gzhan du byol ba lta bu'i rtog pa mnal lam du'ang rgyang bsrings te shin tu zungs thub pa lhun
po ltar ji mi snyam par bzhugs pas/ sus kyang ci'ang byar med pa sprin bral nyin mor byed pa ltar gzi brjid kyi dpal rab tu 'bar te/ sngon gyi dus rmog ston gsang bdag chen
po 'jigs bral chos dbyings rdo rjes rje nyid la 'jigs bral gyi slob dpon don thams cad grub pa zhes zhal rtsed kyi tshul du mtshan gyi cod paN dpyangs pa dang / rje de
nyid nas/ phyis o rgyan smin grol gling du bsnyen par rdzogs skabs bcas 'jigs med mkhyen brtse'i zlos gar phyogs las rnam rgyal dpal bzang po zhes pa'i mtshan phul ba'ang
skabs 'dir mngon gyur gyi don dang ldan pa'i lung

bstan lta bur sems/ des mtshon snyan khung ma thug cing thugs kyi gshis sus kyang bsgyur du mi btub/ mchog dman bar ma gang la'ang thugs dal dal skabs lta bur gnas tshul gyi
gsung gleng dri med zhib tu mdzad pa las zhal mi bsre ba dang / sbugs 'thums tshig sna thung ngu'i go dka' ba mi mdzad cing / gsung sgros rnams kyang mdo sbug med pa lhug
par stsal/ lhag par bka' gdams gong ma'i gsung sgros dang / bla ma rnams kyi zhal gsung dang / rje nyid kyi mdzad tshul sogs gna' gtam ya mtshan cing zla tshod tshes grangs
khungs dang gtan tshigs sogs shin tu zhib pa chos kyi snying po can mang du gsungs mod/ bdag lta bu'i blun po ni ngo dga' dang / phyogs lhung gi gtam chal chol chang
bzi'i blab col lta bu la mgu ba las/ de rigs nor skyong gi mdun du rtswa bzhag pa lta bur ma zad/ tha chad 'ga' zhig rna ba sun snang yang skye srid par 'dug /de las gzhan
du rang nyid mngon par bstod cing bsngags 'os smad pa dang / deng sang bla dpon phal cher gyis skad cha dri rgyu'i snying po nged rang la su zhig gis smad/ su zhig gis
bstod/ ci zer bar 'dug sogs re dogs kyi gze re tsher ma gzengs pa lta bu de 'dra gtan nas mi mdzad/ ma rabs 'ga' zhig gis rje nyid la gting nas gus pa med bzhin du deng
dus bla dpon spyi khyab kyi mdun sar gtam gyi lag sne med du mi rung ba ngo dga' phye gtor/ rang rang gi dga' mi dga'i rnam rtog snying por byas pa'i bstod smad dang / khyad
par mtho dogs dma' dga'i phrag dog gi zur za khyi rgan zug pa las lod pa de rigs gsan pa tsam nas gtam 'phro bcad de snyan gyi phyir phyogs su'ang mi bzhag par ma zad/
rjes su'ang mi de rigs kyi gtam la nyon nyan ci'ang med ces thugs

shin tu mi dgyes/ rje nyid kyi mdzad spyod gang la sus kyang chos dang mthun par brgal du med mod/ rang rang gi bsam sbyor phyin ci log pa dang ma mthun pa rgyu mtshan du bzung
nas smod pa dang skur pa sogs brgya la snyan du son na'ang mos pa sna tshogs pa'i sems can sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pas kyang mi mgu na bdag lta bus lta ci smos zhes re
dogs kyi zug rngu til gyi shun pa tsam yang mi mdzad cing / rje nyid kyi dgongs spyod gang yin pa de drang por bsrangs te bzhugs pa las bsgyur bkod kyi tsab tsub cung zad
kyang mi gnang / mkhas pa dang mi chen sogs kyi mdun sar ngo srung phye gtor mi gnang zhing zhum pa'i rnam pa tsam yang med par gsung sgros tshun chad drang tha ler gzengs
bstod de stsal/ phal pa dang byis pa chung ngu dman pa rnams la brnyas sems dang khengs pa mi gnang bar gsungs dpangs lhod pa dang zhal rtsed sogs ci dgar mdzad pas dbugs
dbyung ba las 'jigs 'jigs dang sgrob sgrob mi mdzad rung / sngon gyi las 'phro sad pa dang / nang du ting nge 'dzin mnga' ba'i mthus mchog dman thams cad zil gyis gnon
nus pa'i brtul zhugs khyad par can mnga' bas kun kyang gdong zhum bzhin du btud/ rje nyid kyi mdzad pa che phra gang la'ang / gal che skabs gting nas thugs yid ches pa'i
bla ma re re tsam la brtag pa mdzad pa tsam skul ba dang / rje rang nas bla ma dang dkon mchog la lung zhus brtag sgril re tsam ma gtogs/ gzhan chos dang mi 'gal zhing
/ 'jig rten dang mthun par dpyad de rang tshugs bzung nas 'jug pa ma gtogs mi mang kha mang gi gros kha mi 'ding / gsung las kyang rang re dang por skyes dus kyang gcig
pur skyes/ mthar 'chi dus kyang gcig pur 'chi

bas gal che shos de gnyis la blo ston gros byed mkhan su mi 'dug pa/ tshe 'di'i don rang thag rang gis ma chod pa ci yod ces bka' stsal nas rang dbang gzhan la mi bskur/ gzhan
gyis thugs blo 'dra zhus na'ang / nged la mngon shes ni med/ blo ni rang re thams cad smra shes don go mi'i lus rten can yin tsa na/ 'dod pa thog tu babs na dga'/ mi
'dod pa ma byung na dga' ba'i ci drag gang drag gi rnam rtog can re yin mod/ re bas yong ba sgrib pa'i dpes de 'dra i 'ong ci cha bas blo bkod nas bsam tshod ga la 'ong /
sprang po'i nyal bsam gyi dpe las med pas ci'ang lung ston mi shes zhes pa dang / lar yang mi mang tshogs pa dang / bka' chos sogs kyi skabs blang dor gyi spyi bshad re
tsam ma gtogs/ mi re re nas khyod kyis 'di gyis 'di ma byed ces bka' bkod de 'dra gtan nas mi mdzad cing / bka' las kyang / 'brom ston pas/ mi nyan pa la kha ta byed pa mtshangs/
/zhes pa ltar deng sang slob ma brgya yod kyang bla ma la nyan nges pa re re'ang dkon/ bu brgya yod kyang pha la nyan pa re re'ang dkon pas de 'dra la bslab ston
byed pa mi rang gnyis ka tshig pa za ba'i rgyu las ci yod ces mi thag rang gis nam yang mi gcod/ snying thag pa nas blo gtad pa yin tshe dkon mchog la lung zhus sogs zhib
cha mdzad nas sne re tsam bka' gnang ba las gdul bya bslu ba'i bab col mi gnang bas mtshon/ deng sang blo chung yid rloms mi 'ong bzhin du gzhan gyi mgo 'dren/ mi shes
bzhin du mngon shes dang rdzun lung 'chad/ mi thon bzhin du phan tshun bar 'dums/ mi nyan bzhin du gzhan la bslab ston dang slob dpon byed/ mi dga' bzhin du ngo srung dang
phye gtor mi byed rgu byed

pa/ spre'u dang byi la'i brtul zhugs can mang po la bsams na bla ma'i rnam thar kho na dran pa las gzhan du ci/ rje nyid sku na gzhon nu'i dus sku gzugs thang po zhig yin 'dug
rung / phyis 'khrugs gzhi dang / sbyar dug gi gzhi sogs byung bas rim par bod khams spyi'i bsod nams dman pas sku gzugs babs je zhan dang / snyun khams sna tshogs pa
je ljir gyur pa'i skabs su'ang / deng sang phal gyis blo sbyong la bsnyad pa'i tshul 'chos lta buu ma yin par/ nged sngon gyi las ngan pas sman gyis mi phan/ rim gro'ang
de dang 'dra/ na dga' shi skyid ga la yin/ chu tshod rer bde mo 'dug rgyu byung na los bzang ste/ sngon las la bcos su ci yod pas las bdag gir byed pa las 'os ma mchis zhes
khu sim mer bzhugs pa las/ ci drag ci'ang mi mdzad/ gzhan 'ga' res phyogs gzhan du mkhas pa/ btsun pa/ bya btang / grub thob/ gter ston sogs khyad par can 'di dang 'di
lta bu bzhugs zhes zhus na/ srid pa zer ba ci dang ci'ang srid pas de 'dra los yod ces las/ phal cher yongs su 'dris la sdang / /rtag tu gsar pa gsar pa 'tshol/ /zhes pa
ltar chos dang bla ma snga ma dor nas/ phyi ma phyi ma tshol ba'i a gsar dang / phrag dog gis gzhan la smod pa sogs mi mdzad/ lar/ grub thob dang / gter ston sogs los bzang
ste/ deng sang mkhas blun gyab chung sus kyang dang po grub gter gyi rigs la ha las las gnam sa khengs pa tsam du bsngags pa brjod cing rjes su 'brang / chos zhu/ je
zhig na bka' gdams rin po che'i gsung las/ rang re rnams dge ba'i bshes gnyen la zhe sa dang bcas pas skur pa 'debs su

'ong zhes pa ltar/ zhe sa ma zhus na'am zhe sa na zhes sngon du 'gro bas/ thugs sna thung / dbang yod che/ ngan long che/ mdzad rgyu mang / dran 'phrul rgod/ gsung rgyu mang
/ cha bzhag med/ phyag rdzas kyis don mi thon/ 'dzin 'chang che sogs kha shes tshad gtong ba dang / sprang po'i kha 'gegs pa'i ngan pa'ang zer don ci yod pas su la'ang
bzang ngan ci'ang ma smras par 'on pa ltar sdod na dga' zhes gsungs pas gnad che ba zhig yin 'dug snyam/ 'ga' zhig gis rten 'brel zhes gsung mod/ rje nyid nas/ rten 'brel
zhes pa de rang shugs kyis 'grigs pa las/ ched du bcos pas 'grigs rgyu yin tshod mi snang / mkhan chen bo dhi sa twa dang chos rgyal khri srong dus kyi rten 'brel la ltos/
rang shugs kyis 'grigs pa de'ang deng sang gdul bya thams cad bsod nams zad/ log rtog rgod/ the tshom mang / mnyam 'grogs che/ dam nyams mod/ de'i rjes su 'brang zhing
blo gtod pa kho nas bla mas ci byas skyon 'ba' zhig mthong ba'i dus 'dir rten 'brel bzang po de'ang 'grigs dus dka' zhes yang yang bka' gnang ba'ang thugs nyams can gyi
gsung du nges shing / rje nyid nas rten 'brel yin zhes nyag hor gyi khram chas byed/ nag chang spyod/ rta rgyugs/ mda' 'phen/ me mda' rgyags/ ri dwags gshor/ glu len/ bro
rdung / lung bstan/ lha babs/ 'dre babs zer ba'i srog rlung can a rag gis bzi ba lta bu la/ nged rang lta bus gang zag gi tshod gang zag gis mi zin pas mtha' gcig tu legs
nyes kyi kha tshon ga la chod kyang / spyir btang dam pa rnams thugs gting nas khrel bar ma zad/ chos rgyal khri srong dus nas/ dbu zlum mdo'i sde/ lcang lo

sngags pa'i sde zhes pa gnyis las/ khram chas rkun ma'i sde zhes pa'i phung po gsum pa zhig gtan nas med ces gsungs pa'ang blo gzu bor gnas shing mdo sngags kyi bstan pa la
mno bsam yod pa'i mi zhig yin na de 'dra zhig los yin e shi re snyam mod/ las ngan rnams la ci cha yod/ 'ga' zhig spyir grub mtha'i dgag sgrub mang po'i spu sud tsha po
dang / lhag par rang stong dang gzhan stong am zhig gi phyogs zhen rke chad chad 'then pa mang mod/ rje nyid nas rang rang gi grub mtha' gsungs pa'i skabs chos skad ma 'dres
par thad kar go sla zhing don 'dums pa re gsungs/ spyir btang grub mthas gtan la dbab bya'i snying po ni chos thams cad kyi chos nyid yin te/ de ni sher phyin las/ chos
nyid shes bya ma yin te/ /de ni rnam par shes mi nus/ /zhes gsungs par ma zad/ bod yul gyi rtog ge pa thams cad kyi gtsug gi nor bu rngog lo chen po lta bus kyang don
dam pa sgra rtog gi yul yin pa lta zhog /zhen pa'i yul tsam yang min par bzhed na/ gnas lugs mthar thug pa ni tshu rol mthong ba'i blo ji tsam zab kyang gtan la 'bebs mi
nus/ gnas skabs phyogs re nas gzhal ba'i dbang du byas na mkhas grub chen po rnams kyis rnam par bzhag pa'i chos skad re re la'ang sgrub byed kyi gtan tshigs dang 'thad pa
mang du snang bas rang rang gi lugs srol gang yin pa de'i rjes su 'brangs te bla ma gong ma'i bzhed pa rkang tshugs pa zhig byung na ha cang phyogs zhen rang mi dgos/ 'on
kyang chos skad dang grub mtha' phan tshun bsre ba dang / rang gi grub mtha'i rkang ma zin pas gzhan gyi na yam rgyab rten du khyer ba dang / lta sgom spyod 'bras kyi
lung thams cad mo ngan ma'i

thag cha 'dzings pa bzhin byas te lung don rigs pas rgyab 'khyol mi nus pa de 'dra ni rang gi grub mtha' la yid ma ches/ gzhan gyi rjes su bsnyegs 'dod kyang ma snyogs/ mkhas
pas mthong na bzhad gad kyi rgyu las ma 'das pas rang tshugs re zin pa byung na ni legs zhes gsungs/ la la gter lung ngam/ rang gi bla ma ga ge mo dang che ge mos gsungs
so lo zhes rang phyogs 'ga' zhig zhal mjal ba'am/ phyag dbang thob pa tsam gyis ngan song med ces sangs rgyas byang sems kyi rgyal tshab sogs su bsngags pa ha cang thal
ba mang po byed/ gzhan phyogs 'ga' zhig mkhas btsun bzang po'i yon tan mthong chos su mnga' ba rnams la'ang 'brel tshad ngan song du 'gro skad pa mang ba la/ rje nyid nas
rang gi bla ma la 'jig rten gyi zhen pho rus tsam min par snying nas sangs rgyas su mthong ba'i mos gus kyi bstod bsngags yin na bzang mod/ gzhan phyogs kyi chos dang
gang zag bzang po'i rigs la dad pa ma byung rung / log lta'i skur 'debs de 'dra byed pa ni chos spong ba'i las zhes mtshams med lnga las kyang thu/ gter lung rigs kyang 'ga'
re blun po snying kham can gyis o rgyan padma rdzun rgyab tu spyan drangs nas gsar du chags sdang gis dkrugs te sbyar ba'i lag rjes mngon sum pa'ang mang / gal srid gter
yig tshad ldan las phab pa zhig yin du zin kyang / dgongs gzhi/ dgos pa/ dngos la gnod byed ci rigs pas mtha' gcig tu khungs de tsam la 'chel nas chos dang gang zag 'gangs
che ba la smod pa'ang blun che ba yin pas/ 'di 'dra 'dzin pa lta ci smos/ /thos par gyur kyang rna ba dgab/ /ces gsungs pa ltar ro zhes bka' gnang ba blun po snying
kham can

dag 'di rigs la bag yod cung zad re dgos par sems te/ 'phags pa chos thams cad 'byung ba med pa zhes bya ba'i mdo las/ rigs kyi bu/ phra ba ni las kyi sgrib pa yin gyis/ su
las kyi sgrib pa mi 'dod pa de dag gis gzhan gyi spyod pa la khong khro bar mi bya'o/ /de'i spyod pa thams cad la yid ches par bya'o/ /'di snyam du pha rol gyi sems ni bdag
gis mi shes te/ sems can gyi spyod pa ni shes par dka' 'o snyam du sems bskyed par bya'o/ /don gyi dbang de gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pas 'di skad du chos ston te/ gang
zag gis gang zag la tshod gzung bar mi bya'o/ /gang zag gis gang zag gi tshod bzung na rma 'byung bar 'gyur te/ nga'am gzhan yang nga dang 'dra ba dag gis gang zag la
tshod gzung ngo / /rigs kyi bu su bdag bsrung bar 'dod pa des gzhan su'i spyod pa la'ang brtag par mi bya ste/ de dag la 'di ni 'di 'dra'o/ /'di ni 'di 'dra'o zhes dpya bar
mi bya'o/ /nyin mtshan du sangs rgyas kyi chos la brtson par bya'o/ /zhes sogs 'byung ba dang / bsdus pa'i mdo las/ 'jam dpal dam pa'i chos spong ba'i las kyi sgrib pa
ni phra'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i bka' la la ni bzang bar 'du shes/ la la ni ngan par 'du shes pa ni chos spangs pa'o/ /gang chos spangs pa des chos spangs pas
de bzhin gshegs pa la skur pa 'debs pa yin/ dge 'dun la ngan du brjod pa yin no/ /'di ni rigs so/ /'di ni mi rigs so zhes zer na chos spangs pa'o/ /'di ni byang chub sems
dpa' rnams kyi ched du gsungs pa'o/ /'di ni nyan thos rnams kyi ched du gsungs pa'o/ /'di ni rang sangs

rgyas rnams kyi ched du gsungs pa'o/ /zhes zer na chos spangs pa'o/ /zhes tshad mar gyur pa'i lung 'di la'ang 'gal zlar ma gyur pa rje 'di kho na tsam las mang du ma mthong
ngo / /bdun pa zhar byung du bsod nams kyi tshogs rlabs po che sgo du ma nas spel ba'i tshul ni/ deng sang dus ngan snyigs ma lnga bdo ba'i mtha' la thug /thub pa'i bstan
pa lung rtogs gnyis ka gzugs brnyan tsam la spyod pa'i skabs 'dir/ bstan pa 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen du grags pa phal po che rnams kyang thos bsam sgom gsum gyi mdzad pa
gal chung ngu bzhag nas/ rgyal bstan ris med la phan pa dang 'gro ba mtha' dag gi bsod nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba la dmigs pa'i thugs bskyed yod med ji ltar yang gcig la
gcig ltos tshul gyis lha khang / sku gzugs mchod rten/ gar 'chams kyi chas sogs ltar snang ya mtshan dang 'ur sgrob skyed pa'i bya ba las kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni mang zhing
/ de las dman pa kha cig so so'i dgon gnas kyi gzhi 'dzin tsam gyi ched du thos bsam sgom gsum gyi bya ba ling gis bor nas mi tshe hril por dkor rjes su rgyug kyang yul
gyi mi dpon gyi thob 'jal/ gzhan tshe 'di'i gyod dang kha mchu'i gyang gud kho na'i ngang du gram gseng chu blugs kho na las bstan pa yar rgyas 'ong rgyu med pa'i khar
mkho rgu'ang 'dzom dus med pa sogs spyi'i lam srol lta bu yin 'dug kyang / rje 'di ni sku tshe hril por thos bsam sgom gsum sogs dam pa'i tshul dgus bstan dang 'gro ba'i
don sgrub pa'i mdzad pa kho na ma gtogs/ bstan don dang dge ba'i mthun rkyen du bsnyad pa'i dbyar ldom dgun ldom grong chog gson gshin gyi dkor nag gi rjes su nyin gcig
tsam yang phebs bzhud mdzad ma myong ba dang / dman pa'i brtul

zhugs lhur bzhes pas thob 'jal gyi log 'tsho sogs kyang gtan nas mi mnga' bas spyi mthun ltar na kun spangs bya bral kho na'i tshul du bzhugs kyang sngon gyi thugs bskyed tshogs
bsags kyi stobs las ji ltar mkho ba'i 'dod rgu thams cad 'bad med lhun grub tu 'byung ba dang / ji skad du/ me tog dri ni rdzi phyogs min mi 'gro/ /rtsa brgya spos
sam tsandan kyang ma yin/ /dam pa'i dri ni rdzi phyogs mi 'gro ste/ /phyogs rnams kun tu mi mchog dri yis khyab/ /ces pa ltar sku che ba'i yon tan gyi snyan pa'i grags pa
sa bla'i lha rnams kyis bsgrags pa lta bus phyogs mtha' dag gi bla chen mi dpon skye bo pho mo grangs kyis mi chod pa 'dus nas 'byor 'khos dang bstun pa'i mchod 'bul dang
/ skyabs 'jug bsngo rten chad med du 'byung ba de dag thams cad kyang gnas min du khab gcig gi rtsa ba tsam yang chud zos su btang bar mi mdzad par/ dkon mchog gi rten
gsum bzhengs pa/ bla ma dang dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur/ dus dang / rgyun gyi mchod pa/ phongs pa la sbyin pas rjes su 'dzin pa sogs gtong ba nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgo 'phar gtan
pa med par dbye bar mdzad pa de dag zhib par smos kyis longs pa'i go skabs ma mchis kyang / 'dir de dag las gtso che ba tsam rags bsdus su smos na/ thog mar lha khang
dang sku gsung thugs rten gyi skor la/ rje nyid kyi zhal gsungs rnam thar rtsa tho las ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin lha khang bcu gsum tsam bzhengs par mdzad pa'ang thog mtha'
bar gsum kun tu 'gan bzhes phyag bstar gyis bzhengs pa dang / gzhan dag la zhal 'debs mthun rkyen zhal bsgos sogs kyis kyang rnam dkar gyi mdzad sgo skyong ba'i lha khang
rtsa lag mang du bskrun pa'i

gtso bo rdzong gsar bkra shis lha rtse'i dbu rtser mngon byang lha khang ka ba lnga bcu nga lnga'i mal steng 'og phyi nang shin tu dngos gtsang bkod mdzes su yun thung ngus
mthar phyin par bsgrubs pa'i nang rten gyi gtso bo thub dbang sku khri rgyab yol gyi bkod pa sogs khyad mtshar rin chen du ma'i brgyan sogs shin tu spus nam dag pa/ thub

tu spus legs/ zhal bram gzugs/ 'dod khams ma/ phyag bzhi/ phyag drug /rgya gar shar li'i mgon po gri gug /rnam sras/ nor rgyun ma/ g.yas phyogs gtso bo tshe dpag med/
li sku dang kha skong gser zangs 'dres ma brgyad kyis bskor ba/ 'od dpag med gtso 'khor gsum/ steng du sman bla li ma la 'khor bdun zangs gser las bskrun pa mkhyid gang ba
re/ 'og tu slob dpon padma dngul sku la mtshan brgyad gser zangs las bskrun pas bskor ba/ g.yon logs gtso bor byams pa mgon po la 'khor rgyal sras rigs gsum mgon po/ nye
sras brgyad/ mi 'khrugs pa rgya sku la bkra shis lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba/ mdun du sgrol ma li dmar tsha gser can la/ 'khor rgya bod kyi li sku dang gser sku 'dres ma
nyer gcig /phugs logs chos khri'i dbus su thugs chen bcu gcig zhal rigs bzhis bskor ba/ chos longs sprul gsum/ de thams cad kyi steng du gtso bo rdo rje 'chang gtso 'khor

cog

zhang gsum/ mnga' bdag khri ral/ jo bo a ti sha /kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ 'brom ston pa/ rngog lo yab sras/ mar mi dwags gsum/ bu ston rin po
che/ dol po sangs rgyas/ rje rin po che yab sras gsum/ rdzong pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ tshar chen/ thar rtse mkhan chen byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin/
'jam dpal bzang po/ bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan bcas bzhi/ slar gsar du bzhengs par mdzad pa'i mkhan slob chos gsum/ rgyal chen indra bhU ti/ chos rgyal zla bzang / grub chen
sa ra ha/ klu thogs rnam gnyis/ ArYa de ba/ dbyig gnyen/ phyogs glang / chos kyi grags pa/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ 'brog mi lo tsA/ grub chen khyung po rnal 'byor/ pha

'jam pa'i rdo rje gnyis/ bde mchog lU hi pa/ nag po pa/ rdo rje 'jigs byed bskums khru gang / gshin rje gshed dmar po/ dgra nag /'byung 'dul/ mkha' spyod skor gsum/ dmar po

chos gsum/ mar mi dwags gsum/ jo bo rje/ rje yab sras gsum/ gnas brtan bcu drug /tsandan gyi bde mchog /gsang 'dus sogs sku rten spus nam ldan pa shin tu mang po/ lha

shin tu spus ldan byon gtsang / shing gi mchod sdong cha brgyad gser 'dur gsol ba/ gzhan yang gsar du bzhengs par mdzad pa'i rnam snang mngon byang khri rgyab bcas spus
legs mda' tshad ma/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ slob dpon bcas mda' tshad re gtsos lha khang 'di kho nar bla ma yi dam chos srung sogs

kyi sku brnyan gsar rnying che chung lnga brgya skor dang / bka' gdams mchod rten cha brgyad gtsos mchod rten che chung sum cu tsam bzhugs khang sogs bkod legs khyad mtshar
dang bcas bzhugs su gsol bar mdzad cing / gong gsal gsar du bzhengs par mdzad pa'i bla sku re la/ mgar ba las zangs sku bslus pa'i dbang du dngul srang bdun re/ lag bzos
la de lhag srang do re tsam gnang ba bcas mdor bsdoms sku re la dngul srang 'degs brgyad re 'gro nges dang / gtso bo thub dbang sku la dngul rdel tshad brgyad tsam/ byams
pa tshe dpag gnyis bsdoms rdel tshad bdun tsam/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku yon bdag gzhan gyis gus pas phul ba la legs gsos kyi tshul du dngul srang bzhi bcu tham pa gnang
zhing bsdoms pas dngul srang drug cu tsam/ bde gsang gur saM rnams la dngul srang nyi shu re/ dmar po skor gsum can gser chos lha rnams la dngul bzhi ru re/ rnam snang mngon
byang sku dang / rdo rje sems dpa' bcas la dngul srang bdun cu don lnga re tsam/ mchon rten che ba la rdel tshad bzhi/ cha brgyad la dngul srang nyi shu re gnang rtsis
kyis rdel tshad gsum drag tsam gyi yon bstabs pa yin 'dug pa sogs de dag gis phyis 'dir bstan 'gro'i gsos su dgongs te gsar bzhengs dbu rtse'i lha khang rten brten par
bcas pa'i bzhugs tshul phyogs tsam smos pas mtshon/ thub dbang gnas bcu lha khang ngo mtshar kun tu gzigs pa'i zhing khams ka ba dgu'i mal gsar bzhengs la/ rten gtso gser
zangs las grub pa'i thub dbang longs spyod rdzogs sku che legs khri rgyab yol sogs spus ldan la 'khor nye sras brgyad/ gnas brtan bcu drug /ltung bshags

so lnga/ rdo rje 'chang li ma/ sgrol ma nyer gcig /gu ru mtshan brgyad/ kun rig rtsa lha so bdun/ rgyal ba rig lnga sogs gser zangs shin tu spus nam ldan pas mtshon/ gzhan
yang sku brnyan sna tshogs pa phyogs bsdoms sum brgya sum cu tsam/ gser zangs byang chub mchod rten che legs/ cha brgyad cha gsum sogs mchod rten che chung sum cu so bzhi
tsam/ bka' 'gyur rin po che/ bstan bcos 'gyur ro 'tshal/ 'khor lo tha ma'i mdo sde phyogs bsdus nges don pod drug /sher phyin stong phrag brgya pa/ sa skya gong ma rnam
lnga'i bka' 'bum/ zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gsung 'bum/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi bka' 'bum/ zhwa lu'i dkyil chog rigs/ rig gnas cha tshang sogs glegs bam shin tu grangs
mang gis g.yon logs drwa mig khyab par bkang / de'i khang steng du dpe mdzod thugs chen lha khang gru 'dzin bkod par gtso bo thugs rje chen po sems nyid ngal gso/ thugs
chen phyag bzhi pa/ bcu gcig zhal rnams gser zangs phra bkod sogs spus nam ldan pa/ bde gshegs so lnga chung / mchod rten cha brgyad/ dpe sgam bzhi'i khrod du/ sa skya/
rnying ma/ bka' brgyud/ dge phyogs kyi yig cha ma tshang ba med pa/ sman rtsis 'grel pa sogs rigs gnas skor te bris ma shas che'i glegs bam shin tu grangs mang gis phyur
bur bkang ba dang / steng du zangs gser gyi ganydzir che legs bcas/ 'du khang steng lam 'bras lha khang du/ thub dbang gnas bcu/ birWa pa/ gong ma rnam lnga/ gu ru mtshan
brgyad/ bla sku rigs re zung / mchod rten spus legs/ sa skya bka' 'bum sogs/ bla ma lha khang du gsar bzhengs 'dra zhal/ grub

mtha' ris med bla sku sogs sku bco lnga skor/ rnying ma rgyud 'bum/ rdzogs chen snying thig ya bzhi/ klong chen mdzod bdun sogs glegs bam du ma/ dzaM nang sgrub phug lha khang
steng 'og tu gu ru bde ba chen po/ mtsho rgyal sku bcas zangs gser las bskrun pa/ gzhan de ga phan tshun tu sgrol ma nyer gcig sogs gser sku'ang mang tsam/ mdzod bdun
sogs glegs bam mang rab/ 'og tu gzim khang yin rgyu'i nang sku zhal thang / mchod cha/ thab chas skor cha tshang rten 'jog dang / zla gam dbang phug sgrub khang du rtsa
gsum byin rlabs rang bab lder so byon legs kyis gtsos rten gsum dgos cha tshang ma/ rong me dkar mo stag tshang sgrub khang dang rten gsum bcas/ khang dmar mdor lha khang
bang ba gsar 'dzugs dang zangs gser las grub pa'i thub sku mda' tshad ma gtsos pa'i rten gsum mchod cha ci rigs sbyor 'jags dang / kham bye thang du rigs gsum lha khang
ka ba dgu can gsar bskrun mdzad pa'i nang / thub dbang / nye sras brgyad/ gnas brtan bcu drug /rigs gsum mgon po che legs re/ chos sku yum chen sku rgya nag ma khru tshad
la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis bskor bas mtshon sku thor bu mang po/ bka' gdams mchod rten bzo dbyibs khru tshad la sku gdung cha brgyad zangs gser las bskrun pas bskor
ba/ sher phyin stong phrag brgya pa'i glegs bam bcu gnyis sogs chos sna mang tsam gyi glegs bam/ ldebs ris la sdom gsum brgyud pa/ ris med bla ma sogs tshon ris spus dag
dang ganydzi ra bcas/ rje nyid kyi gzim spyil bkra shis 'chi med grub pa'i dga' tshal gyi lha khang phyi nang du bla ma yi dam chos srung gi sku brnyan li ma/ gser zangs
gsar rnying

brgya dang bcu skor/ gsung rten glegs bam shin tu mang pos phyi nang thams cad khyab par bkram pa'i byin rlabs kyi gzi brjid dpal du 'bar bar bzhugs pa bcas 'di rigs rje bla
ma rang nyid kyis mgo lung rgyu 'don bcas kyis gsar bzhengs gnang ba'i lha khang rten gsum 'ba' zhig dang / gzhan yang ngos kyi ri khrod sgrol ma lha khang du 'chi med
'phags ma'i sku brnyan gser zangs phra bkod sogs nam ldan gtso 'khor bcu bzhi gnang zhing / rdzong sar 'du khang du sku brnyan thor bu bzhi bcu skor rten bzhag dang / a lo
dpal 'byor dgon du mkhan bla ma bkra shis 'od zer gyi lha khang du'ang ston pa longs sku gser zangs las bskrun pa/ bde gshegs so lnga/ nye sras brgyad kyi ldem sku gser
zangs mtho gang ba re bcas stsal/ dgon chen kun yon lha khang du bla brgyud/ kye rdor lha dgu sogs gser sku lnga bcu tsam stsal gnang dang / rdzong sar mnga' sgang / gnas
ra bcas kyi lha khang gsar bskrun sogs kyis mtshon pa'i gzhan dang gzhan kun la de 'dra'i rnam dkar rten bzhengs kyi bdag rkyen ci rigs pa gnang ba ma zad/ grwa rkyang
sa sku drwa mig tsam bzhengs pa'i rtsol ba byed mkhan rnams la tshon rtsi yan gnang ba'i mthun 'gyur rnam pa kun tu ma mdzad pa med pa lta bu'i 'di rigs kyang rje bla ma'i
thugs rje brgyud nas byung ba gor ma chag pas mtshon/ mdor na snga phyir gong gsal lha khang khag rnams su bkod mdzes su gtan bzhag mdzad pa dang / bla dgon gzhan la'ang
ci rigs par bstsal ba bcas gser zangs 'ba' zhig las grub pa stong phrag gnyis tsam bzhengs par mdzad pa dang / gsung rten skor rje nyid nas jo nang rin 'byung gi rgyab
chos tshul du lha so so'i sgrub thabs las tshogs bcas

dkyus gcig tu bka' bsdu spel ba'i gsang sngags gsar ma'i sgrub thabs rab 'byams gcig tu btus pa'i glegs bam chen po bcu gcig gi yon smar zong sbyar te spar du bskrun par mdzad
pas mtshon/ gsar rnying gi 'don cha nyer mkho mang tsam/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ jo nang rje btsun sgrol mgon zhabs kyis bsdebs pa'i bdag cag gi ston pa'i mdzad
brgya/ rgya gar chos byung / byams chos lnga sogs bka' pod phal che'i rtsa ba/ mngon pa gong 'og dang / kun mkhyen rong po'i 'byed gnyis kyi 'grel pa sogs gzhung dang gzhung
'grel du ma phyag bstar gyis spar du bkod pa dang / dpyod ldan 'byor pa can gzhan la'ang zhal bsgos kyis bskul zhing dngos po'i zhal 'debs sbyar ba'i sgo nas bsgrubs
pa'ang / dgon chen du rong ston chen po'i sher phyin mngon rtogs rgyan gyi 'grel bshad dang rgyud bla ma'i 'grel pa bcas/ rma bya byang brtson gyi dbu ma rtsa ba'i 'grel
pa/ re mda' ba'i dbu ma 'jug pa'i 'grel pa/ mtsho sna ba'i 'dul ba mdo rtsa'i 'grel chen glegs bam gnyis/ skyed tshal ba'i 'dul TIka /mchims 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi mngon
mdzod 'grel chen glegs bam gnyis/ sa bzang paN chen spyod 'jug 'grel chen/ rgyal sras thogs med spyod 'grel dang / mdo sde rgyan 'grel/ klong chen pa'i yid bzhin mdzod rtsa
'grel/ mi pham rgya mtsho'i dbu ma rgyan gyi 'grel chen/ 'u yug pa'i tshad ma rig pa'i mdzod sogs mdo sngags gzhung 'grel rig pa'i gnas sogs kyi glegs bam bzhi bcur nye
ba'i spar dang / bka' gter gsar rnying grub mtha' ris med pa'i gzhung gdams man ngag /tha na so so'i lam mthun man ngag tshad ldan shog ldeb gcig

'dug kyang gsar bris kyis bzhengs par mdzad pa'i pusti nyis brgya yar brgal dang / bod dbus gtsang du bzhugs pa'i spar ma gal gang che thams cad/ mdo khams 'dir sbar ldeb gcig
tsam gang mchis tshar re ma btab pa med pa sogs bris ma dang spar ma bsdoms pas pusti ka stong phrag gnyis tsam gsar du bzhengs par mdzad pa de dag la'ang glegs shing
/ glegs thag /gdong dar/ chab mgo /sgril chas yan shin tu rgyu spus dag pa'i bkur sti sri zhu bcas mig gi bdud rtsir mdzad pa dang / thugs rten lhun grub steng mchod sdong
mthong grol chen po thog tshad shin tu mtho ba gser dngul phra rgyan gyi bkod pa sogs spus nam ldan pa dngul rdel tshad brgya dang brgyad tsam gyi babs kyis bskrun par
mdzad pas gtsos gser zangs 'ba' zhig las grub pa'i mchod sdong che chung brgya phrag lhag pa bsgrubs par mdzad pa ste/ gong smos rten gsum/ lha khang bcas rab tu mang ba
bzhengs par mdzad pa'i rigs gtso che ba rags pa bsdus pa'i lugs kyis sa bon tsam smos par zad kyi/ sku brnyan dang glegs bam gyi tshogs 'du mdzad pas de dag gzhan la gnang
stsol mdzad pa yan rnam grangs sogs re re nas zhib par smos kyis mi longs shing ha cang yi ge'i tshogs su che ba dang / 'dir de tsam las bkod dgos pa'i gal chen po rang
yang mi 'dug pas de tsam mo/ /bla ma dang dge 'dun la yul khyad par bar dgongs te bsnyen bkur mdzad pa'ang / rje rang nyid kyis zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi bzhes pa'i
bla ma rdo rje 'dzin pa/ dge ba'i gshes gnyen snga phyi kun gyi zhal sngar bka' chos gsan pa'i snga logs sam thog mar zhu rten me tog gam maNDal/ mjug grub pa'i sku drin

gtang rag gi mchod sprin dngos po spus nam gang ldan rtsal sprugs kyis g.yo zol ser sna'i dri mas cung zad kyang ma gos par gus shing dwangs ba chen pos lan mang du spros te
phul ba dang / phyis 'dir yang dpal yul sprul pa'i sku karma kun bzang bstan 'dzin/ dzar ga mchog gi sbrul sku kun bzang rnam rgyal dag gi zhal snga nas zab chos kyi dbang
lung du ma gsan bzhes gnang ba'i skabs rnams su yon dang maNDal gyi dngos po bzang la gya nom pas dgyes pa bskyed pa dang / bdag cag la'ang bong ba gser du gzigs pa'i
dag snang gis rje nyid kyi bla ma'i gral du 'jog cing snga phyi dus rnam kun tu maNDal/ zhabs brtan sogs kyi ched du sku gsung thugs rten rtsa ba gang ches thog drangs/
dngos rdzas nyer spyad mkho rgu spus ka gtsang dag gi rigs gyur yang nas yang du stsal ba sogs kyis mtshon/ ris med kyi bla ma chos kyi 'brel ldan rnams la bkur bsti mchod
'bul rgya che la rgyun chags par mdzad pa'ang / bla ma lnga bcu pa las/ mi bzad de nyid 'dod pa yis/ /cung zad yid 'ong gang dang gang / /shin tu khyad par gyur pa nyid/
/de dang de ni bla mar dbul/ /zhes sogs mdo rgyud bstan bcos kun nas bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen la bkur zhing mchod pa'i tshul rgya cher 'byung ba'i don thugs dbus su
bcangs te phyag len du khel bar mdzad pa dang / ris med pa'i dge 'dun gyi sde che phra gang na su mchis pa thams cad la phyis der dus 'khrugs stobs su bdo ba'i rkyen gyis
phal mo che nyams gud cher gyur ba rnams la zhig gsol zhal 'debs kyi tshul du gnang sbyin dngos ja stong phrag gsum lhag pa stsal cing / rgya bod kyi dpon chen/ chos rgyal
sde dge dpon blon rnams la mthun

sbyor mdzad gal gnad bkrol gnang ba'i sgo nas sngar gnas sor chud kyi nyams pa gsos pa'i bdag po'i rkyen dang / mchod thebs kyi zhal 'debs/ lugs gnas tshul mthun gyi zhal bsgos
tshul bzhin stsal ba'i sgo nas dar rgyas 'phel ba'i bka' drin rlabs po che gnang ba ni/ ji skad du/ skyes rabs las/ zla ba'i kun dga' nyi ma'i rab gsal dang / /me yi
tsha ba rlung gi mgyogs pa dang / /snying rje'i dga' ba skye bo che rnams kyis/ /gzhan la phan pa lhan skyes rang bzhin yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar bstan 'gror gcig tu phan
pa lhur bzhes pa'i rnam thar gtsang ma ni rje 'di la mnga' ba mngon sum pa'i tshad mar grub cing / gzhan yang phan tshun gyi chos sde che chung rnams la lo re bzhin du
gzungs sngags dang bsngo ba'i rten yon sbyar gnang ba snga rjes dngos ja bzhi stong lhag pa'i rtsa ba nyams med du phul bas mtshon/ tha na dben pa'i rir dge sbyor la gnas
pa'i bya bral yan la chos dang 'tsho chas kyi mthun rkyen yang dag pas skyong ba sogs bla ma dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur chos dang mthun pa'i phyag len 'di lta bu sku nyams
su bstar ba'i phyis kyi dus 'dir gangs can tsam na rje 'di tsam las mang du mchis pa mi dran to/ /dus dang rgyun gyi mchod pa'i sprin du gyur pa khor yug tu chad pa med par
mdzad pa'i tshul yang / gong du ji ltar smos zin pa'i lha khang bcu gsum rtsa lag rnams su mchod pa'i yo byad phun sum tshogs pa spyi dang / bye brag spos mar me sogs
kyi rgyun thebs sbyor 'jags/ khyad par bde mchog nag po lugs kyi sgrub mchod/ gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub mchod/ sbyong rgyud kun tu rig pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub
mchod/ rigs gsum sgrub

mchod sogs gsar rnying gi rgyud sde mang po'i sgrub mchod kyi rgyun ji srid par 'dzugs par mdzad pa'i chas 'khor yo byad mchod rdzas gzabs spros sogs mchod pa'i sprin phung
rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / gzims spyil gyi lha khang phyi nang bar khyams kun tu mar me'i phreng ba nyin mtshan rgyun chad med pa/ dri bzang gi bdug spos rgyun btul/ gzhan
yang me tog gi rigs gyur/ chab gtsang ma'i mchod yon brgya tshar mang po/ zhal zas kyi phreng ba sogs dus kun tu chad bul med pa'i mchod 'bul dngos dag gtsang sbras thon
pa dang / nyin bstar chags su tshogs mchod kyi rdzas bza' btung bda' dgu'i yo byad dang ldan pa re chag med/ rgyal khams bstan 'gro spyi'i don du glud bsngo re la glud rdzas
dngul gyi dong tse gsum bzhi re'i rtsa ba yod pa nyin bzhin btang ba sogs gnyug mar skyong ba'i mchod sbyin gyi rigs rgya chen dang / dmigs bsal dus kyi mchod pa'ang
yar mar tshes bcu'i mchod pa rgyas pa re la mar me'i phreng ba kho na'ang brgya phrag kha yar gyis mtshon tshogs kyi yo byad sogs mchod rdzas dngos dag ci rgyas/ rgyal ba'i
dus chen bzhi dang / nya stong brgyad sogs la gsung chog skabs babs dang 'brel ba'i spos dang mar me brgya rtsa'i phreng ba du ma tshar du dngar ba'i mchod pa'i sprin
gyi bkod pa kun tu bzang po'i smon lam las byung ba lta bu'ang lo zla bstar chags su chag 'phri med par 'du mdzad cing bsod nams kyi tshogs gsog pa'i thabs kyi sgo la gcig
tu brtson par mdzad pa 'di tsam yang rgyu 'bras rten cing 'brel 'byung zab mo'i gnas la thugs kyi nges pa gzhan dring mi 'jog par 'drongs pa'i rnam thar du nges pas shes
ldan rnams

cis kyang ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /ji skad du/ sbyin pa'i g.yab mos legs bos te/ /snyan par smra bas yid rab drangs/ /don spyod pa yis bag phabs te/ /don mthun gros chen gdab
par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis gdul bya 'dun par byed pa'i thabs la bskal par goms pa brtan pa'i mthus/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'jug ngogs
dam pa 'di lta bu'i phrin las rmad du byung ba bdag gir mdzad pas/ mchog dman kun la zang zing dngos po'i gnang sbyin gya nom pa phangs pa med par ster bas dga' ba dang
mgu ba skyed cing / dman pa'i 'gro ba bya khyi yan dbul zhing phongs ba'i rigs la gang 'tshams kyi zas gos sogs lhug par stsal bas lus sems la phan pa nye bar bsgrub pa
dang / tha na gsung tshig snyan cing yid du 'ong ba'i 'phros gtam gnang ba yan gyis gzhan sems la spro ba skyed pa sogs mdor na gtong ba nam mkha' mdzod chen po'i sgo gtan
pa med par dbye bas bsod nams kyi tshogs rlabs po che bsags pa'i nor bu'i gram bu thang mar brdal bas srid zhi'i dbul ba thams cad gcig car du bcom par mdzad pa yin no/
/rtsa ba'i sa bcad brgyad pa mdzad pa phrin las mthar phyin nas sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings su bsdus pa'i tshul ni/ rje bla ma thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen
po de nyid thog mar yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po bsnyen nas shes bya'i gnas spyi dang khyad par mdo sngags kyi chos tshul ris su ma chad pa mtha' dag la gsan bsam mthar phyin
par mdzad pas chos kyi rgya mtsho chen por gyur/ bar du gsan pa tsam du ma bzhag par thos don rgyud la sbyor ba'i sgom sgrub sngags gsar rnying yongs

rdzogs su mdzad pas sngon sbyangs kyi 'phro sad nas sa dang lam gyi yon tan yongs su rdzogs/ mthar smon lam dang snying rje'i rtsal shugs kyis ris su ma chad pa'i bstan pa
dang mchog dman bar ma'i 'gro ba mtha' dag la phan pa dang bde ba'i phrin las kyi bdud rtsi'i klung chen po phab/ khyad par du sa skya paN chen gyi zhal nas/ lung rig rjes
su gdams pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos tshad mar gyur pa'i lung dang / sgra tshad dngos stobs dang mthun pa'i rig pa dang / chos nyid zab mo dang mi
'gal ba'i rjes su gdams pas skal pa dang ldan pa'i gang zag dbang po mchog dman mtha' yas pa thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam la bkri ba sogs deng sang snyigs dus na
bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu sus kyang 'gran gyi zla dang bral ba'i mdzad pa'i phrin las thams cad mthar phyin nas/ mdo sde rgyan las/ ji ltar chu yi snod chag na/ /zla ba'i
gzugs brnyan mi snang la/ /de bzhin sems can ngan pa la/ /sangs rgyas gzugs kyang mi snang ngo / /zhes gsungs pa ltar gdul bar bya ba'i snyigs ma'i skye bo rnams bsod nams
dang skal ba dman pas thugs rje 'jug pa'i yul du ma gyur cing / zhing gzhan du phrin las 'jug pa la don che bar dgongs te dus rgyun du'ang dred bo rnams chos la bskul
ba'i ched du/ ban rgan nam 'chi mi shes/ ci la'ang 'bras bu med/ cis kyang dgos pa med ces bka' stsal pa dang mthun par/ dgung lo don gsum bzhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lo'i
zla ba dang po'i nyer lnga'i dus mchod rgyas par btang / nye skor gyi yig nyob sogs gtsang mar mdzad nas mchod dpon bla ma la'ang de ring phyin chad khyod nas dka' las ci'ang
mi dgos

zhes bka' stsal nas sbug gi gzims gshag tu phebs/ phyir nyin nas sku khams mi dwangs pa'i tshul bstan/ de nas rim par zhabs g.yas phyogs skrangs ba zhig gis bzhengs bzhugs
mi bde ba byung skabs zhabs 'greng ba rnams kyis sku rim bsgrub dgos tshul nan tan zhus par/ sku rim gang yang bsgrub mi dgos zla ba rjes ma'i nyi shu skor drag 'gro ba yin
gsungs/ thar rtse dang phan khang mkhan rin po che rnam gnyis dang phran la'ang zhabs brtan ci drag gis bskul ma byung ba ltar/ rang nas kyang 'phags ma'i snying thig
dang tshe lha rnam gsum gyi sgrub mchod sogs zhabs brtan gsol 'debs rgyas par zhus shing / nye gnas rnams la'ang bsgrub bya'i bslab ston gang shes zhus pa de nang rdor sems
yig brgya ci 'grub byas na legs/ gto tshogs sogs ni nged rang gi tshe la gto bca' ma myong bas dgos pa med tshul phebs pa ltar rdor sems snying po dung yon kha shas yar
mar dgon khag rnams la rgyeb chog dang / rje nyid kyi thugs bzhed ltar gzims chung phyi mar bla ma dpon slob kha shas nas mkha' 'gro'i tshogs skong dang me mchod grangs
mang bsgrubs pa sogs zhus/ skabs rer nye gnas la bi ma la mi tra bar snang la bzhugs 'dug /khyod nas e mjal ces pa tsam gsungs/ bsnyun zug che rigs gang yang med cing gsol
chas kyang thugs la gang babs res mos tshul gyis bzhes/ de rjes tsam zhig 'o ma bskol ba mchod zhal gang lhag tsam bzhes zin nas zas skom gyi gsol chas gang yang bzhes
par ma mdzad/ dbo zla ba'i dga' ba gnyis pa'i nang mo rgyun bstar gyi phyag bsil nas da las ka tshar ba red/ bca' lag phar khur gsungs/ me tog 'thor nas shis brjod shin
tu mang

po mdzad/ de rjes nas gsung gang yang ma byon par mnyam par bzhag bzhin pa'i ngang nyin phyed ma zin tsam la 'od gsal chos kyi dbyings su snyoms par zhugs so/ /de skabs kho
bo la'ang bya ma rta 'byor bas rings par bcar yang gang zag gzhan 'grel thugs dam gsal 'debs sogs zhu ba'i yul min cing 'dir snang sprul pa'i bkod pa bsdus pa'i de ma thag
slob dpon chen po bi ma la mi tra dang dgongs pa dbyer med bum pa chag pa'i nam mkha' dang phyi'i nam mkha' dbyer med du 'dres pa ltar gyur pa la sngon nas nges shes rnyed
zin pas mchod 'bul dang gsol 'debs thugs yid bsre ba'i mnyam bzhag gtso bor bgyis/ zhag gsum pa'i nyin spyi 'gre ltar chos sku las gzugs sku'i rnam par bzhengs par bskul
nas/ bla ma mchod pa'i rim pa gsol 'debs smon lam sogs yid tshim par zhus/ thar rtse mkhan rin po che 'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje yang phebs grub pa dang kho bo bcas
nas rnam 'joms dang sme brtsegs sogs kyis bsgrubs pa'i khrus chus sku gdung rin po che legs par bkrus/ dri bzang gi phur mas byugs/ gser sbyang gis bris pa'i gnas yig
gsar rnying gi rgyud sde gong 'og rnams las 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas sras gcig gi rgyud btags grol gyi glegs bam dang 'khor lo'i rigs mang po/ /bla ma dgongs 'dus rgyud
dgu sogs sku'i gnas rnams su phul/ ras dkar dri bzang gi chus bgos pas sku la dkris/ dbu rgyan thor tshugs stod g.yogs smad g.yogs gsol/ phyag tu rdo rje dang dril bu
phul te longs spyod rdzogs pa'i rnam pas gzims chung phyi ma'i nyin bzhugs kyi gdan la bzhugs su gsol/

mchod pa'i bye brag dang tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgyas par bshams nas nyin bdun tsam la mkhan rin po ches mkha' spyod ma dang / kho bos rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub mchod dang 'brel
ba'i bla ma mchod pa rgyas pa/ sngon gyi phyag gzhes ltar dbang skur len pa dang / slar yang dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo la dbang bzhes pa'i mos pas dbang bzhi phul cing /
tshogs mchod/ 'dod pa'i don la thugs rgyud skul ba'i gsol 'debs rnams gzabs rgyas su zhus/ rje rin po che nyid kyis rnam pa kun tu gsung 'phros phyis tshod bla ma rnams gdung
gog mchod rten du bzhag pa 'di ma 'ongs pa na bla ma de'i rus la gnod pa'i zhabs 'dren dang / gzhan dag la sdig pa gsog pa'i rkyen du 'gyur zhing / de ltar bzhag pa
des bla ma'i dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i thabs su'ang mi 'gyur la/ gson po rnams rang rang la bsod nams dang bsags pa zhig med phyin ro rul gyis phan btags pa'i bshad khungs gang
na'ang med pas shul gtsang byung na legs pa sogs rgyu mtshan mang du phebs pa ltar/ dbo zla ba'i gnam gang nyin gza' skar dge ba la mkhan rin po ches kye rdor/ dpon slob
rin po ches mkha' spyod ma/ kho bos smin gling rdor sems/ dgon gyi byang 'dren bla mas kun rig /so sor dpon slob mang tsam bcas dkyil 'khor bzhi'i sgo nas sku gdung rin
po che tsan dan dang a ga ru gtso bor gyur pa'i bzang shing gi me la bsreg bzhu phul/ de nyin me tog gi char yang shin tu mthug par babs/ zhag gsum du gdung khang rgyas
btab cing mchod 'bul phul/ de nas zhal phyes te cho ga bzhin gdung rus rnams bsdus nas 'thor zegs med par sbyangs btul zhus te dri med rnam gnyis kyi sAtstsha tshad ldan
btab

ste gdan sa'i gdung rten dang / lhun grub steng mchod sdong chen mo bcas la bzhugs su gsol bar bgyis so/ /de nas ji skad du/ 'dul ba lung las/ sA la'i shing la 'khri shing
bzhin/ /dam pa rnams ni bsten gyur pa/ /bzang po'i dpal gyis 'khyud par byed/ /ces dang / gang zhig gser gyi ri la brten bcas pa/ /de yis bya tshogs thams cad gser du 'gyur/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar/ lha dang bcas pa'i gtsug rgyan skyes bu dam pa las kyang dam pa chen po'i rnam thar bzang po'i tsan dan gyi tshal du sdong dum bzhin zhabs 'bring
du gnas pa dag kyang khyad par du gyur pa'i yon tan gyis mdza' ba chos nyid de/ rje nyid kyi sku dbon lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa'i dkyel che zhing ya rabs drwa ma'i rnam thar
phul du byung bas brgyan pa skal bzang rdo rje lags dang / phyi nang rig pa'i gnas kyi gtsug lag la dpyod pa'i blo mig padmo ltar rgyas pa/ rje btsun bla ma nyid kyi
sku dang grib ma'i tshul du 'bral ba med pas mnyes pa sgo gsum nas bsgrubs pa'i nye gnas chen po 'jam dbyangs legs pa'i blo gros dang / ring nas zhabs 'bring du 'khod cing
mnyes pa'i zhabs tog phul du phyin pa/ bslab gsum ldan pa'i dge slong dge ba'i bshes gnyen kun dga' rgyal mtshan gtso bor gyur pas gus shing dang ba'i blo gros dri ma med
pa dung dang kun da lta bus mtshams sbyar te rtag gus kyi brtson pa chen pos gshegs rjes dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i thabs rgya chen po bsgrubs pa'i tshul mdor bsdus par smos
na/ dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi lha rten khyad 'phags bla ma dge 'dun dang bcas par dgongs rdzogs mchod 'bul gtong ba rgya che'i mdzod sgo yangs por phyes pa las/

gangs can ston pa'i zhal skyin lha ldan jo shAka mched gsum mdun stong mchod dang 'brel ba'i dngos po rgya ma chung tsam gyi mchod 'bul dang / dpal gyi bsam yas sogs dbus gtsang
gi sgrub gnas lha rten yongs grags khyad 'phags rnams la gser gso snyan shal/ spos dang mar me'i phreng ba stong rtsa sogs rgyas bar spros te phul ba dang / phyag na
padmo gong sa rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa/ srid skyong de mo ho thog thu ste rtse shod so sor kha btags A she dang / rin chen gnyis pa/ bzang gos kha 'brel sogs babs
thob dang bstun pa'i 'bul mtshon/ gtsang paN chen rin po che/ dga' ldan khri rin po che/ sa skya khri chen rin po che sogs sa skya'i sku ngo gdung brgyud rin po che lhan
rgyas/ rgyal ba karma pa/ 'brug thams cad mkhyen pa'i mchog sprul/ karma pa'i rje dbon rnam gnyis/ stag lung ma rin po che/ rtse'i yongs 'dzin/ ngor e waM khang gsar/ zhabs
drung khag lnga/ thar rtse/ phan khang / klu sdings sogs ngor pa'i bla brang khag /rgyud stod smad mkhan po/ /shar rtse byang rtse/ mchims phu zung sprul/ zhwa lu sprul
sku gnyis/ lho brag thugs sprul/ rba kha sprul sku sogs la sku gsung thugs rten/ rin chen dang po dang gnyis pa'i dbyig nor/ dar gos sogs gang la gang 'os kyi mchod bsngo
dang / sa ngor gtsos/ rwa sgreng / zhwa lu/ bsam yas g.ya' ma lung / mchims phu/ gdan sa thel/ rtses dwangs/ sne'u gdong rtse tshogs/ yar lung shel brag /ras chung sbug
/lcags rtse gri gu/ lho brag smra'o cog /mkhar chu/ bkra shis lhun po/ stag lung sogs kyis mtshon pa'i dgon sde che phra'i dge 'dun 'dus pa/ ri khrod sgrub pa po bcas
la mang ja mchod 'bul yon 'bul rgya chen pos mnyes par

byas pa dang / mdo khams khul 'di'i bla ma dge 'dun la dgongs rdzogs mchod 'bul skul ba'ang / thog mar thar rtse mkhan chen nas dgung tshigs gnyis pa nas gsum pa'i bar kye
rdo rje'i sgrub mchod rdul tshon la brten pa'i sgo nas mchod 'bul zhus pa'i sku yon dgongs rdzogs su/ nang mdzod/ dngul gyi maNDal 'khor tshang / tshe dpag bod li/ grub chen
brgyad kyi zhal thang / 'jam dpal mtshan brjod sogs sum bid can/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ rgya gar chos 'byung / phyag dril dngul rtse can/ phyag phreng rgyan ldan
shin tu spus legs dngul srang drug cu 'gro ba/ dngul rkyang srang 'khor bdun cu don lnga/ mtha' dkar sogs rnam grangs brgya dang bcu gnyis la rgya srang sum brgya lnga
bcu'i babs/ thar rtse zhabs drung mdun nang mdzod/ sku gsung thugs rten/ dngul gyi maNDal 'khor tshang / rgya srang lnga bcu sogs rnam grangs so bdun la dngul srang brgya
re gsum babs/ gzhan sku 'khor las tshan so sor gang 'tshams kyi dngos po gya nom pa bstabs pa dang / e waM ngor thar rtse bla brang rang du gtan bzhag 'bul rgyu thub dbang
rgya gar shar li/ sgrol ljang bod li/ sku tshab padmA tsarYa/ rgyud sde lnga'i zhal thang / lam 'bras pod ser dmar sngo gsum/ tshul ljon dgongs rgyan pod gcig /klu sgrub
dang ngag chos lam 'bras pod gnyis/ ngag chos 'bel gtam pod gcig /dam pa'i mkhyud dpyad pod gcig /sgrub thabs kun btus pod bcu gcig 'khar gsil lnga/ sba lcag byin can/
rnal 'byor ma'i phyag mtshan rdo rje'i kha TAM ga gser dngul bkra ma/ gu ru nyi ma 'od zer phyag mtshan li ser rdo rje/ dngul bum 'khor tshang cha/ rdo dril gsar bskrun
gser rtse can spus legs nyer lnga/ tshe bum shin tu khyad nam can/ dbu rgyan rigs

lnga skyo 'bur gser shog can cha nyer lnga/ de 'brel rtsa chings/ dar dpyang cha nyer lnga re/ stegs khebs rab 'bring nyer lnga/ gser dngul bkra ma'i spos phor che legs cha/
gser dngul bkra ma'i rgya gling legs pa cha/ dung ser dngul rgyan can/ rkang gling gser dngul bkra ma phra rgyan can spus legs/ gser dngul bkra ma'i mchod gzhong sogs 'bor
bsdoms dngul rdel tshad nyer lnga'i babs phul/ de bzhin phan khang mkhan rin po che'i mdun dgung zhag rdzogs par kye rdor sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i yon du nang mdzod/ tshe
dpag med gser sku/ nye sras sum thang / tshe dpag med brgya sku/ jo bo'i chos chung / rdo dril rnying ma gser rtse can/ gser dngul bkra ma'i nang mchod/ gsol ltir spus
legs/ rgya dngul gar bu rdel tshad/ mtha' dkar sogs rnam grangs mtshan bzang so gnyis dang bcu gsum sa'i grangs ldan la rgya srang nyis brgya nyer lnga'i bab thob/ bla mchan
sogs las tshan la'ang de mtshungs smar zong gi dngos po 'os bstun bcas phul/ thar rtse dpon slob/ dbal spungs dbon rgan/ nyi grags mchog sprul/ dge mang sku zhabs/ dpal
yul karma 'gyur med sprul sku/ sku zhabs khams sprul/ nang chen phur bla dang / brag g.yabs gtsang sar sprul sku/ dza ka sprul sku rin po che sogs kyis gsar rnying rgyud
sde bka' gter gyi dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo lhag pa'i lha dang bla ma dbyer med du sgrub cing mchod la dbang blangs pa'i tshul gyis dngos grub rnam gnyis bde blag tu sgrub
pa'i lam zab mo la nye bar gzhol ba'i legs 'bul dar gos rin chen/ pags rigs/ ther phrug /rta drel sogs dngos po sbus nam ldan cing sbom mtho ba'i yon bstabs pas dgyes
par byas/ gzhan yang dpal spungs tA'i si tu'i mchog sprul mdun lha rdzas/ rten gsum/ dngul gyi mchod chas cha tshang / rje dbon rnam

gnyis/ dpal yul rgya sprul rin po che/ kaHthog zhing skyong / si tu/ rdzogs chen rin po che/ zhe chen rab 'byams/ rgyal tshab/ rgya rong dbon sprul/ gling rje drung sogs gsar
rnying gi bla ma che rgu rnams la mchod bsngo'i rten sku gsung thugs kyi rten mchog /sku chas mchod chas mtshon pa'i nyer spyad/ dar gos/ rin chen sogs dngos po nam ldan
spus gtsang rgya che'i mchod 'bul spros pa sogs rnam grangs ming nas smos kyis mi longs pa dang / kho bo cag la'ang rten gsum khyad can rigs gtsos sbam mtho ba'i dgongs
rdzogs skul byed bstabs shing / dgon sde rnams su'ang / lhun grub steng du dngul srang brgya tham pa'i babs/ rdzong sar grwa mang 'dus par dngul srang nyer lnga/ spyi chen
par dngul srang nyer lnga/ spyi chung khag gnyis la bzhi ru re bcas la he ru ka'i yig brgya dang / thugs rje chen po'i yig drug yon du phul/ dpal spungs dngul srang brgyad
cu yig brgya dang smon lam rnam lnga'i yon dang / sgrub sde gong 'og tu'ang babs 'os re/ rdzogs chen dgon pa'i 'dus sder dngul srang nyer lnga'i babs/ zhe chen dngul
bzhi ru'i babs/ kaHdpal gnyis su'ang de bzhin/ 'dzing stag mo sgang / sbra mtho/ spom 'dzang / khang dmar mdo rnams kyi 'dus sde so sor dngul srang bcu re'i babs yig drug
dang smon lam rten/ bon dgon lcang lung du dngul srang brgyad babs phul ba sogs ris bral gsar rnying bon gsum gyi chos sde dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja'i dod kyi
bsnyen 'bul dngos rdzas bzang dgu ser sna sogs kyi dri mas ma sbags par rje btsun bla ma'i zab dgongs 'od gsal mi slob pa'i lam du yongs su rdzogs pa'i gsol gdab thugs
rgyud yang dag par skul ba'i thabs rgya chen por 'jug pa ste/ rgyas par brjod na dge ba ngoms pa'i skyon dang yi ge mang gis dogs pas rags bsdus de tsam dang /

gzims mal du 'dra sku sman 'dam las bzhengs pa/ dgongs bzhed byams sku mtho bco lnga pa dngul rdil tshad nyer lnga tsam gyis gsar bskrun dgon chen du bzhugs pa dang / chos
sku'i rten mchog tu rje nyid kyi gdung tsha sogs bzhugs pa'i mchod sdong mtho dgu lhag tsam zangs shas gser spus gnyis ka ci mthug /phra rgyan gyi bkod pa rin thang gang
che thams cad rtsal sbrugs/ sgros cha chags tshad sogs gzabs rgyu gang yod kyis shin tu spus nam dag cing mig gi bdud rtsir gyur pa rgya dngul rdil tshad so bdun tsam gyi
rgyu chas kyis bskrun cing dri med rnam gnyis kyi srog shing 'dzugs chog /gdung rus tsha sgrub sogs gzhung mthun gyis mtshon/ ring bsrel rnam bzhi sogs rten mchog khyad
'phags kyis gtams te ye shes sems dpa' dngos su bstim pa'i bkra shis rab gnas kyi cho ga tshad dang ldan pa bcas kyis mthong grol chen mor bzhugs pa dang / longs sku'i rten
'jam dpal chos dbyings gsung dbang li dmar gser dngul bkra ma'i rgyan can dngul rdil tshad gsum lhag tsam gyis gsar bskrun mdzad pa'i bzhed pa thugs bcangs dang / sprul
sku'i rten bdag cag gi ston pa'i snang brnyan jo bo shAkya mu ni'i sku tshad dang / rje btsun bla ma nyid kyi 'dra zhal mtho bcu pa byon legs gnyis la dngul rdil tshad
nyer bdun tsam/ gzhan sangs rgyas byang sems nyan thos kyi 'khor gser sku bdun cu skor/ gsung rten pusti grangs mang / gdung rten bzhugs khang bang ba nang 'dam lnga sgo
khang bcas/ de nang mchod cha yo byad mkho tshang / mar me'i rgyun 'dzugs bcas bsam pa dag cing sbyor ba gus pa chen pos brtson pa lhur blangs te bla ma mnyes pa'i bgyi ba
dam pas bsngags shing chos dang mthun pa'i bya ba rlabs su che ba gegs med mthar phyin gyis dgongs rdzogs rjes sgrub kyi rim pa mtha' rgyas bsgrubs dang sgrub bzhin pas
shin tu dge legs su byas pa'o// //

gnyis pa gang zag gzhan dang thun mong ma yin pa rje nyid kho na'i khyad par gyi chos su gyur pa nang gi rnam par thar pa ni/ gangs can ljongs kyi bstan 'dzin phal mo che rang
rang lugs su mkhas shing grub pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar bas bstan pa skyong zhing 'gro phan sgrub pas dad cing gus par bya ba'i yul kho na las ma 'das mod/ mdo sngags
kyi bstan pa phyogs thams cad nas gsan bsam sgom pa mdzad cing ris su ma chad pa'i bstan pa spel cing gdul bya skyong ba ni rje thams cad mkhyen pa 'di nyid kyi khyad par
gyi chos su grub pa ste/ de'ang rig pa'i gnas dang sde snod gsum gyi mdzad pa'i rnam thar mdo tsam gong du song ba las shes/ 'dir mkhas grub chen po pradznyA ra smis/ rgyal
bas lung bstan gangs can 'gro ba'i mgon/ /gcig tu bstan pa 'ba' zhig nyer dgongs pa'i/ /sngon gyi chos rgyal lha gcig btsan po de/ /gangs ri'i khrod 'dir ston pa gnyis
pa yin/ /zhu chen lo tsA ba gor bai ro dang / /rgyal ba'i gdung 'tshob 'brom ston u pa sI/ /mkhas grub chen po khyung po rnal 'byor pa/ /skad gnyis smra ba bla chen 'brog
mi dang / /rnal 'byor dbang phyug rje btsun mar pa'i zhabs/ /grub pa'i sar bzhugs dam pa rgya gar dang / /ji gyo lo tsA mkhas grub o rgyan pa/ /byang phyogs sgrub brgyud
'degs pa'i ka chen brgyad/ /dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang nas legs 'ongs pa'i/ /gangs ri'i khrod 'dir sgrub brgyud srol chen brgyad/ /de dag grub thob gong ma'i gshegs shul
yin/ /thar 'dod rnams kyang lam de'i rjes su zhugs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ byang phyogs gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir lo paN sprul pa'i skyes mchog rnams kyi bka' drin las legs
par byon cing /

de dag thugs nyams su bzhes pas grub pa'i 'bras bu mngon du mdzad nas/ dam pa'i skyes bu re res kyang gdul bya grangs med pa byang chub chen po'i go 'phang du dbugs dbyung
bar mdzad pa sgrub brgyud shing rta chen po brgyad kyi ring lugs 'dzin pa dbus gtsang mdo khams rnams su gang bzhugs rtsad gcod mdzad/ 'phags yul paN grub rnams kyi rtsa
ba'i srol 'byed dang / rang gis gsan yul de yid ches pa byung phyin bar gyi brgyud pa yod pa tsam gyis chog par mdzad pa'i phyag srol ltar/ so so'i chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i
yongs 'dzin dang gdams ngag tshol ba la sku ngal khyad du bsad de 'bad rtsol chen pos don gnyer mdzad/ gzhung gdams man ngag gi dpe tshad ldan che phra mang nyung ci zhig
yod kyang gsar bzhengs mdzad nas/ 'ga' zhig lan grangs mang po/ phal cher tshar re ma 'chad pa med pas dbang khrid man ngag gi rgyun chad par nye ba thams cad snod dang
'tshams par 'chad spel sgom sgrub la sbyar nas bstan pa'i srog rtsa mthud par mdzad pa ste/ de'ang so so'i ring brgyud bar ma chad par bzhugs so cog gsan pa gzhir bzhag
/nye brgyud kyi bka' babs byung ba'i tshul ni/ dang po mkhan slob chos gsum gyi bka' drin las byung ba snga 'gyur rnying ma la/ thog mar dgung lo nyer bzhi chu yos sa ga
zla ba'i tshes drug gi nyin shangs mdo sram pa sgrub khang gi dpal chen po mjal zhing tshogs mchod mdzad pa'i tshe/ nyams kyi snang bar dpal chen po dngos su mjal/ sgo gong
du zur yab sras gnyis bzhad gad theg ger bzhugs nas ru lu'i sngags kyi dbang / badzra sa twa'i rgyud bshad/ hU~M yig gi man ngag gnang ba'i nyams snang ches gsal zhing
brtan par byung bas sgyu 'phrul gsang ba snying po'i nye brgyud thob/

dgung lo so brgyad pa me sbrul lor ru dam bsam gtan gling gi mkhan po rdo rje 'dzin pa padma badzra las 'dus pa mdo'i dbang gsan skabs/ dbang dngos gzhi'i skabs su dkyil 'khor
yongs rdzogs kyi gsal snang brtan po shar/ de nub mnal lam du lung pa zhig nas gyen du phebs pas ri rtser sgrub khang dkar po zhig snang / de la gtad nas phebs te nang
du phyin pas phug tu ras yol btang ba'i mdun tu gtor mchod sha khrag gi dri ya nga ba bshams/ zur der sngags pa ral pa can zil can zhig gis raksha'i phreng ba bgrang /
rnga zhig brdungs nas 'don pa byed mur 'dug pa la khyod su yin gsungs pas lan ma ster/ slar yang khyod su yin ces hur por gsungs pas rnga de drag brdung zhig byas nas/ byang
chub sems kyi rnga chen 'di brdungs pas/ /pho nya sum brgya drug cu 'dir 'dus shig /ces drag por gsungs pas yol ba de'i phag nas pho nya sum brgya drug cu yin snyam pa'i
mtshon cha thogs pa mang po 'khrab cing byung ste nyid kyi sku lus dum bu brgya stong mang por gtubs song ba la 'jigs skrag na tsha sogs gang yang med pa'i rang bzhin
ltad mo bltas pa 'dra ba zhig gi rjes su rdo rje sems dpa'i sku 'od lam mer yod pa zhig tu gyur nas/ sngags pa de so ye shes dbang phyug dang 'dus mdo'i smin grol dus gcig
la rdzogs pa'i nyams snang byung bas 'dus pa mdo'i nye brgyud thob/ mkhan po nyid kyang ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul yin gsungs pa 'di rigs phal cher
rtsar gsum sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i lung byang du'ang gsal cha yod par 'dug /dgung lo bcu drug pa shing lug sa ga zla ba'i tshes brgyad la mnal lam du/ rgya gar gyi yul spang

ljongs sman gyi nags tshal sogs ches yid du 'ong ba zhig tu phebs pa na rdo rje gdan gyi ke'u tshang rim dgu'ang zer/ dha he na'i 'du khang yin snyam byed pa'i mchod rten gyi
rnam pa lta bu'i lha khang dgu brtsegs gser gyi rgya phib sogs bkod pa blo las 'das pa zhig gi nang du bud med cig gis lam sna byas te rim par phebs pa'i rtsag 'og ma
rnams su paN grub phyag dpe thogs shing 'chad pa dang / sku brnyan sogs mang po bzhugs snyam byed pa las zhib par ma rtogs/ rim pa brgyad pa der phebs pa na slob dpon 'jam
dpal bshes gnyen paNDi ta'i cha lugs can gyi sku'i g.yas g.yon du glegs bam mang po brtsegs pa zhig mjal ba la gus pa chen pos btud cing gsol gdab mdzad pas/ g.yon phyogs
nas glegs bam zhig blangs te bstan pa sher phyin sdud pa'i rgya dper 'dug /de nyid dbur bzhag nas dgongs pa gtad de mtshan nyid kyi chos thams cad kyi bka' lung rdzogs
pa yin no gsungs/ g.yas phyogs nas shog bu dung mdog la bod yig tu bris pa'i glegs bam zhig blangs nas bstan pa rdo rje sems dpa' snying gi me long gi rgyud ces bya bar
snang / de nyid dbur bzhag nas dgongs pa gtad de gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i tshul spyi dang khyad par rdzogs pa chen po sde gsum gyi tshig don byin rlabs thams cad rdzogs
pa yin no gsungs/ lung bstan 'ga' zhig kyang mdzad pa'i mthar dgyes pa'i tshul gyis 'od du zhu nas rje nyid la thim pas dar cig rnam par mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin
la 'byams/ de sad nas phyir phebs lam rtsag 'og ma rnams su grub thob/ paN chen/ sgom pa dang / bshad pa dang / gzim pa po mang du bzhugs pa rnams sems sde'i mkhas pa nyer
gcig sogs yin snyam byed pa las byin rlabs

so sor zhus nas sgor phebs pa'i tshe/ gtsug lag khang gi sgo der bud shing sogs med pa'i me chen po zhig 'bar zhing 'dug pa la/ 'dir bsreg dgos snyam pa zhig gi ngang me der
zhugs pas gdos bcas kyi phyi nang thams cad tshigs pa'i rjes su snang ba de dag 'gags nas lus 'od lus bi ma mi tra yin snyam pa dang sems bde stong zag med kyi ye shes
mu mtha' med pa la 'byams pa'i ngang du mnal las sad pa na nyams de zhag kha shas kyi bar du ma yal bar byung bas rdzogs chen sems sde'i nye brgyud kyang thob/ dgung lo so
gsum pa chu byi zla ba bcu pa'i nang rdzong gsar bkra shis lha rtse'i rje nyid kyi bzhugs gnas su kho bos gsol ba btab pa'i ngor klong sde rdo rje zam pa'i dbang lung khrid
bcas stsal ba'i sgom tshul bla ma'i byin rlabs kyi nub mo mnal lam du wa seng ge brag yin snyam pa'i stod la brag dkar shug pa'i nang yod pa/ dkyil spang ri yin pa'i
mthil du brag dkar khyi tshugs bcas pa 'dra ba yod pa'i brag rtser spang mi pham mgon po'i sku 'bum yin rgyu'i sa 'bum lta bu zhig 'dug pa la dad gus kyis bskor ba mdzad
pas sa sku lta bur song / mthar bgres po phying thul can/ sgom shing g.yon du brten/ tshul shing mdun du bzhag pa can zhig tu gyur pa la gsol 'debs mang du mdzad pas yun
gcig nas tshur gzigs te brda bzhi bstan byung bas klong sde'i smin grol tshang bar thob pa'i nges shes skyes pa ni rdzogs chen klong sde'i bka' babs brnyes pa'o/ /dgung
lo nyer gcig lcags byi snron zlar gzho stod ti sgro brag dkar du phebs skabs spyir gnas kyi byin rlabs lta bus thugs snang 'gyur nas kun rtog gi ri mo dag pa'i snang ba 'ba'
zhig tu shar ba dang / tshogs khang chen

mor tshogs mchod mdzad pa'i skabs cung zad mnal du song ba na/ o rgyan yab yum gnyis kyis mkha' 'gro snying thig gi dbang lung khrid gsum yud tsam la rdzogs par stsal ba'i
dag snang shar/ yang lo de ka'i sa zla phyi ma'i bco lnga skor gangs ri thod dkar du gnas 'brel mdzad skabs/ dag pa'i snang bar klong chen pa'i ye shes kyi skus phyag dbu
la bkod nas/ bu zhes pa'i gsung gis dbugs dbyung stsal/ bla sgrub thig le'i rgya can gyi dbang bskur sogs kyang thugs gter du brdol nas yi ger bkod par mdzad sbyar byang
'ga' zhig tu kun mkhyen bla ma dgyes pa'i 'bangs zhes pa'ang de la dgongs pa yin gsungs/ mnal lam du kun mkhyen pas mkha' 'gro yang tig gi byin rlabs bla ma sgrub pa'i dbang
dang khrid bcas gnang ba dang / gdung rus lta bu'i sku brnyan zhig kyang phug pa de nas phyag tu son pas rdzogs chen man ngag sde padma'i lugs kyi bka' babs thob/ dgung
lo nyer bzhi chu yos sa zla'i tshes bcu gsum nyin 'o yug sding ma'i lam du phebs pa'i chibs thog tu/ thog mar snang yul thams cad 'od dmar ser gyis khyab pas tha mal
gyi rtog pa 'gags te phyi gong rdza'i ra bar phebs nas lce btsun seng ge dbang phyug la mkha' 'gro mang pos bskor ba'i gral du 'khod/ 'das rjes zhal chems kyi tshul du lce
btsun snying thig bka' stsal ba'i sngon gnas rjes su dran/ mkha' 'gro ma dpal gyi blo gros kyis byin gyis brlabs pas tshig don thams cad phyis yun ring mo song yang mi
brjed par bkra lam mer thugs la gnas par byung ba ni man ngag sde bi ma'i lugs kyi bka' babs brnyes pa'o/ /gnyis pa jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha'i bka' srol las byon pa'i
bka' gdams

kyi bka' babs nye brgyud brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ spyir 'brom ston gyi gdan sa rwa sgreng du snga rjes lan bzhir phebs pa la/ nam phebs dus thugs snang 'gyur ba'i byin rlabs chen
po'i nges shes rnyed pa dang / lhag par dgung lo nyer bzhi chu yos snron zla'i tshes brgyad la jo bo 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / jo bo'i 'dra thang dbu yon mjal skabs de
dang de dngos su mjal ba'i dag snang gsal bas/ de skor sbyar dug dogs pa'i bsnyun khams lci ba zhig yod pa'ang skad cig gis dwangs pa'i ngo mtshar chen po byung / dgung

par gtad pa'i gsal snang byung ba la de dang mthun pa'i gsung mgur mdzad pa'ang mgur pod du bzhugs so/ /gsum pa grub chen bi rU pa'i bka' srol gdams ngag lam 'bras bu

'dra sku mjal skabs sku brnyan de nyid tshar chen dngos su snang bas byin gyis brlabs par shar/ mu gu lung gi sgra bsgyur rgya gar phug tu lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhig
nyams bzhes mdzad skabs cung zad mnal du song bar/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba sku'i rnam pa ha cang mi gsal tsam zhig gis glegs bam zhig dbu thog tu bzhag nas/ rgyud kyi bshad

tshes bcu bzhir mnal lam du/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po sku shin tu gsal bar mjal ba'i sku 'od kyi rang bzhin gyi thugs ka'i dbus su 'od kyi gang bu shel sngon po'i mchod rten
dbyibs lta bu'i stod kyi char yang dag lha dgu/ bar du dgyes rdor lha dgu/ 'og gi char phur pa gtso rkyang bcas sku dngos dang mtshungs par gsal ba'i bla ma yi dam dbyer
med kyi zhal nas yang phur dang / lam 'bras kyi bskyed rdzogs snying po khyad par can stsal ba gsan/ bzhi pa mnga' bdag mar pa'i bka' brgyud kyi bka' babs brnyes pa'i
tshul ni/ dgung lo nyer gcig lcags byi lo'i zla ba dgu par lho brag gsas mkhar dgu thog tu mar pa lo tsA'i sku 'dra rin po che mjal skabs mar pa dngos kyi dag snang shar/
de nub mnal lam du mar pa yin snyam pa la sku dngos mi gsal ba zhig gis/ dngos po'i gnas lugs lam dang ni/ 'bras bu skye ba'i rim pa'o/ /zhes ye shes mkha' 'gro'i rdo rje'i
tshig rkang la gsung bshad mdzad pa gsan/ dgung lo nyer dgu sa sprel dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes nyer lngar gzhung spre zhing du phebs lam chibs thog nas yengs ma lam lta
bu'i skabs/ mnga' bdag mar pa sku dar yol zhig mdun mkhar bzhugs nas rgyud dang gdams ngag gi snying po shlo ka gcig gsungs/ rngog chos sku rdo rje yin pa'i gsal snang lam

po res rkyen byas

/zhes gsungs te 'khor dang bcas pa rje nyid la thim pas thugs yid dbyer med du 'dres pa'i nyams shar te de phyin chad ka dag gi gnas lugs la rang bzhin gyis brtan pa thob

pa la/ sgom rim

nas dbye mi chog par bzhag /slar lo gcig song rjes bltas pas phar bzhag dus dang 'dra bar bzhugs shing / der yud tsam gyi snang ba las ma byung tshul gsungs pas/ rgya
nag rgyal po 'khor bcas sngags par dad nas bkur bzos rgya chen po dang bcas te slar bod du phebs pas sngags pa rnams la phan chen po thogs pa de yin zhing / de dus kyi
gnas skabs rnams dran gsungs nas de'i gnad kas mi pham rang la 'byed rnam gnyis kyi bshad lung zhig stsal ba thos/ yang me yos zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gsum la rje rin
po ches mdzad pa'i bde mchog rgyud 'grel sbas don kun gsal steng nas rgyud bshad zhus pa dang po tshugs pa'i nub mo mnal lam du/ sku lus las mi gtsang ba dang / bu ga rnams
las khrag rnag mtha' yas pa zhig zag /sku lus dri ma med cing shin tu yang ba gshog pa dang ldan pa zhig tu gyur pas 'phur nas phyin pas rgya gar lho phyogs zhig tu phebs/
der thang yangs pa zhig gi mthar brag dang nags tshal yod pa'i ri bo zhig dang nye bar 'dug pa la gzigs pas/ ri mgul der grub chen lU hi pa yin zer ba'i rnal 'byor
pa zhig

zhal phar phyogs te khog ma la me 'bud nas tshod ma btso ba ltar snang / ri de'i gsham nas bdag la dngos grub cig stsol ces 'ga' zhig bos pas zhal tshur gzigs pa na nyi ma
lta bu'i gzi brjid shin tu bzod dka' ba zhig snang / slar yang bos pas mdun gyi me de dmar thar thar drag tu gtor byung ba'i gseb tu nyungs ma bsregs pa'i rdog po zhig snang
ba kha phyes ba'i nang du shing tog las grub pa lta bu'i 'khor lo bde mchog gi sku brnyan ser smug ches legs pa zhig 'dug pa zhal du gsol pas sku lus dang dbyer med du
'dres pa'i bde bas gang ba lta bu'i ngang nas sad pa na 'khor lo bde mchog gi byin rlabs yongs rdzogs thob pa'i nges shes 'khrungs/ shab bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims
