kyi sngon gnas rab tsam gsal zhing / mnga' ris paN chen rin po che'i bag chags 'al 'ol 'char ba na de dag gi skabs su sgrub brgyud brgyad kyi lam srol rnams dka' ba du mas
btsal ba dran pa na dga' ba dang skyo ba 'dres pa'i nyams ci rigs 'char bar snang gsungs/ rje rin po che tsong kha pa'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis dang ba'i yid rgyun chags
su 'byung zhing / jo nang rje btsun rin po cher mos gus thun mong ma yin pa rgyun chags pa la brten/ yang dang yang du mjal ba dang / skabs shig khong gis bzhes ma grub
pa'i gter chos phreng ba skor bzhi las lta ba'i phreng ba gzhi rgyud/ rnam shes phreng ba skyed rim/ ye shes phreng ba rdzogs rim/ las kyi phreng ba sgrub chen dang las
phran skor sogs yin pa'i gsungs bshad mdor bsdus gnang / de rnams kyi gter dpe zab pu lung gi rdza mo hU~M 'drar yod pa ma 'ongs pa'i dus su spyod par gyis shig pa'i rjes
gnang yang stsal gsungs so/ /gnyis pa sa gter gyi bka'

babs tshul ni/ dgung lo chung ngu'i dus nas gter gyi lung bstan mang du byung 'dug kyang rten 'brel gzhan dbang du song / dbyar ru nang bzhugs skabs gnas ri yin pa'i brag zhig
nas rdo gru bzhi la brda yig yod pa zhig rnyed pa rtsa gsum bde gshegs 'dus pa'i chos skor yin 'dug pa las byang ldeb lnga bcu tsam phab/ rdo rang mal du rgyas gdab/
las byang de phyis bar phyag tu bzhugs kyang phyis byon thugs sgrub rnam gsum gcig dril lta bu'i lha sngags thams cad rnam pa gcig pa kho nar snang bas dpe mi mngon dbyings
su rgyas btab pa yin gsungs/ dgung lo nyer dgu sa sprel dbyug pa zla bar lha ldan nas bsam yas phyogs su phebs pa'i tshes bcu'i nang mor nye gnas pa sngon du song / sku
nyid rkyang pa brag dmar mgrin bzang lha khang mjal du phebs pa na nye skor der bud med cig gis lha chen 'jig song ba'i phyag mdzub cig phul byung ba sku 'phrag tu btsud
nas phebs/ bar der yod pa tsam yang ma dran/ phyis zhig na bza' yang brje skabs sku chings bkrol bas thang du lhung song ba ci yod gzigs 'dod pa zhig byung nas mdzul mo
bcags pas/ nang du thugs rje chen po sems nyid ngal gso'i chos skor dang / dri med kun dag sa yang gter du sbas pa'i bla rdzogs thugs gsum gyi snying po gcig dril rnams
kyi shog ser/ bram ze nyer gcig gi gdung rnams byon kyang rlung phyogs tsam yang ma bsgrags pas nye gnas tshul khrims rgya mtsho zhabs tog pa rgyun gcar yin rung gter bzhes
pa'i phyogs tsam yang ma rtogs/ sems nyid ngal gso'i nyams bzhes khyug tsam re gnang / phyis sa pho rta lo dgun zla 'bring po'i tshes bcur ye shes mkha'

'gro'i sku la byang la brten/ lo rgyus gnad byang dang yang byang tsam gtan la phab par mdzad/ lo rgyus gnad byang las/ thog mar chos 'di'i sgo 'byed pa: dbang gi gnas su dbang
gi dus: dbang chen padma'i rigs skyes pa'i: rnam 'phrul zung gi don du ston: tshom bu dang bcas skal bzang 'gyur: ces gsungs pa ltar/ lcags sbrel snron zla bar rgyal
dbang karma pa bcu bzhi pa nyag sked dpon gyis gdan zhus la phebs pa'i yar lam chu stod zla bar gter lhung phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur/ kho bo la snga ma nas 'di don zur
tsam bka' stsal phebs pa dang 'di skabs rje bla ma nyid kyang zla gam dbang phug tu phebs 'dug pas rgyal dbang rin po cher yang mtshams sbyor snyan gsan gang drag zhus pas/
zla gam dbang phug tu gnas mjal phebs nas dgongs par gang babs kyi dbang zhig gnang grub par zhu rgyu mdzad song bas/ rje rin po che yang thugs dgyes pa chen pos rgyal
dbang rin po che/ si tu sprul pa'i sku gtsos bdag cag 'dus pa brgyad la sems nyid ngal gso'i don dbang / mtsho skyes snying thig gi rtsa dbang / lce btsun snying thig gi
dbang bcas rje nyid kyi zab gter las byon pa'i bla rdzogs thugs gsum tshang bar mdzad nas bka' drin tu stsal ba thob pas ches skal pa bzang por gyur cing / thog mar rten
'brel legs par 'grigs/ chos 'di'i cha lag gnas der bzhugs yod par snang ba'ang phyag tu son par nges kyang sa gter gyi rtsa ba'i rten 'brel thog mar 'chugs pa'i dbang gis
sa gter la brten pa'i shog ser rigs gzigs pa tsam gyis kyang thugs ches bsnyun pa ma zad shog ser gyi lab gleng tsam yang zhu dka' ba dang / de'i gnad kyis chos bka' phal
cher mgo mthong tsam las cha lag tshang ba gtan la 'bebs thub

pa gtan nas ma byung / 'di'i rgyun khyer cig zhus pa rtsom mi dgos/ shog ser la yod gsungs nas 'bebs pa rtsom pa na 'phral der phyag la bsnyun khams tshabs po ches thebs pa
bcas chos bka' gtan la 'bebs ma thub pa ni/ spyir gdul bya phal mo che skal ba dman pa'i steng thog ma nas yid gnyis zhugs pa'i dam sel gyi grib dang / khyad par chos bka'
'di nyid zhal phyes pa tsam gyis kla klo'i nyer 'tshe phyir bsring ba yin 'dug pas de lta bu gangs can pa'i bsod nams kyi skal bar ma shong bar zad do/ /dgung lo so gcig
par g.yo ru khra 'brug nas lung bstan gyi nges pa gzigs pa bzhin/ dpal chen chu bo ri'i gu ru'i sgrub phug nam mkha' lding du bod khams bde thabs kyi phrin las mdzad pas/
gu ru bde ba chen po gtso 'khor grangs med pas nam mkha' khengs te sprul pa mtha' yas pas bod khams dbugs 'byin stsal pa dang / lo skor gcig gi bar du bod yul dbus su
mtha' dmag gi 'jigs pa mi 'byung ba'i mtshan ma khyad par can brnyes/ de'i phyi lor rgyang yon po lung gi gu ru'i sgrub phug tu tshogs mchod mdzad pa'i tshe de'i sgo gong
du gu ru'i sku tshab dang bsam pa lhun grub ma'i chos skor bzhugs pa gsal bar gzigs shing chos kyi rnam grangs sogs ji lta bar thugs la shar/ slar dgung lo so dgu pa sa
pho rta lo dbo zla ba'i tshes bcu'i tho rangs su nam mkha' nas thod phreng rtsal gyi dzapra dbyangs shig grags pa'i rjes thog tu/ spyan nas 'od zer gyi sbu gu phra la g.yel
ba zhig lho rgyud kyi phyogs g.yas g.yon nas chu bo 'babs pa'i brag ri zhig gis 'dabs su zug /der gu ru'i sku tshab bde ba chen po'i rnam pa khru

gang pa dang / chos skor rnams shog ser glegs bam chen po'i rnam pa mngon sum lta bur gzigs pa la/ thugs rtog zhib tu bcug pas sku dang shog ser da lta'i tshad ci lta ba la/
de na gang bzhugs kyi chos kyi tshig don lam lam thugs la gsal ba zhig byung yang / gnas dus sogs kyi rten 'brel dang dgos pa'i dbang gzhan gzigs nas rje nyid kyis 'don
par skabs su ma babs pas/ gter chen mchog gyur gling pa la rgyu mtshan dang bcas te 'don par bskul bas/ gter chen nyid la'ang lung bstan dang gsal snang khyad par can gyis
mtshams sbyar te/ sa rta smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu la rtsi rke'i chu bo 'dus pa'i nor bu spun gsum gyi brag nas sku tshab dngos grub dpal 'bar dang / chos skor shog
ser/ don kun 'grub pa'i gi waM gi bam po bcas tshegs med par dngos grub tu bzhes/ shog ser la brda yig dngos su mi gsal yang yab sras zhal rgyas pa'i thog gter sgrub zhag
bdun mdzad cing bdud rtsi lnga'i chu la sbangs pas zhag po lnga nas brda yig gi grong khyer bdun bkra lam gyis shar ba'i ngo mtshar chen po dang bcas/ mgo zla'i tshes bcur
lhan rgyas kyis gtan la phab pas/ gter chen rin po ches ji ltar gsungs pa dang mthun par rje bla ma la'ang gsal snang nges pa can shar bas gcig la gcig thugs yid ches
nas 'khrul pa dang bral bar gtan la pheb/ de'i phyi lor kun mkhyen bla ma gtso 'khor gyis thugs sgrub rnam gnyis zung 'brel gyi tshom bu tshogs sgrub mdzad pa'i tshe na'ang
/ gzhal med khang rgya khyon bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbus su/ thugs sgrub gnyis kyi lha tshogs steng 'og lta bur mngon sum bzhin

bzhugs pa'i gtso bo'i zhal nas gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa gsungs shing / khyad par gsol 'debs tshul bzhi'i sgo nas 'chad pa'i man ngag stsal ba dang / gter srung so sos
kyang phrin las sgrub pa'i gsal snang khyad par can gzigs/ sku tshabarin po che thugs dam rten du bzhugs shing / thugs sgrub yid bzhin nor bu'i sku rten gser zangs las
grub pa padma shel phug tu bzhugs/ chos kyi phrin las kyang spel bar mdzad mod/ zhal gdams snying byang chos tshan bcu gsum skor rnams rten 'brel gnad cig gis spel bar ma
gnang ngo / /dgung grangs zhe drug pa me stag lo'i zla ba dang po'i nub gcig gi tho rangs khar rnga yab gling nas 'ongs pa yin zer ba'i dpa' bo'i chas can gnyis byung nas
'di lo skor snga ma shing stag lo la dus tshod dngos yin kyang rten 'brel ma 'grigs/ da lan gu ru rin po che'i bkas khyed la sprod du phyin pa yin zer/ shog dril zhig
sprad nas mi snang bar gyur/ shog dril de mdun du nas bzed nang du bcug na ma gsal nas gzigs pas gter gyi kha byang du 'dug pa ltar lo de'i zla ba bcu pa'i nang gter chen
mchog gyur gling pa dang lhan rgyas rong me dkar mo stag tshang du phebs/ gnas zhal gsar du 'byed par mdzad/ mchog gling nas kyang gnam lcags rdo rje dang dam chos snying
po skor lnga bzhes/ rje nyid kyi gnas mdun brag dkar nas thugs sgrub rdo rje drag rtsal gyi sku rten bzhes/ si ngu g.yu mtshor dar chags pa mtsho dkyil 'khyag pa brtibs
nas rnam pa gnyis kas tshogs skong gser skyems phul/ bka' bsgo mdzad nas mtsho dkyil du lding thag 'phangs bar lan gnyis la ma byung / de nas

gter srung klu'i rgyal po gser gyi gdugs bcas 'ong ba'i gzigs snang byung ba dang lhan cig mtsho phyur nas gser phye nyil gyis byung ba'i skabs lding thag khud du gter sgrom
'byon/ rje bla mas mtsho nang nas gser sgrom zhig bzhes pa he ru ka zhal sbyor gyi rnam par bzhugs pa zhig byon/ de skabs yod pa'i grwa 'khor gzhan rnams kyis bye ma'i
nang nas gser phran tshegs rnyed/ de rjes ni gser rnams gar song med 'dug /gter sgrom nas thugs sgrub rdo rje drag rtsal dang / rtsa gsum sgyu 'phral drwa ba'i chos sde ngo
mtshar can shog ser ldeb brgyad tsam byon pa las/ rdo rje drag rtsal chos sde lam rim ye shes snying po gtan la phab nas ljags bshad tshar kha shas gnang / rtsa gsum chos
tshan kha shas phabs kyang gzhan la gnang grub pa ni ma byung ngo / /dgung grangs zhe gnyis pa chu khyi hor zla gnyis pa'i tshes nyer bdun nub mo gnyan chen thang lha
dngos su 'ongs nas sgrom bu zhig phyag tu phul nas/ khyed rang snying drung gi phug par 'ongs na sgrom bu 'di sprad dgos pa yin kyang dus thog la ma byung / da nas dus yol
zin pas ci bya med na'ang khyed rang la thengs pa yin/ dbus gtsang du'ang dus bde mo 'ong dka' bas nged rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar bi ma mi tra'i mdun 'gro ba yin zer ba
la/ rje nyid nas de ltar yin dus phyogs gang du'ang dus bde 'jags dka' ba 'di bzhin ci phan ci dgos bi ma mi tra la zhus shog gsungs par/ dus khug bcu yod pa'i brgyad pa
la slebs pa yin/ re zhig bi mas kyang ci gsung yod dka'/ thugs rje chen po bsgom/ ma Ni bzla/ dam skong dong sprugs ci mang byas na khol bu re rer bde bar srid/ thams cad
bsam pa bzang

po gal che ste zhes zer ba'i mur yal song gsungs/ sgrom de rjes nas zhal 'byed pa'i nang klu 'jim las grub pa'i gu ru'i sku tshab mkhyid gang thod phreng sde lnga yab yum gyi
byang sems kyi 'dam pas g.yogs pa/ gu ru rin po che'i tshems/ sprul pa'i ring bsrel chu shel mdog can grangs mang / bla ma sku bzhi'i sgrub thabs rnams byon pa'i tshems
kyi ring bsrel dad ldan zhu pa po su byung la gnang bas stong phrag mang po song yang 'dzad du med la/ phyis sku gshegs kha'i snga lo tsam nas gter srung gis phar khyer
ba red gsungs mi bzhugs pa yin 'dug /bla ma sku bzhi'i chos skor ni tshes bcu'i sku'i rnam 'gyur rnams gzhir byas pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum du bzhugs pa'i
rgyas pa de yin par 'dug kyang / dbu'i lo rgyus phyed lhag tsam las gzhan gtan las 'bebs par ma gnang zhing yang gter du rgyas btab par mngon/ dgung grangs zhe bdun pa me
yos smin drug zla ba'i yar tshes nang a lo dpal 'byor sgang du phebs/ phran bu la'ang bka' 'phrin gnang ltar zhabs bcar zhus/ tshes bcu'i nub mor stod 'bras mo ljongs nas
smad g.yu lung gangs ra yan gyi gnas che chung stong phrag lhag pa'i bkod pa dang gter kha sogs sgrib med du gzigs pa'i gsal snang shar/ tshes bcu gcig nyin rgyab ri zhi
khro shel phug la tshogs skong mdzad/ grol tig skor gsum dang / gnas yig 'ga' zhig gi shog ser bzhes/ 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char byung / gnas yig kha shas gtan la phab
bar mdzad/ yang me yos lor rje nyid dang mchog gling lhan rgyas phebs bzhud mdzad skabs yab bzhis ri bo khyung lding ngam khyung tshang brag

nas rdo sgrom rim pa gsum pa zhig spyan drangs pa la rtsa gsum bka' 'dus kyi cha lag rjes 'bangs nyer lnga so so'i sgrub thabs dam rdzas bcas bzhugs pa yin 'dug kyang / dam
rdzas phyogs bsdus tsam las gzhan spel bar ma mdzad/ de rjes dbyar thog cig la gter ston kun grol gsang ba rtsal phyag mjal du bcar ba na/ da res gter lhung phyogs su song
/ pha waM gser gdugs can na sangs rgyas rabs bdun gyi ring bsrel yod pa dang / padma shel rir gter kha zhig yod pa sogs rje nyid sngar phebs skabs gra 'grigs po ma byung
ba dang da phan dngos kyis phebs pa mi 'ong bar 'dug pas de rigs lon rgyu byung na gal che ba yod tshul bkas gnang ba ltar/ gter ston kyang byon nas tshogs skong gser
skyems gsol 'debs mdzad kyang ring bsrel gzhan ma byung / zla gam dbang phug tu zhag gsum sgrub pa tshogs skong grub pa'i snga dro gnas kyi dbu rtser lha srin dam bsgrags
mdzad pas/ 'ja' sprin 'khrigs pa'i nang du padma shel ri nas bya rgod cig 'phur te 'og gi brag rtser babs nas gter sgrom zhig bzhag song ba sindhU ra'i 'jim rlon pas btums
pa zhig yod 'dug pa de ka ltar khur nas rje bla mar phul bas nang gi sgrom zhal phyes pa las/ tshe dbang rig pa 'dzin pa'i sku tshab li smug las grub pa/ rtsa gsum spyi
'dus kyi chos skor/ gnas chen mang po'i mdo byang gi shog ser rnams bzhugs par snang ba las spyi 'dus kyi las byang dbang tsam zhig 'bebs par mdzad/ shog ser yang gter
du bsdams par mngon no/ /rje nyid kyi sku skye ba 'di'i zab gter gyi gtso bo gtsang g.yas ru rtsis kyi lha khang du bzhugs pa'i rtsa gsum bka' 'dus chen mo yin

par snang yang bzhes ma grub pas de'i cha lag tu gyur pa/ gter ston las rab gling pas kaH thog nas spros bral bde chen sgos sgrub kyi shog ser bton pa sogs dang / kho bos lag
tu 'byor pa'i gtsang rong bkra shis lha rtse'i nye sras brgyad kyi sgrub skor/ rdzongs shod bde gshegs 'dus pa'i pho brang gi rig 'dzin brgyad kyi sgos sgrub yod pa rnams
kyang gtan la pheb pa ma byung ngo / /gzhan yang bod du lan rjes mar phebs skabs nyid dang nye gnas tshul khrims rgya mtsho gnyis kho na zhabs rkyang gis dbus gtsang
gi dgon pa dang gnas rten rnams la phebs pa'i tshe/ shangs zab bu lung du phebs nas spang ljongs yid 'ong zhig tu gsol tshigs mdzad pas/ brag der rje btsun sgrol ma'i sgrub
skor rgyas pa nyid kyi gter skal de yod par shin tu gsal yang zhag bzhugs don gnyer mdzad rgyu ma byung bas shog ser dngos phyag tu ma son kyang de nang gang yod thugs
la bkra lam mer gsal bas rtsa ba ldeb gsum bzhi skor phyag bris su gnang ba'i skabs der/ jo jo zhig gis sgrol ma'i sku rnying zhig phyag tu phul nas 'di la rin rtsa gser
zho bdun gnang dgos zhus pa ltar gser zho bdun kho na sku chas glo 'dogs su yod pa byin gsungs/ tshul de nye gnas pas ni gtan nas mthong mi 'dug pas gter srung gis dngos
su phul ba dang gser de'ang gter tshab tu dgos pa yin 'dug /sku brnyan 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi thugs dam rten yin gsungs nas shin tu thugs rtsis chen po mdzad/ phyis gter
chen mchog gyur gling pa la legs so zhes pa'i gsung lan gsum byon/ slad nas sgrol ma zab tig gi smin grol dang lhan cig kho bo la bka' drin du

stsal ba da lta yang khrod kun bzang bde chen 'od gsal gling gi rten gtsor bzhugs pa 'di yin la/ jo mo kha rag tu phebs lam du phur pa khyad can zhig phyag tu son pa'ang gter
srung gis dngos su phul bar nges pa dang / me yos lor khang dmar mdor phebs skabs/ kho bos 'di skor rdor sems gter kha bzhugs nges par bdud 'dul rdo rje'i gter lung las
gsal bas sne gcig bzhes nas gnang thub pa gsol ba btab pas/ padma shel rir bai ro'i gsang phug tu mchog gling dang phran cag kha shas bcas lhan cig phebs nas tshogs 'khor
gnang ba'i mthar phug de ka nas bai ro'i thugs dam rten gyi rdor sems li sku khyad par can zhig bzhes nas phyis kho bo la stsal ba dang / rdzong shod kyi sku'i gnas nas
padma rgyal po'i sku rgyan dpag bsam shing gi 'bras bu yin 'dug gsungs pa mdzub mgo tsam shin tu ngo mtshar can bzhes pa dang / gnas de'i dpal de'u'i mgon po phyag bzhi
pa'i gsang phug nas mnga' bdag nyang rin po ches yang gter du sbas pa'i gnam lcags rdo rje khyad par can zhig bzhes pa phyis rdzogs chen dgon du nang rten stsal/ khro zil
phram gyi mdun ngos chu mig gcig nas mkha' 'gro las kyi dbang mo'i rang byung gsang ba'i bdud rtsi dang / zla gam dbang phug nas dzam bha la'i sku rnying / de'i nye phyogs
sgrol ma brag nas 'phags ma'i snying thig gi sgrub rten ril bu/ si ngu g.yu mtsho nas mon mo bkra shis khye'u 'dren gyi dar sham/ byang chub shing gi lo mas mtshon khams
dbus gtsang gsum nas rten dang dam rdzas mang po zhig bzhes yod par snang yang 'dir rang gis thos tshod tsam bkod pa yin la/ de rnams kyang thang yig las/ nga yis sa

steng gter gyis bkang nas yod: dngos grub 'dod na gter gnas kun nas longs: zhes gsungs pa ltar sbyor lam yan chad la gnas pa'i gang zag skal ba can la gter gyi dngos grub phyogs
gang nas kyang rtsol med du 'byung ba yin 'dug go /rje 'di nyid dang mchog gyur gling pa lhan rgyas su gyur pa'i zab gter bla sgrub skor bzhir grags pa/ phyi'i bla
sgrub bar chad kun sel/ nang sgrub yid bzhin nor bu bsam pa lhun grub/ gsang sgrub mtsho skyes snying thig /yang gsang rdo rje drag rtsal rnams dang / snying tig skor bdun
ces pa dga' rab rdo rje/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ shrI seng ha/ bi ma la mi tra/ gu ru padma/ ye shes mtsho rgyal/ bai ro tsa na bcas kyi snying thig so sor bzhugs pa las/
bar chad kun sel rje nyid la thog mar byung tshul gong smos ltar la mchog gling gi shog ser yang lo brgyad tsam du gtan la 'bebs thub pa ma byung ba phyis rje nyid nas
rten 'brel mthun sbyor gyis gtan 'bebs mdzad skabs kyang las byang chen mo'i skor dang bkol byang rnams mchog gling nas phab/ gzhan thams cad rje nyid nas 'bebs par gnang
'dug pa dang / gzhan gsum po bshad dang 'chad 'gyur ltar la/ dga' rab snying thig smad shod dzaM nang brag dkar yang rtse dang / bai ro'i snying thig rdzogs chen sde gsum
padma shel phug nas lhan rgyas kyis spyan drangs/ mtsho rgyal snying thig seng gnam brag dang / sde gsum cha lag rigs gsum snying thig ye rgyal nam mkha' mdzod nas mchog
gyur gling pas spyan drangs pa'ang gtan la phab dus lhan rgyas mdzad pa yin cing / snying thig gzhan rnams ni rje bla ma nyid la bka' babs par snang mod/

gnas dus kyi rten 'brel sogs kyis phyogs mtshon tsam las ji bzhin gtan la pheb thub pa ma byung ngo / /spyir sa gter gyi gtso bo rje bla ma nyid la rtsa gsum bka' 'dus/ mchog
gling dang thun mong du rtsa gsum sgyu 'phrul drwa ba/ kho bo la rtsa gsum dgongs 'dus kyi bka' babs mnga' ba las rtsa gsum dgongs 'dus kyi gter kha shing khyi lor dngos
grub tu thob pa/ spyan sngar gzigs 'bul zhus pa dgyes tshor chen pos gdan sogs snga rgyun las lhag pa'i mnga' gsol mdzad/ mchog gyur gling pa rten 'brel gyi thog ma 'chugs
nas thugs sgrub bar chad kun sel gyi shog ser 'bebs ma thub pa'ang khong gis dbu bton pa yin/ da res khyod kyi gter kha 'di'ang tshang ma gtan la 'bebs thub dgos pas
brda yig gi rgyus yod dang grogs dan gnyis ka mdzad gsungs nas tshogs skong gsol 'debs gzabs rgyas bcas/ chos sde la mdzod lngar bzhugs pa'i lung gter gyi mdzod chen po'i
dgongs 'dus rnam bzhi'i nang tshan bla ma dgongs 'dus chos tshan tho bkod gnang / rig 'dzin mchog sgrub chos tshan bzhi tsam phran dpon slob zung 'brel nas legs par grub
mtshams gzhan rkyen zhig la brten nas sku bsnyel bas 'phros lus/ 'di skor dag snang mang du 'dug kyang 'dir ma bkod/ de phyin 'bebs je dkar song yang rje nyid nas khur
len mdzad pa'i thugs dgongs zhal bzhes 'gyur med gnang ba'i me byi zla ba bdun pa'i tshes drug gi tho rangs 'od gsal ngang / gangs ti se yin zer ba'i shel dkar mchod rten
dbyibs bang rim brgyad pa'i steng du phebs/ der gter rtags kha cig yod pa'i brag phug zhig tu chos gos lhung bzed phyag 'khar bcas bzhugs/ bud med 'ga' shas

dang mnyam tshogs 'khor zhig mdzad par/ shar phyogs nas nyi ma zhig shar/ de'i zer la 'ja' 'od me tog gi char babs pa dang lhan cig o rgyan rin po che phebs nas mdun tu stegs
zhig la byams bzhugs mdzad/ za ma tog lta bu'i dmar ser zhig bsnams nas/ 'di rgyud lung man ngag chu bo bzhi 'dus pa'i dbang yin gsungs te gnas gsum du bzhag /kA ya a
bhi Shinytsa oM sogs sngags rnams gsungs mthar phyag tu gnang ba zhu la khad lta bu'i snyi nyor nyor zhig 'dug pa zhal du bzhes pas ro mngar ba zhig gi khu bas sku lus thams
cad gang ba'i snang ba byung / da tshig bdun gsol 'debs 'bum ther zhig grub pa gyis dang o rgyan babs 'ong gsungs pa'i 'phros la nyams sad/ de nyin phran la tshig bdun
'bum ther de 'grub par byas nas rtsa gsum dgongs 'dus gtan la 'bebs thub pa zhig yin 'dra gsungs nas gter sgrub kyi tshul du gnas dang 'don lugs ljags bkod zhib par stsal
ba bzhin bsgrubs pa'i skabs tshig bdun sgrub thabs de byung ba rje'i bka' bzhin phal cher yi ger bkod/ de phyin rje nyid la mjal mkhan sogs je mang song ba'i rnam g.yeng
kho nas thugs lcogs pa gtan nas ma byung bas yid ches dpang po thub pa'i rdo rje'i gsung de 'dra zhig med phyin rtog pa'i 'char sgo yi ger bkod pa la dgos nus gang yang
ma mchis shing gnas dus kyi rten 'brel phal cher yang yol zin pas kho bo'i skal pa'ang de tsam du zad do/ /gsum pa de las 'phros pa'i yang gter gyi bka' babs byung ba'i
tshul ni/ dgung grangs bzhi bcu don grub sa mo lug gi lor skabs shig mnal lam du/ gter chen sangs rgyas gling pa sngags btsun gyi chas stod gos

rgya kha'i steng sku gzan smug pos dkris pa zhig mjal ba la gus 'dud bcas nyid kyi rdzogs chen snying po bsdus pa de gnang thub par zhus pas phyag tu glegs bam zhig bsnams
te/ rdzogs chen snying po bsdus pa las 'dis dga'/ 'di nged rang gi bsam yas brag seng ge'i gdong can nas bton pa'i gter 'byung chen mo yin gsungs nas phyag tu stsal ba zhal
phyes nas gzigs pas phyed gter ston de snga byon zin pa dang / phyed da lta dang 'byung 'gyur rnams kyi rnam thar dang gter chos kyi rnam grangs zhib par snang ba slar
pusti yar phul ba phyag tu bzhes nas nyid kyi dbur bzhag ste byin rlabs kyi tshig 'ga' zhig gsungs pa'i mthar gter ston glegs bam dang bcas pa nyid la thim pas nyid kyi
sku glegs bam der song ba 'dra zhig la gter ston stong rtsa lhag pa'i lo rgyus gter chos rnams re re nas bkra sa ler gsal ba zhig byung / de las sad nas kyang zhag shas de
ltar thugs la gsal zhing / phyis su'ang dgongs pa ched du gtad na zhib cha mkhyen par 'dug gsungs/ gter rnying dpe lung gnyis ka med rigs dang / dpe rgyun yod kyang rgyun
dkon gras rigs la ched du gsol 'debs mdzad pa na gter ston de dang de'i ye shes kyi skus dbang lung stsal cing / gter srung mkha' 'gro rnams kyis yang gter du sbas pa'i
shog ser dang rten dang dam rdzas phul ba ni mngon sum grub par snang / de las thog ma'i skabs shig gter ston sangs rgyas bla ma sngags btsun chas stod gos ser po'i steng
mnab gzan rgya smug dkris pa zhig dngos su byon nas khong gi gter chos rtsa gsum dngos grub brtan gzigs yin gsungs chos tshan nyer gcig pa'i byin rlabs stsal/ chos skor
de nyid brda yig tu bkod par mdzad pa dngos gzhi gtan la phab pa

ma byung yang mdor dril nyams len rtsa gsum dril sgrub kyi las byang dang gtor dbang tsam mdzad par snang / gu ru rin po ches g.yo ru khra 'brug tu bka' 'dus chos kyi rgya
mtsho'i chos 'khor bskor ba'i skabs su lha lcam mandA ra bas ma 'ongs pa'i gdul bya la dgongs pas gsol ba btab pa'i ngor stsal ba/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i dgongs pa'i gnad
gcig tu dril ba/ tshig nyung la don 'dus pa/ nyams len bde la byin rlabs che ba/ bka' 'dus snying po'i yang bcud bla ma bstan gnyis sku gsum bde gshegs 'dus pa'i zab
tig mthong ba rang grol gyi gdams skor bal bod mtshams purNa rdza ri'i shar phyogs kyi pha waM dga' ba 'khyil ba 'dra bar gter du sbas pa rgya lo tsA ba rdo rje bzang pos
spyan drangs nas slar 'dab gter du sbas pa/ gter srung mkha' 'gros shog ser phyag tu phul ba la le'u brgyad bzhugs pa'i le'u drug yan gtan la phab/ gter sgrub cung zad mdzad
pas gter ston nyid kyis byin rlabs kyang stsal/ don dbang dang phab zin pa'i lung bka' drin tu stsal ba thob/ padma saM bha was mchims phu la sogs pa'i sgrub gnas rnams
su rgyal sras lha rje gtsos rje 'bangs 'dus pa phyi ma rnams la bla rdzogs thugs gsum gcig dril thugs rje chen po padma zhi khro'am padma rgyal po'i chos skor la rgyas
'bring bsdus pa snying po'i yang bcud bzhir bzhugs pa las zab don kun 'dril yid bzhin nor bu mthong ba rang grol gyi chos sde mang yul byams sprin gyi gtsug lag khang du
sbas pa gter ston nyi ma seng ges bton kyang yum dang grwa 'khor gyis thugs sun phyungs pa'i rkyen gyis 'gro don brtul bas slar yang gter du sbas pa/ rab tshes dang po
me yos zla ba lnga pa'i dmar phyogs kyi tshes

bcu'i nub zhing skyes dbang gi mkha' 'gro tsaNDi kas shog ser sgril kha chung ngu zhig phyag tu phul ba lo skor gcig tu gsang ba'i rgyas btab/ phyis sa yos lo'i sos kar sngar
gyi mkha' 'gros shog ser 'bebs par bskul ba dang / nyams kyi snang char g.yo ru khra 'brug gi khyams stod o rgyan lha khang du phebs/ sku tshab nyid gu ru rin po che dngos
su gyur nas bka' 'dus sgrub chen stegs bu'i khar dkyil 'khor dbang rdzas rnams skad cig gi sprul nas smin grol chig rdzogs su stsal ba'i nyams de las sad pa na/ brda
yig gi tshig don thams cad bkra lam gyis gsal ba ltar gu ru rin po che la rtse gcig tu gsol ba btab nas gtan la phab pas nyin zhag gnyis la rtsol med grub nas thugs nyams
su'ang bzhes shing 'chad spel mdzad/ gu ru rin po che brag dmar zan yangs su bzhugs pa'i tshe rje 'bangs grogs lnga dang / zhang blon rdo rje sprel chung bcas kyis zhus
pa'i ngor rnal 'byor ma rgyud padma gar dbang gi mkha' 'gro'i rtog pa las phyungs te stsal ba padma mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs phyi nang gsang ba yang gsang de kho na nyid
du sgrub pa rnams la zab pa dang rgya che ba dang snying po'i tshul gyis gdams ngag 'dra min gsum du bsdus nas gter gnas gsum du sbas pa rnams gter ston so sos bton/ shin
tu zab cing 'dril ba gsang sgrub lha lnga'i gdams skor gtsang rong chen gyi nyin mo'i stod phyogs brag dmar zla gam 'dra ba'i phug pa'i sgor sbas pa rong zom lo tsA ba
chos kyi bzang pos gter nas bzhes pa mkha' 'gro ma rig byed rtsal zhes grags pa'i dbang lung gi rgyun gnas gsar 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dang zhig po gling pa rnams kyis
kyang gsan thor 'khod rung / phyis 'dir dpe lung gnyis ka'i

rgyun mi bzhugs pa la rab tshes lcags 'brug lor chos bdag mkha' 'gros dpe rnying dngos su phul/ o rgyan rin po che dang lo chen bai ro gnyis kas smin grol gyi gdams pas byin
rlabs stsal te bu dpe rgyas par bkod/ lo de'i sa ga zla bar cung zad thugs nyams su bzhes pas grub pa'i mngon rtogs kyang gsal bar byung gsungs/ sa rta lo'i skabs shig
yar rje o rgyan gling pa sngags pa rnying pa pad zhwa can dngos su byon nas bka' 'dus chos kyi rgya mtsho'i tshom bu nyer gcig pa snying po bcud dril gyi gdams pa stsal ba
gtan la phab ste rim par thugs nyams su bzhes pas bar chad kyi g.yul las rgyal/ chos 'di mtha' dmag sogs nag phyogs gdug pa'i tshogs kyi gnyen po gcig tu gyur pa'i stabs
thog mar glegs bam zhal phye ba tsam la'ang 'tshubs chen po re 'byung bar 'dug gsungs/ sku tshe 'dir mngon spyod kyi phrin las phra mo tsam yang mdzad ma myong yang chos
'di'i byin rlabs shugs 'byung gi tshul du/ nyag dpon pa'i dus zing gis mdo khams pa thams cad sdug bsngal la sbyor skabs chu phag zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes nyer lnga'i nub
mnal ltas su/ mdun du lcags slang zhig gi nang ling chung bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi so so'i snying gar stag ma'i lo ma la e nr-i tri dzaHkhrag gis bris pa re re bslan pa bkod
'dug /der mi brjid can zhig gis dang po'i 'khrugs pa 'di la dmag dpon che khag ming thogs bzhi bcu zhe bzhi yod/ de re re la skyob pa'i lha zhe bzhi/ rjes 'brang gi dam sri
zhe bzhi yod pas dkar phyogs dar na rgyal khams su bde 'jags cung zad kyi rgyur 'gyur srid kyang / nag phyogs dar na phung khrol tshab je cher 'gyur bas dam sri 'di rnams
bsgral dgos zhes nan gyis btud nas

zer 'dug pa la/ rje nyid nas kyang ci dran med pa la thog mar gur drag gi sgom bzlas zhig mdzad mur dpal mgon ma ning gi skur dngos su gyur 'dug /de'ang gnas gyur nas kun thub
rgyal mo sku mi tshad las 'das pa zhig tu song 'dug pas dmigs pa'i sbyor bas dgug bstim re re mdzad pa na/ dam sri gzig sogs gcan gzan/ sdig sprul sogs klu nor/ khra
glag sogs 'dab chags sha zan 'jigs rung gi mgo can grangs med pa bkug nas ling chung la bstims pas re re bzhin tshad las 'das pa'i gzugs brnyan chen po srog dang bcas par
gyur pa mtshon cha sna tshogs kyis bsgral/ khrag gi rgyun 'od chu ltar bab/ de dag gi sha zos/ khrang 'thung ba sogs lhag med du byas/ de 'dra re re bzhin bgyis pa'i grangs
nyer bzhi rdzogs mtshams mnal sad/ dngos su'ang khrag dri snom pa sogs byung 'dug /de rjes ngos bzung med pa'i bsnyun khams kyis gsung 'gag pa sogs kyang byung 'dug pas/
de skabs bstan pa'i rim gro 'don bya sogs sgrub mkhan mang 'dug kyang don du rje 'di nyid kyi thugs rjes nag phyogs gdug pa'i tsha ngar phyed tsam zhi nas rgyal khams
su bde skyid sprin bar gyi nyi ma tsam brdol bar mngon no/ /gu ru rin po ches mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal la thugs dam snying por stsal ba mkha' 'gro gsang ba kun 'dus
kyi gdams skor e gzar mo lung gi phug par sbas pa/ jo mo sman mo padma mtsho skyid la mkha' 'gro rnams kyis gter dpe dngos su sprad kyang rang gi thugs nyams su bzhes pa
tsam las gzhan la spel ba'i skabs su ma babs pas slar 'dab gter du sbas/ jo mo nyid dbus gtsang gi rgyal khams rnams nyul nas phebs pa'i skabs

lho brag tu gu ru chos dbang dang mjal bas smin grol gyi gdams pas rjes su bzung / gsang ba'i las rgyar brten pas ye shes kyi rtsa mdud grol te bka' brgyad gsang rdzogs kyi
rgyud sngar ma khrol ba'ang gtan la 'bebs thub pa sogs byung bas gzungs ma'i gtso mor gyur/ phyis 'dir rje nyid chos dbang rin po che'i dus kyi bag chags shin tu gsal ba
dang / sngon gyi rten 'brel las ye shes mtsho rgyal dang ngo bo gcig la rnam par tha dad du snang ba'i jo mo nyid kyis byin gyis brlabs shing ye shes kyi bha santa'i sgo
'byed pa dang / gter srung gis gter dpe spyan lam du phab pas dgongs pa nam gtad spyan lam du brda yig rtsol med du 'char bar snang bas mdos skong dang sgrub pa'i khog dbub
ma gtogs chos sde gzhan tshang bar gtan la phab par mdzad pa chos sde 'di ni deng sang gi sngags skor zhugs pa kun la shin tu gal gnad che bar 'dug ste/ gzhung gi lung
byang las/ sngon tshe 'og min gsang chen zhing : ye shes rang snang pho brang du: dbyings kyi yum chen kun bzang mo: longs sku rdo rje phag mor bzhengs: chos nyid rang
sgras gsang chen rgyud: dus gsum dus med rtag tu gsungs: bar du mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i gling : o rgyan rang byung dur khrod du: bcom ldan badzra wA rA hIs: padma thod phreng
bdag nyid la: rgyud lung man ngag gsang ba'i mdzod: smin grol yongs su rdzogs par stsal: da lta don gyi rnal 'byor ma: bka' yi sdud po mtsho rgyal lcam: dhA ki 'bum gyi
tshogs bcas la: bod yul grub pa'i gnas kyi mthil: dbang chen dgyes pa'i pho brang du: bdag nyid mtsho skyes rdo rje yis: rdo rje phag

mo'i gsang ba che: rgyud kyi dgongs pa snying por dril: lung gi nges pas gtan la phab: man ngag lag len dmar khrid du: thugs kyi nying khu brnag pa byin: rang rang nyams len
mthar dbyung la: rin chen sa yi snying por sbos: nam zhig mkha' 'gros byin brlabs pa'i: rigs ldan bu mo sprel lo ma: sbas tshul jo mo'i ming can la: mkha' 'gro rnams kyis
chos 'di gtad: byin rlabs rtogs pas rang bzhin grol: dus der gzhan don cher mi 'byung : 'brel tshad bde chen sa la sbyor: phung po lhag med byung chub thob: slar yang
bod khams sdug pa'i dus: chos kyi rgyal po'i skye ba'i mtha': mtsho rgyal khyod kyis byin brlabs pa: sus kyang brtag par dka' ba yi: ma nges 'gro 'dul rig pa 'dzin: sgyu
ma lta bu'i skyes bu zhig: mdo khams shar nas 'byung dang 'phrad: lo tsA chen po'i ye shes dang : gnyis min gnyis su snang ba'i tshul: sngags kyi gdung mtha' byang chub sems:
blo gros mi zad gter la gtad: gnyis ka'i smon lam la brten nas: skal ldan 'ga' yi nyams chag sbyong : la la sngags kyi brtul zhugs spyod: 'ga' zhig bde chen ye shes
rnyed: dngos grub dga' ston rgyas par 'gyur: zhes bka' stsal pa ltar ro/ /gu ru rin po che nyid ngo bo dpal che mchog he ru ka dang rnam dbyer med kyang gdul bya drang pa'i
slad du rdo rje bdud rtsi'i grub brnyes slob dpon bdud rtsi gsang ba las gdams ngag yongs rdzogs gsan pa'i tshul bstan/ bod du gnyags dznyA na ku mA ra la bdud rtsi yon
tan gyi rgyud lung man ngag spyi dang khyad par rdo rje bdud rtsi gsang ba chen po'i man ngag snying thig zab mo ting nge 'dzin bdun gyi rim

par phye ba'i gzhung nyid yar lung bsam 'grub shel gyi brag phrag tu bsgyur tu stsal cing / chos rgyal yab sras sogs 'dus pa rnams la smin grol stsal/ dpe rgyud padma brtsegs
pa'i phug par rgyas btab pa phyis ra mo shel sman ye shes bzang pos spyan drangs te thugs nyams su bzhes/ slar rdo rje'i lung don bzhin rang gnas su sbas par mdzad pa/
rje nyid dgung grangs nga bdun me byi zla ba dang po'i yar tshes skabs kyi tho rangs shig tu sngags srung e ka dzA Ti nyid zhing skyes kyi mkha' 'gror rnam par 'phrul pas
gdams pa 'di'i gter dpe tA la'i lo mar nag ra dang brda yig 'dres mar bris pa phyag tu phul te lo rgyus rgyas par zhus/ de rjes o rgyan rin po che la gsol 'debs yang yang
mdzad pas snron zla'i tshes bcu'i tho rangs dag pa'i snang bar padma 'od kyi gzhal med khang du gu ru rin po che 'khor dang bcas pas sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
cing gdams ngag gcig rdzogs su stsal/ las kyi rdo rje gnyags lo chen po'i zhal nas 'di nyid bdud rtsi yon tan gyi bka'i gtso bo yin cing da dung sman gyi rdzong 'phrang
chen mo'i bka' babs yod tshul gyi lung bstan kyang mdzad/ de nas bzung ste gter shog tu gang bzhugs pa'i tshig don thams cad sgrib thogs med par thugs la lam mer chub
pas chos skor yongs rdzogs mig 'phrul lta bu'i cho 'phrul chen po ngo mtshar ba'i bkod pas gtan la phab nas kho bo cag la skal ldan du dbugs dbyung zhing dbang khrid gdams
ngag thams cad bka' drin du stsal/ 'di'i dbang skur kho bos ched du zhus pa'i sta gon nub mor/ rje bla ma nyid ri rong dog po zhig tu phebs/ mi zhig la sa cha 'di gar red
dris pas so ma pu

ri'i nye skor red zer/ de nas yar byon pas thang cung yangs pa zhig tu phebs pas/ mi des so ma bu ri ya ki red zer/ ri shin tu gzar zhing mtho ba'i rtse mor brag dkar 'dra
zhig snang / der 'dzeg pas yud kyis phyin pa na khang pa rtsag mtho zhig snang ba'i nang du phebs pa'i rtsag mang po zhig bgrod/ da rung steng du rtsag gnyis yod snyam/ bar
snang du slebs pa lta bu mtho ba'i nang du khri stan zhig 'dug pa nyid kyi yin snyam gyis der bzhugs/ der ri che'i phyag mdzod lta bu zhig 'dug pa la 'di na shin tu gnad
che ba'i rten ci 'dra yod ces dris par/ 'di yi rten gyi gtso bo 'di yin zhes phug logs su sgam zhig 'dug pa la mdzub mo btsugs/ de na ci 'dra yod dris pas/ rgyal po dzaHla
bka' babs chu bo bzhi'i dbang gi chu rgyun ma chad pa yod zer/ der nged rang da lta'i cha byad ltar 'dug pas sgam de phyes song ba 'di gang yin gyis lta phod sa mi 'dug
zer/ nyid phebs pas de nang khron pa gting med pa 'dra ba la/ bar dan du chang bum lta bu'i ljang gu che legs zhig 'dug pa na nyid sngar mal bzhugs/ nged kyis de drangs
byung ba shin tu phra ba'i ba thag gis sbrel ba lta bu'i ngang / de nang nas bum chu dkar shas can zhig phyag tu blugs byung ba de bzhes pas sku lus kyi nang thams cad
gang / bde ba skyes/ chang bzi lta bu'i rnam 'gyur dang / rtog med kyi nyams 'char/ slar nged la gnang ba nged rang yang nyid la skyes pa'i nyams de shar song / mi des da
res sku zhabs rnam pa tsho zhal 'dzom/ dbang bum gdan drangs/ skal pa shin tu bzang pas nga rang la'ang gnang bar zhu zer bas lag tu blugs pas 'thungs song ba de la'ang
nyams de skyes song / de na re/ da res rnam

pa tsho la bum chus sku lus gang ba bum dbang / bde ba gsang dbang / chang bzi lta bu sher dbang / rtog med kyi nyams skyes pa bzhi pa yin zer nas nam mkhar 'bags pa mkha'
'gro ma dmar mo rus rgyan can zhig tu gnas gyur song / der thugs dgongs la/ mi de rgyal po dzaH mkha' 'gro 'di las kyi dbang mo che yin dgongs pa byung gsungs/ gong gi lung
bstan bzhin rong sman nyi ma 'od gsal gyis yar 'brog gi rdza rong bhi nas spyan drangs pa'i sman gyi rdzong 'phrang chen mo'i snying po bsdus pa'i sman gyi rdzong 'phrang
snying thig ces che mchog bdud rtsi'i dkyil 'khor sger sgrub 'brel ba'i sman gyi chos sde ngo mtshar ba zhig kyang bzhugs pa snang mod/ gtan la 'bebs grub pa ni ma byung
/ yang zab thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i gdams pa ye shes 'od kyi snying po'i chos skor ni/ sngon rab byung drug pa'i lcags mo glang gi lo'i smal po zla ba'i
tshes bcur dpal gyi bsam yas mchims phu'i brag sna seng ge'i gdong nas gnubs chen po'i rnam 'phrul skyes mtha'i byang sems o rgyan dri med kun dgas gdan drangs/ bla rdzogs
thugs gsum rgya che ba'i skor rnams khyab gdal du spel ba la brten nas gdul bya mtha' yas pa smin grol la bkod/ snying po 'di nyid lung byang ltar thugs nyams su bzhes
te gzhan la ma spel bar dpal gyis bsam yas brag dmar mgrin bzang gi bre gu'i sul du rgyas btab pa/ rje nyid la 'gro 'dul 'phags pa'i thugs tig dang lhan cig gter srung
mkha' 'gro mas dngos su phul ba ring du gsang rgyas btab/ rab tshes me mo glang lor mnal lam du khang pa zhig tu phebs par/ phug der zhe chen dbon sprul nyid gos skya zhig
mnabs nas bsnyel ba'i tshul mdzad

nas bzhugs pa'i sku drung du phebs par 'dir ma byon/ nged rang yang mo dga' ches pas mi lo pa mang po byung / rgya nad cig 'gos nas khog smad rul yod/ dri ngan bro bas zhe
ldog gsungs pa dang dri ngan kyang bro ba snyam byed/ cung phyir gyed pas da cung zad bzhugs dang kha dal zhig byed gsungs/ der bzhugs pa dang deng sang kong sprul khyed
gnyis nas gter chos rgyun yod med sna tshogs 'chad spel byed pa red de/ nged kyis de dus kar gling zhi khro'i btags grol sngags la zhu dag byed rtsis byas pa dbang phyug
nyer brgyad kyis srog de'u bcad byas pa yin/ phod le e red gsungs par/ gsar ma 'dra yin na rgyun yod nges pa zhig las shlo ka'ang 'chad srol med/ khyed rang rnying ma ba
rnams kyis bka' gter dag snang gi brgyud srol mang du 'dren srol 'dug pa bzhin nged gnyis nas kyang tshig brgyud ci thob byas pas tshig brgyud med pa cher med/ rgyun dkon
kha shas nyams rmis sogs thob nges ma gtogs gtan nas khungs med 'chad spel byed kyi med gsungs par/ a cang los chog /khyed rang gnyis gter chos rnams kyi bdag po yin 'dug
pas de rnams legs po red kyang / jo mo sman mo zer ba'i gzhong 'tshong ma de dang / ra mo shel sman lha rje skya tho ba de rigs kyi gter chos la rtsa ba byed dus/ nga dri
med kun dga' yin pas de'i bla rdzogs thugs gsum shog ser de gal chung du bskyur ba de ma red gsungs/ der dri med kun dga'i gter chos shog ser zhig snga mo nas lag tu byung
yang 'bebs rgyu sogs ma byung / da res nyid kyi dbang lung zhig mdzad rog zhus nas shog ser de'ang bsgril kha chen po zhig phyag tu bzhugs snang 'dug pas phyag khar
phul ba/ khyed rang rnams slob dpon padma dang / yu bu rnams

kyi gces lo ma ye shes mtsho rgyal gnyis kyis dgos tshad thams cad gnang dus des ma chog pa ci yod gsungs/ nan gyis zhus par de ma thag rnal 'byor pa ral pa sku rgyab nas gtsug
tor du dkris pa/ nang gos dkar po/ de steng dbang gos/ mnab gzan can zil che ba zhig tu gnas 'gyur nas bar snang la 'phag ste/ shog ser thog nas dbang lung dang spyi
bor bzhag nas bka' gtad mdzad pas shog ser spyi bo nas thim snyam ngang de nang ci yod tshig don thams cad khral lam me dgongs pa byung / de nas 'di gsungs/ khyed rang gnyis
kyang dkar chas re byas na legs pa red/ de snga gter ston gyi m-ing thogs mi 'dug /ming thogs dgos/ 'di la gnad chen po yod/ nged kyang sprul sku de'i skabs su dkar
chas ma byas pas rten 'brel 'chug /da dus rgyun mkha' 'gro grib sel shin tu gal che gsungs nas je mthor song ba da rung cung bzhugs grogs zhus kyang nam mkha'i dbyings su
thim pa dang mnal sad/ phyir nang kho bo cag la de ltar byung tshul phebs pas gtan la 'bebs thub par gsol ba btab pas/ bla sgrub/ thugs rje chen po/ phyag chen bcas 'bebs
par mdzad cing dbang khrid chig rdzogs su stsal/ khyad par zab dbang thun mong ma yin pa bka' drin bskyangs te de la brten nas tshe mthar phyin pa'i lung bstan kyang stsal/
bla sgrub cha lag 'ga' zhig bzhugs par snang yang rim lus su gyur cing kho bo'i lam zab le'u bdun ma'ang bla sgrub 'di'i cha lag tu gtogs par snang / 'di'i bla sgrub
yid bzhin nor bu'i lung byang las/ 'di ni rang byung padma bdag nyid kyi: thugs kyi gsang ba rmad byung dwangs ma'i bcud: sku gsum dbyer med 'od kyi snying po'i gzugs:

snod ldan rnams dang 'bral ba'i zhal chems tshul: 'di yin 'di las gzhan du ma bcos par: rtse gcig nyams longs brda yi yi ger bris: mchims phu'i nye 'dabs brag gi sul du sbos:
ma 'ongs rtsub 'gyur dus kyi bar skabs su: gnubs ban rang gis spyod pa'i smon lam thob: dri med ming can de dang 'phrad nas kyang : rang nyams blangs nas ma phyi'i shog
ser ni: 'gro 'dul 'phags pa'i thugs kyi ti ka dang : lhan cig sbas pas rtsub 'gyur yang mtha'i dus: da lta'i dus kyi lha sras mchog grub rgyal: gter ston rkyang pa'i skye
ba bcu gsum pas: 'di nyid blangs nas ring du gsang rgyas gdab: dus su babs tshe snod ldan mchog la spel: des kyang nyams blangs rtogs pa'i rtsal chen rdzogs: kun bzang
gdod ma'i sa la phyin par 'gyur: ces gsungs shing / 'bebs pa'i dus tshod/ rmi lam tshul du chos kyi bdag po yis: bka' gtad byin rlabs skul ma thengs gsum 'ong : zhes gsungs
pa'ang ji bzhin byung bar 'dug go /zhe chen dbon sprul 'gyur med mthu stobs rnam rgyal 'di'ang rdzogs chen bzhi pa mi 'gyur nam mkha'i rdo rjes khong gter ston rgya zhang
khrom gyi skye ba yin/ de skabs mthu stobs che bas deng sang ma nyes kha yog mang ba red gsungs pa'ang ye shes kyi gzigs pa 'khrul pa med par snang ste zhang khrom skye
ba dri med kun dgar yongs su grags shing de'i skye ba dbon sprul rin po che nyid yin pa lung las gsal ba'i phyir ro/ /me glang zla ba dang po'i tshes nyer drug nub mor
dag pa'i snang bar/ thog mar nged rang khri mtho ba zhig tu sdod nas sku gsum ston pa'i dgongs mdzod ring mo zer ba'i chos bka' phal cher sher phyin tshigs bcad byas pa
lta bu la gzhung lam

gsang sngags yin pa/ le'u sum brgya drug cu/ po ti bdun yod pa zhig bshad 'dug pa/ gter ston sus red gsungs pa thams cad kyi thog ma'i gter ston de red zer/ sangs rgyas bla
ma i red gsungs pa ma red gtsug lag dpal dge'i chos red zer/ chos de tshang ma gsan tshar ba dang / gnas 'gyur nas nyang sha mi go cha yin zer ba'i lo tsA sku che zhing
gzi brjid can/ dbu la paN zhu leb bzhag mdzad pa zhig mjal bar/ khyed snga 'gyur lo tsA ba yin na rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i gral du mi 'dug na gsungs pas/ rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i
gral du yod rung med rung nged rang la/ mkhan po bodhi satwa/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ bi ma mi tra/ be ro tsA na bzhi'i gdams ngag thams cad yod pa yin gsungs/
der gdams ngag gnang bar zhus pas/ mkhan po'i gdams ngag phyi sde snod gsum/ slob dpon gyi nang kri yo ga sde gsum/ bi ma la'i gsang ba yo ga gsum dgongs bcud gcig tu dril
ba dgongs mdzod chen mo zhes bya ba bsam yas has po rir gter du sbas pa sha mi rdo rgyal gyis bton nas 'gro don mdzad/ 'gro don rdzogs nas dpe rnams mkha' 'gros drangs
pa yin/ glegs bam bdun yod/ des dgos pa med pas 'di de'i snying po dgongs mdzod zab tig yin gsungs nas le'u gsum pa zhig gi dbang lung rdzogs par gsan/ gu ru padma badzra
nyid tshe lam gyi grogs mchog mandA ra ba dang bcas te brag phug mA ra ti kar 'chi med tshe'i dngos grub bsgrubs nas grub pa'i skabs su sku gsum he ru kas rgyud dang gdams
pa'i gsang mdzod dpag tu med pa gtad cing byin gyis brlabs/ chos rgyal gyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor longs sku 'khor lo bde mchog gi gdams skor mang du stsal

ba rnams rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum du phyes nas gter gnas so sor sbas ba rgyas 'bring gnyis mda' bdag nyang dang bon po lha 'bum gyis gton/ bsdus pa zab don snying po'i bcud
'dril 'di nyid e yul rig pa'i 'byung gnas kyi kha stod gangs bar phug mo che zhes pa'i brag skyibs chen po'i sgo drung pha waM dbang phyug gi mtshan rtags can tu sbas pa
rgya ston padma dbang phyug gis gter nas bton te bla rdzogs thugs gsum gyi chos dang bstan srung gur mgon gyi rgya gzhung dregs pa zil gnon skor man ngag le tshan lnga/ dam
rdzas bdud rtsi'i sman gyi ril bu bcas spyan drangs te/ 'gro don ci rigs mdzad cing gur mgon skor rnams yar lung klu pa'i bla ma rnams brgyud de deng sang sa skya'i gur
mgon gzhung pod me 'bar mar bzhugs pa yin cing / bla ma bde mchog gi chos skor rnams lung byang ltar gnas de nyid du yang gter gyi rgyas btab pa phyis rab tshes sa stag
lo'i sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcur ye shes kyi mkha' 'gros rje bla ma rin po che nyid la gter dpe dngos su bstan cing brda sprod mdzad pa'i rjes thog tu gter ston padma dbang
phyug nyid kyi sku mngon du snang bas dbang dang gdams ngag rdzogs par gnang / de 'phral tshig brgyud yi ge ris su gtan la phab/ chu rta mgo zla'i nyer lngar don brgyud
smin grol gyi gdams pa kho bo cag la chig rdzogs su bka' drin stsal/ gsar ma la yongs su grags pa'i dril bu rim lnga'i khrid kyang ring brgyud bka' srol 'ga' zhig smin khrid
du gsan cing / nye brgyud dag pa'i snang bar grub chen rdo rje dril bu pa yum dang bcas pas brda'i dbang bzhi bskur/ rim lnga'i rtsa tshig sho lo ka gcig bkrol te gsungs
nas mthar bsam mi khyab pa'i skabs su dbyings dang ye shes dbyer med par byin gyis brlabs pa'i chu bo'ang

gcig tu 'du ba ma zad gsar ma'i dril bu rim lnga'i khrid kyi byin rlabs sa chen kun dga' blo gros kyi bar du byung yang de phyis rgyun mi bzhugs kyang / 'di'i dbang gi skabs
rim lnga'i byin rlabs khyad par can yod pas rgyun de'i go yang chod par snang ngo / /zab mo'i rgyud sde mang po'i bcud bsdus pa'i zhi byed bdun gyi man ngag rim pa phye
ba bcu gcig gi gzhung padma saM bha wa dang lha sras ye shes rol pa rtsal gyis bsgyur nas 'u shang rdo'i nub phyogs lha ri rol po brag tu sbas pa rab byung gnyis pa'i nang
lha btsun sngon mo'am lha dbang rgya mtsho blo gros kyis spyan drangs/ ma phyi sgrags kyi yang rdzong du sbas pa rab byung bco lnga pa'i sa pho 'brug gi lor gter chen
mchog gyur gling pas spyan drangs te shog ser rje bla ma rin po cher phul ba gtan la phab nas dbang lung spel bar mdzad/ yaksha dzaM bha la nag po'i gdams skor 'phags pa'i
yul du tshong dpon gyi bu su kha de ba la bka' babs pa rnams rgyal po gu ru de ba las slob dpon chen pos gsan pa'i tshul mdzad/ yagsha rtsa ba'i tantra dang ratna rtsal
chen 'dus pa'i rgyud le'u sum brgya bdun cu rtsa bdun pa'i zab gsang snying po'i yang bcud dum bur phyungs pa dzambha la nag po'i sgrub thabs kyi man ngag rin chen gter
spungs zhes bya ba lag len dmar khrid kyi tshul du bsdebs nas/ bod yul mnga' bdag rje 'bangs rnams la thugs brtse ba chen pos rjes su gdams/ snyigs dus 'gro ba'i don du mtsho
rgyal gyis dpe rgyud 'dra min gsum re bkod nas gter gnas gsum du rgyas btab pa las gnyis po gter ston gzhan gyis spyan drangs/ zab chos 'di nyid bdud 'joms rnam 'phrul
bal po a hU~M 'bar gyis spa gro gcal gyi brag dmar po'i nub phyogs me lce

'khyil ba 'dra ba nas me pho 'brug lo ston zla ra ba'i nya la spyan drangs nas 'gro don rgya cher mdzad/ bar skabs su dar rgyas che ba byung na'ang phyis brgyud pa'i nges tig
med pa dang gter chos kyang nub pa ltar gyur pa'i skabs/ rab tshes lcags 'brug lo'i cho 'phrul zla bar rje bla ma rin po che la chos bdag mkha' 'gros srog 'khor man ngag
dang bcas pa'i dpe rnying dngos su phul cing sgrub thabs kyi skor rnams byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshul du stsal ba la brten nas gtan la phab pa'i skabs su mnal lam dag pa'i
snang bar/ yul ljongs shin tu nyams dga' ba zhig gi kha stod ri bo glang chen 'gying ba lta bu'i gdong pa'i thad tsam du rje nyid phebs pas rgyang ring po nas 'od kyi
gang bu ljang gu shin tu bkrag mdangs dang ldan pa la je nyer slebs pa'i tshe rdo shel ljang nag dwangs ba la nyi zer phog pa'i rkyen gyis 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs su 'phro
ba/ dbyibs nor bu mig gcig lta bu che zhing dwangs pa zhig gi drung du slebs pa na ngo mtshar gyi snang ba bcas nang du zhugs pas/ rin po che'i khri bkod pa phun sum
tshogs pa'i steng du dzaM bha la nag po ljang 'od 'tsher ba/ zhal phyag sogs mngon rtogs dang mtshungs pa shin tu gsal ba la 'khor rnams kyang yod dgongs pa byung / de nyid
skad cig gis o rgyan snang srid zil gnon gyi skur gnas gyur nas smin grol gyi gdams pa chig rdzogs su stsal/ 'di'i sgrub thabs kyi skor rnams sngar bal po a hU~M 'bar
dang gu ru jo tshe'i gter dpe gnyis po gcig lta bu yod pas brgyud pa gnyis 'dres su 'gyur ro gsungs pa'i gnang ba dang bcas byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma khyad par can brnyes/
nor lha rnams kyi nang nas kyang 'di sgrub pa la rgab 'dre'i bar chad med cing bcas pas chog pa'i 'khor lo

sogs zab gnad ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba dang ldan pa yin no/ /ma 'ongs snyigs ma'i dus su bod khams rgyal bsen 'byung po'i 'tshe bas mnar ba la thugs rjes dgongs nas/ gu
ru rin po ches rta mgrin dmar po dpa' bo gcig pa'i man ngag gnam lcags 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i gdams ngag zab la 'dril ba mdzad nas chos rgyal la gnang / des kyang mon gyi
sgom pa ha mi nA tha la gnang nas rjes su gdams pa dang / gu ru rin po che thog mar gtsang stod la ru'i gser kha la phebs pa'i skabs mi ma yin pas bar chad byas pa btul
cing mon gyi rgyal po se 'dar kha sde brgyad kyi gnod pa las grol bar mdzad pa'i rgyal bsen gnad 'bebs srog gi 'khor lo bcas byang pra dun rtse'i btsug lag khang gi ka zhu'i
nang gter du sbas pa phyis lho'i mnga' bdag chen po'i brgyud pa mol mi 'khyil gyis spyan drangs/ 'khor lo sogs sngar dus sngags pa rnams la dar cing grags che yang phyis
su brgyud pa chad nas yun ring song / rab tshes lcags 'brug lor rje bla ma nyid la zhing skyes mkha' 'gros rgyal bsen srog gi 'khor lo'i dpe rnying dngos su phul/ rta
mgrin dpa' bo gcig pa'i gdams skor yang byin rlabs kyi tshul du gnang ba gtan la phab cing skal ldan rnams la bka' drin du stsal bas slob ma la'ang bar chad bsal ba'i mtshan
ma mngon du byung ba sogs byin rlabs kyi babs chen po dang ldan par mchis so/ /slob dpon padma saM bha ba 'phags yul shar phyogs brag phug mA ra ti kar zab lam snying
po'i sgrub pa la brtson pa'i tshul bstan pa'i skabs su rje btsun sgrol ma dngos su byon nas rgyud lung man ngag gi rim pa rgya chen stsal ba rnams kyi nang nas snying po'i
bcud phyungs te gdams ngag rgyas 'bring

bsdus pa'i tshul du gtan la phab nas bod kyi skal ldan rje 'bangs rnams la gnang / ma 'ongs pa'i gdul bya rnams kyi don du gter kha gsum du rgyas btab pa las bsdus pa sgrol
ma 'jigs pa kun skyob 'di nyid gtsang 'o yug g.yag sde'i lung lag g.yag lce khra mo brag tu sbas pa gter ston g.yag phyar sngon mos bton/ shog ser rnams slar yer pa se ba
lung du 'dab gter du sbas pa rong pa bdud 'dul gling pas spyan drangs kyang gter ston glo bur gzhan dbang du gshegs pas gter srung sman btsun rdo rje g.yu sgron mas shog
ser slar khyer ba/ phyis rab tshes sa stag lo'i cho 'phrul zla ba'i yar tshes brgyad la rje bla ma rin po cher mkha' 'gro tsaNDI kas mnal lam du shog ser phul zhing byin
rlabs stsal ba'i gzigs snang byung ba mnal sad pa na mngon sum du snang ba'i shog gu ljang ser zheng sor do dkyus mdzub gang ba brda ris kyis gtams pa zhig las gtan la
phab cing skal ldan rnams la rim par spel bar mdzad do/ /dbu ru lha sa'i ston pa shAkya 'od kyis byang pra dun rtse'i mchod rten nas drag sngags gtso bor gyur pa'i gter chos
mang po spyan drangs pa'i rgyun phal cher sngar dus byung / deng sang ni dpe rgyun tsam yang dkon par snang ba la/ phyag rdor rdo rje me 'bar ces pa'i sgrub thabs zab
cing 'dril ba yang gter du sbas pa'i shog ser gter srung mkha' 'gros rje 'di nyid kyi phyag tu phul ba'ang gtan la 'bebs par mdzad/ bon po brag tshal gyi rdzogs chen gu
ru bzhi pa dang tshe gur sbrags ma 'dab gter du sbas pa'i shog ser rnams phyag tu 'khor zhing nub kha shas btud mar gter ston nyid kyis de dag gi dbang lung stsal ba'i dag
snang byung bar gsungs/ tshe gur sbrags ma phab par mdzad pa las gsham du tshe bdud bzlog

pa'i mdos zab mo zhig yod pa der 'tshubs shin tu che 'dug gsungs nas lus song / nyang po bsam gtan gling pa'i bka' brgyad dregs pa kun 'dul gyi yang bcud snying po'i chos skor
'dab gter du sbas pa rgyud lung man ngag gsum gyi chos skor le tshan bdun yod pa'i shog ser mkha' 'gros phyag tu phul ba las rgyud lung gnyis dang las byang tsam gtan
la phab par mdzad cing dbang chog sogs 'bebs par ma byung / mchog ldan mgon pos bod khams mtha' dmag zlog pa'i rim gro chen po mdzad nas lha ldan du bzhugs pa'i skabs gu
ru rin po ches snyan brgyud du stsal ba'i bar chad kun 'joms rta mgrin gnyen po lha lnga'i sgrub thabs zab cing 'dril ba nyid/ rje bla ma rin po cher dag pa'i snang bar
mchog ldan mgon po'i ye shes kyi skus slar yang snyan brgyud du gdams pa nyid kyang gtan la phab par mdzad/ gu ru rin po che nyid dur khrod bsil ba tshal du bzhugs pa'i tshe
rgyal yum rdo rje phag mos rgyud dang gdams pa rgya cher stsal ba las bod yul rje 'bangs rnams kyi skal pa dang 'tshams pa'i gdams ngag ci rigs par stsal ba rnams rgyas
'bring bsdus pa snying po'i skor dang bzhir phyes te gter gnas rnams su sbas te gter ston so sos bton pa las/ bsdus pa phag mo dkar mo'i sgrub thabs ye shes 'khor lo gsang
ba chen po'i thugs tig nyid rab byung dgu pa'i mthar e spe lcogs gar dbang las 'phro gling pas yar klung shel brag padma brtsegs pa nas ma 'gags rdzu 'phrul gyi rol
pas spyan drangs/ gsang ba'i thugs dam du mdzad pa las gzhan la spel bar ma gnang / shog ser lung byang ltar 'dab gter du sbas pa chos bdag ye shes mkha' 'gros rje nyid la
mdongs

gsol du phul/ rab tshes lcags pho 'brug lo'i cho 'phrul zla bar gtan la phab pa'i tshe las 'phro gling pa nyid kyis dngos nyams rmi lam gyi tshul du smin grol gyis byin gyis
brlabs shing chos sgo 'byed par rjes su gdams pa ltar bdag cag la bka' drin tu stsal/ de dag ni chos sde rdzogs pa dang ci rigs par gtan la phab grub pa rnams smos pa yin
la/ spyir gong du bshad pa ltar bod yul du byung ba'i gter chos yongs rdzogs la rang dbang thob cing / dmigs bsal yang gter gyi shog ser mkha' 'gro gter srung rnams kyis
phyag tu phul nas bzhugs pa'i rnam grangs kyang / sna nam thub pa rgyal po'i rten 'brel yang snying 'dus pa/ dbon sras khyung thog gi yagsha kI la ya/ gtsug lag dpal dge'i
drag sngags thems bdun/ khyung po dpal dge'i rgyal po mdos bcu'i cho ga /sha mi rdor rgyal gyi dgongs mdzod snying thig /zhu yas gnod sbyin 'bar gyi sku gsum nyi zla
'bar ba'i snang ba dang rta mgrin dmar po/ khu tsha zla 'od dam kuu sa sman pa'i rtsa gsum spyi spungs/ rong sman nyi ma'i 'od kyi gso dpyad rdzong 'phrang snying thig /gu
ru jo tshe'i dri med bshags rgyud chog /grwa sgom chos kyi rdo rje'i gur drag ye shes rang gsal/ a ya bon po lha 'bum mam rta nag gu ru rnon rtse'i ma rgyud zab mo kun
'dus/ o rgyan gling pa'i bka' 'dus nyin mtshan rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ sngags 'chang las 'phro gling pa'i padma sha ba ri dmar po/ bla ma grum dang yon bdag nag po mkhar gyi
gsang bdag gdug pa kun 'joms/ kha rag bde chen gling pa'i mkha' 'gro snying thig snying po rnams bzhugs pa zhal nas dngos su thos shing 'ga' zhig dbu bzhag tsam re 'bebs
par mdzad pa'ang yin la/ rang nas ma 'tshal ba'ang mang

du bzhugs yod par snang ngo / /gter rnying las dpe lung gi rgyun dkon pa mi 'gyur las 'phro gling pa'i padma gtum po/ ra zhi padma rig 'dzin gyi khyung khra/ stag mo gter ston
dpon sras khyung thog gi tshe sgrub ye shes srog tig /ta'u rog rje gling pa'i tshe sgrub gsang ba rmad byung rnams kyi dpe rnying tshan pa re gter srung gis phul ba las
dbang lung bka' drin tu stsal skabs padma gtum po'i me long gi sngags 'khor bsub tu med pa'i rang byon tu song ba dang / khyung khras 'og gdon gyis zin pa'i slob ma'i
nad gzhi med du dwangs pa sogs mngon rtags ngo mtshar che ba'ang byung / nyang gter gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rje dang thugs rje chen po 'gro 'dul gyi dbang rgyas pa'i rgyun
mi bzhugs pas gsar du spel bar mdzad pa'i gtan tshigs gong smos ltar las dmigs bsal zhu gnang ma byung / ra shag ma mo sgang shar lung rgyun tsam kho bos thos shing rje nyid
kyis gsan pa gnang skabs 'di'i dbang de rgyun yod pa zhig byung na bka' drin che dgos tshul gsol ba nan tu btab par/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyer dgu'i nub mor rje'i
dag snang du/ gu ru chos dbang sku bong che zhing dbu skra sgor mo thugs ka'i me long yang yod snyam byed pa zhig mjal ba ra shag ma mo sgang shar gyi dbang lung i bzhugs
zhus pa la cung zad khrel ba'i rnam pas/ ma mo'i sogs mdos kyi lag len shin tu mkhas pa khyung nag shAka dar yin gsungs/ de'ang nye skor du yod snyam byed pa'i mur sgrol
ston 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal mtshan du gnas gyur pa la'ang sngar bzhin zhus pa/ de dus nyid la bka' brgyad bder 'dus dbang byas skabs lha ngo bo gcig /gong ma rnams
la brgyud pa'i chu bo gcig 'dres yod pas des 'thus tshul

gsungs yod pas de kas chog tshul gsungs/ de 'gags nas gnas khang zhig tu o rgyan gling pa pad zhwa na bza' dbang gos steng gzan dkris mdzad pa zhig bzhugs 'dug pa la sgang
shar dbang i yod zhus pa/ de ni khong shin tu mkhas/ phyag len mang po btab/ sne gdong sde pas kong por phud skabs 'di'i bsad mdos bcas na bsgral ba la tshegs med kyang de
bsgral na bod spyi la'ang gnod 'dug pas btang snyoms bzhag pa yin gsungs/ sku rgyab rtsigs ngos nas za ma tog snying gzugs ser po zhig blangs/ 'di srid pa ma mo'i rgyud
lung thams cad 'dus pa yin gsungs/ dbur bzhag nas legs sbyar skad kho na ldeb bcu skor tsam gyi tshod zhig gsungs/ byin rlabs gzi brjid chen po'i mthar za ma tog de zhig
song ba lta bu'i dbu gtsug nas sku lus la thim pa'i rkyen gyis sku lus thams cad tsitta zhig tu song zhing bde nyams kyis brgyal thabs su yun cig gnas pa'i mthar sad gsungs/
tshes sum bcu dgongs mo padma mkha' 'gro'i dbang sbyin sreg bcas mdzad nub/ mdun du bud med thog brtsag tshad cig slebs 'dug pa khyod su yin gsungs pas/ nga sprul sku
chen po'i dpe gnyer yin zer/ sprul sku su gsungs pas sprul sku ra shag chen po yin zer/ khyod la ma mo sgang shar dbang lung i yod gsungs pas yod de dbang yar rjes gnang
ba des chog /dpe 'di 'bul du 'ong ba yin zer/ rgya dpe phra ring pod bzhi phul ba gzigs pas lA nya wa ru na ga ra yig sna tshogs 'dug /'di ci la khur ba yin gsungs pas
do nub sbyin sreg des nga dga' nas 'ongs pa yin zer/ ra shag gi rnam thar rags rim dang / lar ra shag gis 'gro don ma byung zer ba red kyang 'gro don bsam

gyis mi khyab pa mthong thos dran reg grol tshul dang / ku sa sman pas kyang go ma chod zer yang sman kha la rag tshad sems can 'bum phrag mang po grol tshul sogs zer ba'i
mthar mi'i lus la bya rog gi mchu shin tu ring po phyung / gzi brjid chen pos kha phar gyus te song 'phral 'khor g.yog bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas yud kyis gshegs par
gzigs/ de rjes sgang shar dbang rgyas par stsal zhing las byang dang dbang chog gsar bsgrigs gal che ba'i bka' gnang ba'ang grub par bgyis so/ /byang chub gling pa dpal
rgyal mtshan gyi gter byon kun bzang thugs gter 'khor 'das rang grol phyis 'dir dbang lung rgyun chad kyang dpe btsal nas zhal bshu gsar bzhengs mdzad pa'i skabs gter ston
nyid kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma dang / sku'i sras bsam 'grub rdo rje yin pa'i bag chags gsal bar sad/ chu lug zla ba dang po'i tshes gcig la 'di'i dbang lung
stsol bar gsol ba btab pa bzhin gnang ba'i nub dang por jo mo rgya gar ma shing lo'i gos can 'ongs nas chos 'di phyis tshod 'chad nyan mkhan ma byung / da res dga' rtags
yin zer 'bras snye zhig phyag tu phul ba'i nyams byung / nub gnyis par mtshan ring du zhabs phyi zhu ba'i rmi lam byung gsungs/ yan lag dbang rnams gnang ba'i nub mo byang
chub gling pa sngags pa sku nyams rgyas shing zil can na bza' shug tshang lta bu sngon pos g.yogs pa gsol bas thugs rje chen po lha drug de'i skor shin tu rgyas pa gsungs
pa dang / sangs rgyas gling pa rab byung chas can sku 'khris su po ti kha shas bzhag pa zhig gis/ nged kyi bla ma dang slob ma gnyis ka yin pa'i ba yo chos bzang dang
khyod gnyis

kyis de snga'i bya ba rnams legs/ da rung gter rnying skor nyi shu rtsa lnga kha longs pa zhig phab rgyu dang 'jog rgyu thon na khyed rang gnyis ka da rung lo nyi shu rtsa
lnga sdod/ gsang sngags rnying ma'i bstan pa la bya ba rgya chen red 'gro gsungs pa byung 'dug /rta mgrin bde bshegs 'dus ba dregs pa kun sgrol gyi chos skor rnams mon yul
chu bzhi 'dus pa'i mgo bo spa gro dpyad dkar gyi brag dmar po me lce dgung du chad pa 'dra ba la chos rgyal khri srong gis sbas pa/ phyis mnga' bdag sku'i thugs sprul drag
sngags bka' babs gter ston gru gu yang dbang ngam rdo rje yang dbang rtsal gyis spyan drangs ba dang / ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs las brgyud pa'i rta mgrin bka'
ma'i skor rnams kyang gter ston nyid nas gsan pas chu bo gcig 'dres su gyur pas byin rlabs mthu stobs 'gran zla dang bral ba nyid sngar dus dar rgyas chen po byung / phyis
nas dbang lung lta ci dpe rgyun tsam yang dkon pa la/ rje nyid kyi phyag tu yar mar kun nas dpe rnying 'ga' re rtsol med du 'byor pa rnams dbu zhabs bsgrigs nas dpe gsar
bzhengs mdzad/ o rgyan rin po che la gsol 'debs nan tan du mdzad pas/ rab tshes lcags 'brug lo'i gro bzhin zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi tshes bcu'i tho rengs khar sngar gru
gu yang dbang nyid kyis zab gter bzhes shing sgrub gnas mdzad pa'i mu nang rdo rje brag dmar rtsar phebs pa'i snang ba la/ skad cig der gru gu yang dbang nyid sngags 'chang
sku bong dang gzi brjid shin tu che ba/ spyan mig zur gsum sogs khro bo'i rnam pa can zhig mig 'phrul lta bur mjal ba la phyag btsal zhing byin rlabs zhus pa na/ nga
gter ston gru gu rdo rje yang dbang gter yin ces dang /

brag de la phyag mdzub btsugs te 'di nas drag po btsan gyi skor zhig spyan drangs pa yin gsungs nas zhal 'dzum mdzad pa de ma thag rta mgrin gyi chos skor rnams gnang bar gsol
ba btab pa na skad cig gis o rgyan sku mdog dmar smug dbu gtsug rta zhal 'tsher ba he ru ka'i chas can zhig tu gnas gyur nas smin grol gyi gdams pa chig rdzogs su stsal/
'di la chos tshan lnga bcu rtsa bdun yod do gsungs pas da lta'i dpe la nyi shu rtsa grangs las mi 'dug pa ji ltar lags zhus pa na/ dus ring bas dpe phal cher zag pa dang
la la mkha' 'gro mas sbas pa srid mod 'on kyang khyed rang gis gsol ba thob dang dgongs pa'i gter las 'char bar 'gyur ba ltar gung bsgrigs nas nyams su longs dang des
chog ces rjes su gdams pa ltar med du mi rung ba'i chos tshan 'ga' zhig kha bskangs par mdzad cing thugs nyams su bzhes pas byin rlabs kyi rtags mtshan khyad par can brnyes
par snang / gter chen rdo rje gling pa'i gter chos rnams kyi bka' babs snga phyi mang du byung bar snang yang / gtso bor rab byung bco lnga pa thog mar tshes pa'i me
yos lor dpal spungs yang khrod du phebs nas bka' chos mang du stsal ba'i zla ba bcu gcig pa'i phyi ma'i tshes drug gi nyin rdor gling rdzogs chen pha rgyud lta ba klong yangs
kyi dbang gi dngos gzhi stsal ba'i nub mo mnal lam du/ rje nyid lho brag la yag phyogs su khyim bdag zhig gi chung ma rdo rje 'tsho zer ba zhig tu gyur nas 'jig rten
pa'i las thabs la spyod kyin 'dug pa'i skabs shig /khyim bdag des bla ma tshang phebs yong ba red/ gdan gsham dgos zer nas khang pa shig tu byi dor dang gdan bshams pa la
dar cig nas rdo rje gling pa yin zer

ba'i bla ma bong thung sku sha rgyas pa/ thor tshugs chung ngu dang dbu ral yod pa/ stod 'bogs ser po mnabs pa zhig phebs pa la phyag dbang dang bsnyen bkur sogs zhus/ de nub
der bzhugs pa'i mdun du phyin nas de nyid kyis lag bcangs dang 'o byed pa dang 'khyud pa sogs rol rtsed sna tshogs kyis dus 'das/ de'ang lan re rdor gling dang lan re
jo nang rje btsun yin pa 'dra ba la de gnyis dbye ba mi 'byed pa'i za zi zhig gi ngang / nam langs rjes bsnyen bkur 'dra zhus nas/ bla ma rta la chibs/ grwa pa rkang thang
'ga' re dang bcas phebs song / bzhugs khri'i thog tu sgam 'dra ba ldir ldir dar gyis bkab pa zhig 'dug pa/ bla ma tshang sku chas lus 'dug byas de khur nas rjes la rgyug
'bod pa bcas rjes zin pa na phyag tu phul bas 'di khong gi gter rdzas sgam yin/ der lus pa rten 'brel bzang bas khyod rang nas tshags rtsa byed dgos gsungs/ der skyes dman
du song ba dang yul 'pho dgos pa 'dra zhig kyang dran yul du 'dug pa sogs kyis/ kho mos tshags rtsa gtan nas mi thub/ nya ra byed mi phod/ ci dgos kyang mi shes sogs
zhus pas/ skyon med/ re zhig tshags rtsa gyis dang nga rang sleb 'ong gsungs/ nyid nam byon dang gar byon mi shes/ tshags rtsa mi phod pas byin rlabs shig zhu zhus pas/ sgam
kha phye ba'i nang nas shog ser shog dril chen po blangs nas/ gsang sngags lung gi bka' tho chen mo bzhugs so/ /zhes pa'i 'phros su rdor gling gter chos da lta grags
pa ma grags pa mang po zhig gi dkar chags 'dra ba zhig tshang bar bklags te sgam du bcug /de mgo la bzhag nas 'di tshags rtsa gyis dang nged kyi sprul sku khyod rtsar slebs
'ong gsungs/ nga ni na so

cung rgan/ bla ma 'di ni gzhon pas sprul sku nged la 'khrungs pa'i srid dogs med snyam sprul sku nam 'byon zhus pas/ da phan lo lnga brgya tsam na i mi 'byon gsungs/ sgam bu
khyer nas log khar bla ma 'di o rgyan dngos yin 'dug pas kong sprul ma yum de skye ba ci red dri dgos snyam nas de don zhus pas/ chu gnas zhig tu skyes gsungs/ der shin
tu 'gyod pas dus nas chu gnas ci 'dra dang da ci drag zhus pas/ 'on kyang da ni drag le yod/ mi 'khrugs pa zhig byas nas gsung skabs nyid kyi dgongs pa la'ang chu gnas de/
nor bu'i khang pa dang rgyan sogs la longs spyod pa'i ya mtshan can zhig 'dug snyam byed pa'i ngang de las sad gsungs/ rdo rje 'tsho 'di ni dus rgyun dran lam gsal cing
/ bla ma bka' 'dus dang hU~M skor snying thig rnams zhus pa'i skabs su'ang rdor gling nyid mdun gyi drang thad 'dir dngos su bzhugs par gsal ba dang / chos thun tshugs
nas ma rdzogs kyi bar snang sems ro gcig tu 'dres nas sku lus kyang zur du yod med mi 'byed pa 'dra zhig 'byung 'dug gsungs/ lta ba klong yangs dbang lung rgyun ma chad par
bzhugs pa tsam las gter chos gzhan dpe tsam yang dkon pa la thabs rtsol du mas bla ma bka' 'dus/ bka' brgyad gsang rdzogs/ thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho dang ngan
song kun skyob/ hU~M skor snying thig /ma rgyud klong gsal 'bar ma rnams kyi dbang lung bka' drin rtsal grub pa byung / de las gzhan pa'i dpe rgyun gtan nas ma rnyed/
'dus pa skor bzhi las mkha' 'gro bka' 'dus brda yig phyag tu babs kyang gtan la 'bebs grub pa ma byung / rin chen gling pa'i ye shes kyi skus khong nyid kyi bla rdzogs thugs

gsum gyi snying po'i bcud dril gnang nas byin gyis brlabs pa ltar/ me phag zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyer dgu la rdzogs pa chen po gcig chod kun grol gyi dbang lung khrid bcas
bka' drin tu stsal ba'i nub mo mnal lam du/ rgya gar yul yangs pa de'u 'bur mang po yod pa zhig tu phebs/ der mi chas dkar rta dkar la phreng bkal/ gyen 'greng sogs zhon
tshul mi 'dra bar byas pa shin tu mang po'i nang khye'u dar thod can shin tu mdzes pa mo skad can zhig byung nas/ sku zhabs nyid 'dir phebs pa la nged kyi pha ma gnyis dga'
tshor chen po byed/ gsol tshigs zhig zhu dgos zer 'dug pas rta 'di chibs nas gsol tshigs la 'byon par zhu zer/ rta mi dgos khyod rang khyer gsungs pas khos pho ba sga
gong du bkal te 'gro 'dug pa'i rjes la phebs pas pha waM zhig gi rtsar slebs/ der sgo zhig 'dug pa nas nang du phebs pas 'jag khyim lta bu'i nang mdo sbugs gnyis lta bu zhig
'dug pa'i sbugs su bzhugs/ bgres po bgres mo dar dkar thod dang gos can gzi brjid chen po can gnyis 'dug pas yungs ma btsos pa lta bu zhig drangs pa shar 'dug /mi sha
yin nam snyam pa'i 'phrig pa skyes pas thugs dogs gnang mi dgos/ bzhes pa zhu zer/ khyed gnyis su yin gsungs pas nged gnyis dus rtag tu 'dir sdod mkhan yin/ /pha waM rus
sbal nag po zer ba'ang 'di gar yod zer/ khyed gnyis la ming ci yin gsungs pas/ nged gnyis ming mang yang skabs rer pha la legs ldan nag po zer/ ma la e ka dzA Ti zer/ bu
'di la dpal mgon ma ning zer ba yin/ bod nas sngar rin chen gling pa 'dir byung / rdzogs chen chos gtod dgos zer/ nged kyi snying

nor yin pas shin tu phangs kyang kho la o rgyan padmas gnang ba red pas mi gtad ka med byung / chos de sngar dus dang po byung / de rjes rgyun ma chad tsam yod pa la phyis
su chad song bas nged tsho ma dga'/ da res khyed nas spel ba la nged rnams shin tu dga' bas phrin las sgrub zer ba byung gsungs/ yang phyag mjal mang po 'ong ba'i skabs shig
/sngar grub chen thang stong rgyal pos mnga' ris dbus gtsang mdo khams gsum du sku'i bkod pa gsum du bstan pa'i ya gyal/ mnga' ris stod gu ge rong du byung ba'i grub
mchog tshul khrims bzang po zhes dgung lo brgya dang sum cu bzhugs kyang sku la bgres rgud kyi skyon med cing gzhon nu'i tshul du bzhugs nas mthar 'od kyi phung por dengs
pa de nyid bya bral gyi cha byad can mngon sum du byon nas/ khong nyid la 'phags pa thugs rje chen pos stsal ba'i yi ge drug pa'i gsol 'debs kyi sgom bzlas de dpe dang bcas
stsal nas gar song ma byung / sgrub thabs de nyid rig gtad bcas pas kyang 'gro ba mang po rjes su 'dzin par mdzad cing sgrub thabs 'di ni mchog dman kun la phan thogs
shing byin rlabs kyi babs chen po dang ldan pa yin pas yi drug grangs gsog mkhan rnams kyis kyang bzlas pa'i gzhi 'di tsam nyams su lon na byas la ma bsags pa'i las su mi
'gyur bar bde ba can bya ba'i ming snyan po der smon lam btab na'ang don dang ldan par snang ngo / /pad gling gter slob nyer gcig gi gras 'gro 'dul las 'phro gling pa'i
gter chos thugs chen don gsal sgron me 'di'i sgo nas gter ston nyid kyis bum sgrub lan grangs drug cu rtsa gnyis mdzad/ sras brgyud lnga'i bar du 'gro don shin tu rgyas
kyang deng sang dbang lung gi

rgyun mi bzhugs pa la/ gter ston nyid kyis nye brgyud byin rlabs rjes gnang stsal ba ltar/ chu lug zla ba dang po'i tshes nang 'di'i dbang bskur rnams gnang ba'i nub mor/ bud
med nang gos steng stod g.yogs dmar po lhub gyon/ skra rgyab tu bsdams pa zhig gis shel dmar lta bu'i gwa'u zhig khyer nas/ 'di nang bram ze skye bdun sha ril stong phrag
gsum yod pa sngar las 'phro gling pa la phul ba khong 'gro don che bas da gcig las lhag mi 'dug /'di da res las 'phro gling pas khyed la phul shog gsungs pa yin zer ga'u
dbu thog tu bzhag nas par pir mang po brjod nas byin rlabs 'dra ba zhig byas/ de nas bram ze su red dris pas zla ba bzang po red zer/ 'o na zla bzang sprul sku zer ba
de'i skye ba yin nam dris pas de'i 'od zer phog pa tsam byas na chog rgyu red/ ril bu 'di shin tu rtsa ba che bas bca' ga yag po dgos zer bzhugs sa'i nye logs kyi rten sgam
zhig tu bcug song ba/ phyis ril bu dngos su yod 'dug pa la gta' spel yang mdzad/ mkha' 'gro ma de padma'i drwa ba can red gsungs/ me yos zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes drug
nub mnal lam du rin po che nyid kyis rta zhig chibs/ grwa pa rkang thang bzhi tsam bcas zab bu lung mjal du phebs kyin 'dug pa/ gnas mdar sngags pa zhig gis khyim du gdan
drangs/ dbang dang byin rlabs zhus/ bsnyen bkur bstabs/ des mtshon lam du gar phebs pa yin zhu mkhan thams cad la/ zab bu lung gter lung mjal du 'gro ba yin kho na gsungs
kyin 'dug /lam du char pa 'ga' zhig babs pa/ grwa pa rnams nas de ring sdug gnam 'dis ga 'drar byed pa yin na zer ba la/ dga' mo yong 'gro gsungs kyin

phebs/ phyi dro lung pa'i rked tsam sleb pa chu phar ka der 'brog dud phyug po zhig 'dug pa/ che chung med pa thams cad chu tshur kar brgyugs nas byin rlabs zhus/ da ci tsam
'gro dgos dris pa da dung lam phyed las ma slebs tshul bshad/ do dgong bzhugs gnas gar 'ben dris par 'di yan chad char skyibs sogs stabs bde med tshul lab pa grwa pa rnams
nas/ 'o na do dgong khyer rang tshang la gnas tshang i g.yar byas song ba/ nangs snga bar pheb rgyu yin tshe g.yar rgyu yod zer/ de ka yin tshul gyis chu phar kar phyin
par dud tshang des ltag sbra chung logs dang sa thams cad stan dkar gyis g.yogs pa zhig nang bzhag /gsol thug sogs bskyal/ sang nyi shar la bla ma mnga' bdag pa phebs
rgyu yin/ de pa gtsang sbra shin tu che ba yin pas/ nyid dpon slob nas pho gtor sogs 'bag 'bog mi mdzad par zhu 'dug /de nub thugs dam 'dra mdzad kyin bzhugs/ nangs nam langs
pa dang tsha ba bzhes nas chibs btegs te lung pa'i phu la phebs te 'grul ba 'dras lam ngo sprad cing / zab lung bde gshegs 'dus pa'i pho brang du pheb pa dang / pha
wang zhig gi skyibs su rnal 'byor pa thor tshugs chung ngu yod pa/ rab byung chas/ sku bong mi che mi chung / sku sha ran pa/ zhal rgyan cung zad yod pa zhig char yibs lta
bus bzhugs 'dug pa bzhengs nas/ khong 'phreng mgo gter ston shes rab 'od zer yin/ khyed phebs pa rten 'brel shin tu bzang bas da lta gter 'don par 'gro gsungs/ dgyes bzhin
phebs pas pha wang zhig nas shog dril zhig phyung / de ma thag bdag gu Na sa mu dra da lta'i byad dbyibs ci lta bar gnas 'gyur nas/

shog ser 'di'i chos bdag khyed rang yin pas da lta rang du lung bya zhes shog ser tshar gcig dag par bklags song ba grol thig gi chos sde shes rab blo 'phel mi brjed gzungs
thob der snang gsungs/ rje nyid 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug yin pa'i thugs shes gsal yod 'dug /yang rab yid me 'brug zla ba gsum pa'i tshes nyer gcig nyin phran
rje'i spyan sngar phyin pa'i snga nub tshes nyi shu'i tho rangs 'od gsal du/ bud med gos sngon gyon pa zhig gis da 'gro gsungs pa'i rjes la pheb pa'i lam du grog rong
zhig 'dug pa la bud med de 'phur song ba'i rjes la/ rje nyid kyang 'phur nas phebs pas chos dbang dag snang sogs dang phyogs mtshungs kyi lam zhor rgya bod bal po'i yul
khams ra ri tsam shar ba'i mthar ri bo smug pas rtse btums pa zhig mthong ba je nyer song ba dang ri ngos de mchod rten rnam pa je gsal song / khad nyer phebs pas ri sngon
rgyab gnyis su yod pa'i mdun ma de phyi mchod rten dbyibs shin tu gsal ba'i ri bo/ /seng khri'i phyogs bzhir sgo 'dug pas phyogs bzhi kar phebs kyang sgo rnams bcad pas
nang du ma brtol/ ri de'i rgyu mtshan sogs bud med de la dris pas/ 'di shAnta pu ri'i grong khyer yin zer/ der phreng mgo gter chen shes rab 'od zer gar bzhugs/ kho bo mjal
du 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ 'dir dpa' bo thod pa'i dum bu rtsal zer/ khong deng sang bod du bzhugs yod/ 'dir sku gdung la mchod pa rtag tu 'bul ba'i lha dang mkha' 'gro
sogs 'dus pa yin zer/ sgo'i bu ga sgo zhig nas gsan pas phe hrang gi 'phrul 'khor lta bu'i rol mo'i sgra snyan la yid 'phrog pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gdangs/ rgyud kyi
tshigs su bcad pa ngo mtshar ba sgrogs pa zhig

gsan pa mchod 'bul gyi rol mo'i sgra yin zer/ bod du phebs dus dpa' bo thod pa'i dum bu dngos ji ltar 'gyur dris pas/ ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag pa lta bus gsung mi
smra ba zhig tu 'gyur/ bod nas slar phebs pa dang gsung gis chos ston pa zhig tu 'gyur ba'i khyad par yod zer/ de nas rgyab ngos ri gnyis pa de smug po zhig la de nas thag
ring du song 'dug pa zangs mdog dpal ri yin zer bas de'i rtse mor 'phur nas phebs pas/ padma 'od kyi gzhal yas yin nam snyam pa ha cang bkod pa'i khyad par mtshar du med
pa'i pho brang sum thog zhig gi 'og khang du phyin pas gu ru za hor ma la mtshan brgyad kyis bskor ba/ de'i bar khang du phebs pas spyan ras gzigs rgyal ba rgya mtsho la
nye sras brgyad kyis bskor ba/ de gnyis ka sku brnyan gyi rnam par mjal/ steng khang du phebs pas 'od sngon po'i rang bzhin du gzigs nas dag snang las sad gsungs/ 'di dag
gi rgyu mtshan la sogs pa las 'phrang 'go gter ston shes rab 'od zer gyi gter chos kyang nye brgyud byed chog pa yin gsungs/ de las gzhan pa phyis kyi gter ston 'ja' tshon
snying po'i ye shes kyi sku dngos dang snga rjes mjal nas gter chos nye brgyud kyi byin rlabs gsan pa dang / stag sham bsam gtan gling pa/ klong gsal snying po sogs
kyi yang gter dang nye brgyud bzhugs tshugs kyang so so'i brgyud 'dzin rnams la bka' stsal gnang bar thos so/ /bzhi pa zab mo dgongs pa'i gter ni/ sku chung ngu'i dus nas
sngon gnas rjes su dran pa dang tshigs bcad sgrub thabs mang po thol byung thogs med du 'byung ba zhig bzhugs yod 'dug kyang de 'dra'i rigs gal chung btang

snyoms kho nas dmigs med du rgyas btab/ dgung lo nyer dgur son pa'i sa sprel lor bod yul dbus su phebs pa'i byang lam dge rgyal phyogs su khrums zla'i tshes bcur khel bas bla
ma gsang 'dus tshogs mchod mdzad pas thugs nyams 'bar/ phyi rol tu phebs skabs brag phug kha lho nub tu blta ba yid du 'ong ba zhig 'dug pa'i nang du phebs pas thugs spro
bar byung nas bla ma'i rnal 'byor zh-ig mdzad pa'i mthar cung zad mnal du song ba la sgra chen po zhig grags pas sad pa na/ mdun gyi nam mkhar gu ru za hor ma'i chas
can gtso 'khor gsum mngon sum byon nas brda'i byin rlabs stsal te nyid la thim pa'i rjes thog tu mtsho skyes snying thig gi rtsa ba'i chos skor thugs la lam mer gsal bas
de nyid du las byang rdzogs par gtan la phab/ de nas tha skar zla ba'i tshes bco lngar bsam yas su phebs te rdzongs su bzhugs pa'i nyang gter gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rje'i
mdun mchod pa rgyas par phul te snga ma'i las byang btang ba'i tshe sku brnyan de mtsho skyes rdo rje dngos su gyur nas dbang dang gdams pa stsal te nyid la thim pa'i gzigs
snang shar/ yan lag chos skor rnams kyang dgongs pa'i klong du gsal yang ring zhig gsang rgyas btab/ dgung grangs so bdun me 'brug rgyal zla'i yar tshes la gter chen mchog
gyur gling pas rje nyid la bzhugs pa'i zab chos zhig gi smin grol stsol ba'i gsol ba nan du btab pa'i ngor rtsa dbang dang las byang gi bshad pa bcas gnang ba'i nub
mo gter chen mnal lam du/ gu ru rin po ches rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol ba'i ltas khyad par can gzigs/ de'i byin rlabs kyis sna drangs te seng chen gnam brag gi gter kha rnams
kyang phyag tu son/

phyis su bsnyen sgrub mdzad pa'i mthar tshes bcu'i tshogs 'khor skabs thugs nyams 'ur te Da dril bar snang la bzhag pa nye gnas pas kyang mjal ba'i mngon rtags byung / 'di
la'ang bla ma mtsho skyes rdo rje/ yi dam yang dag dmar po/ mkha' 'gro mandA ra ba/ bka' srung dpal mgon ma ning gtso 'khor rnams kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs rim las tshogs dang
bcas pa bzhugs yod par snang rung / gtan la phab pa ni bla ma dang mkha' 'gro'i las byang dbang chog dang bcas pa tsam mo/ /dgung grangs so lnga bzhes pa shing stag rgyal
zla bar 'phags ma yid bzhin 'khor lo lugs 'ga' zhig gi rnal 'byor la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pa'i skabs kyi tho rangs 'od gsal dag pa'i snang char bcom ldan 'das ma yid bzhin
'khor lo yi ge bcu pa'i sgra gdangs can dngos su mjal/ mthar rang nyid la thim pa'i mod la rtog med 'od gsal chen por 'byams klas shing rdo rje gsum dang dbyer mi phyed
pa'i nges shes 'khrungs/ de las sad pa na mdun gyi nam mkha' rig 'dzin shrI siM ha/ bi ma la mi tra/ mtsho skyes rdo rje gsum gtso 'khor dgyes bzhin du bzhugs te brda
don ngo sprod kyi dbang skur stsal ba'i mthar 'od du zhu nas rje nyid la thim pas tha mal gyi rtog pa mtha' dag dbyings su thim/ rig rtsal ma 'gags pa'i 'char sgor 'phags
ma'i snying thig gi gdams skor yongs su rdzogs pa me long nang du gzugs brnyan 'char ba bzhin ma 'dres gcig char du gsal ba'i phyir nyin nas las byang tsam gtan la phabs
shing thugs nyams su bzhes pas bar chad kyi g.yul las rgyal/ khyad par bi ma las yang nas yang du byin rlabs stsal zhing bris zin la zhu dag gi tshul

yang mdzad/ de nas lo lngar gsang rgyas btab ste sa rta lor thog mar gter chen mchog gyur gling pa la smin byed stsal cing chos sgo phyes/ rim par rgyal dbang karma pa bcu
bzhi pa sogs lung zin rnams la gnang ste thams cad kyi sku tshe'i 'phrang bsal cing dge legs kyi rten 'byung yar zla ltar 'phel bar gyur/ 'di la rdzogs rim las tshogs sogs
zab rgyas bzhugs yod 'dug kyang rtsa ba'i phrin las/ dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang / yan lag gi skor las rig 'dzin rnam gsum gyi sgrub skor khyad par can/ tshe dpag med dkar
po dang / rnam rgyal ma'i sgrub thabs tsam 'bebs par mdzad 'dug go /dgung lo bco lnga pa rab yid shing pho rta lo ston zla 'bring po'i tshes bcu bzhi'i tho rangs khar
mnal lam du sa cha 'di yin ngo ma 'tshal ba'i khang bzang bkod legs pa'i nang du maNDal dmar zlum chen po zhig gi steng du sprin dkar shin tu mdzes pa'i dbus grub chen thang
stong rgyal po mkha' 'gro sde lnga dang bcas pa'i mdun du dbang rdzas rnams bkod pas dbang bskur cing gdams pa stsal/ mnal las sad pa na grub chen nyid mngon sum du
mjal ba'i zhal nas/ gzung ba'i yul la mi rtog cing / /'dzin bral rig pa rjen pa'i ngang / /spang blang bsal bzhag bral ba ni/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'o/ /zhes gdams
pa ngo sprod shlo ka gcig stsal nas nyid la thim pas smin grol gdams pa'i skor thugs la bkra gsal gyis 'char bas bco lnga'i nyin grub thob thugs thig gi las byang sogs gtan
la phab par mdzad/ slad nas kyang byin rlabs kyi ltas yang dang yang du byung ba dang / lta sgom spyod pa bogs 'don 'bras bu ste bka' babs lnga'i gdams

ngag ring brgyud bar ma chad pa gsan cing nye brgyud chu bo gcig 'dres su gyur pa nyid/ dgung grangs zhe bdun bzhes pa'i tshe gnas dus kyi rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa la
brten nas 'chi med grub pa'i gnas mchog bkra shis zla gam dbang gi phug par bdag cag skal ldan mchog gi 'dus pa gsum la smin grol bdud rtsi thog mar stsal/ de nas rim par
snyan brgyud rdo rje'i tshig rkang / sgrub thabs snying po skor lnga/ khrag 'thung bde gshegs 'dus pa'i sgrub skor rnams kyang gtan la phab par mdzad/ 'di dag ni sgrub thabs
las tshogs phran tshegs tsam la dgongs gter gyi ming du btags pa dang mi 'dra brgyud lung man ngag gi don zab cing rgya che la tshig nyung zhing 'dril ba gang zag phal
pa'i blo yi spyod yul las 'das pa klong chen rab 'byams bzang po'i gsung dang rjes su mthun par snang ngo / /lnga pa de las 'phros pa rjes su dran pa'i gter ni/ gtso bor
lce btsun chen po'i snying thig ste de'i lo rgyus ni gong du song / lang gro dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyis lo chen bai ro tsa na'i tshe'i sgrub thabs zab mo zhus pa'i sngon
gnas rjes su dran te gtan la phab pa'i tshe sgrub bai ro'i thugs tig dang / lho brag mkhar chur dge slong nam mkha'i snying po la mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis phul ba'i seng
gdong dkar mo'i bcud len rnams bzhugs par snang ba'i phyi ma'i rgyu mtshan gong smos rdo rje phreng ba gsan skabs nub drug pa'i dag snang du shar ba de nyid do/ /drug
pa dag snang gi skor ni/ dgung lo bco lnga pa shing pho rta lo rgyal zla ba'i nang / tshe sgrub zab mo'i bsnyen sgrub mdzad skabs tshes bcu'i tho rangs skabs bzlas thun
