gyi dus su nam mkha' nas Da ma ru'i sgra dang dri bzang gi ngad pa 'thul ba'i rkyen

gyis sgrub rdzas kyi steng du 'od dmar po shin tu gsal ba zhig zhugs song ba'i klong nas 'chi med mandwa ra ba tshe yum tsaNDa lI'i rnam pas yab bka' tshe dpag med hrIHgcig
ma'i skor dang / tshe yum tsaNDa lI'i gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa dbang bskur bcas stsal ba'i mthar shis brjod skabs me tog dmar po'i char sil mar bsnyil ba'i thugs nyams
byung / phyir nang sgrub gzhi'i steng g.yar mo thang lta bu'i me tog dmar po kha shas dngos su snang / de 'phral las byang rtsa ba tsam gtan la phab ste nyams bzhes mdzad
nas gsang rgyas btab/ phyis dgung lo nga dgu rab tshes sa stag lo'i dbyar thog smin grol gyi gdams pa bka' drin tu stsal ba thob/ klong chen pa'i bla sgrub thig le'i rgya
can gyi don gong du song / lcags rta mgo zla ba'i tshes bco lngar dag pa'i snang bar padmas khebs pa'i zhing khams chen por phebs/ der gter chen mchog gyur gling pa nyid
byang chub sems dpa' padma'i myu gu zhes pa'i skur bzhugs par snang ba las/ de nyid kyi sgrub thabs dbang bskur bar do drug khrid bcas kyi gdams pa'i bdud rtsi gsan/
de rjes zla ba gcig tu gsang ba'i dam tshig gi rgyas btab/ rgyal zla ba'i tshes bcur tshogs kyi mchod pa dang rjes su 'brel bar gtan la phab par mdzad pa'i yi ge pa kho bos
zhus pa'i skabs de nyin sa gzhi'i khyon la drod glo bur du babs pas 'khyags pa rnams kyang zhu nas chu bo'i rgyun du 'gyur ba byung ngo / /spyir dag snang la rgyun chad
mi mnga' bas chos sgo mtha' yas pa mnga' ba gzhir bcas kyang sgrub thabs sogs gtan la phab pa ni de tsam las spyod yul du ma gyur to/ /bdun pa de mthun snyan brgyud ni/
dgung grangs zhe brgyad bzhes pa me yos zla ba gsum pa'i nang rdzong

shod bde gshegs 'dus pa'i pho brang du bzhugs pa'i nub gcig 'od gsal gyi snang char mchod rten bde byed brtsegs pa'i drung du phebs/ der bka' babs rig 'dzin brgyad po gu ru
mtshan brgyad kyi rnam pa dang / kun 'dus slob dpon padma thod phreng rnams phyogs mtshams dang dbus su bzhugs pa las rgyud sgyu 'phrul zhi khro/ sgrub chen bka' brgyad
kyi gzhung gdams ngag so sor gsan/ slob dpon chen pos lung a nu dang rdzogs chen a ti'i gdams pa rnams kyang stsal pa phyis bka' brgyad las 'jig rten las 'das pa lnga dang
/ ma mo rbod gtor rnams gtan la phab par mdzad/ de las gzhan pa'i snyan brgyud ji ltar bzhugs sogs ma 'tshal zhing snyan brgyud ces pa'i don ni gsung pa pos gsal bar gsungs
pa de nyid mi brjed pa'i gzungs kyis thugs su chud nas dbu zhabs ma rdzogs kyi bar du ma chad ma lhag par gtan la phab par snang ngo / /sa gter sogs re re la'ang lung
bstan/ kha byang babs tshul/ skul byang / dngos gter bzhes pa'i skabs dang / gter sgrub skabs kyi gzigs snang dang smin grol gsan pa'i tshul/ yun ring por gsang dam mthar
phyin par mdzad nas dus la bab nges pa'i tshe lung dang mthun par skal ldan rnams la spel ba'i tshul rgya cher bzhugs pa smos ci 'tshal yang rje nyid gsang ba srung ba
la thugs shin tu sgam pas su la'ang zur tsam gsung bar dka' zhing phyag tho sogs kyang mi snang bas kho bo la dgos pa'i dbang gis skabs su babs pa kha shas tsam bka' phebs
pa rnams snying la bcangs nas thor bkod pa rnams sgro skur med par bkod pa lags so/ /rdo rje theg pa'i gsang ba mtha' dag

gi snying po bde chen zab lam gyi bka' babs byung ba'i tshul yang / sa stag zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes nyer bzhi'i nub 'od gsal gyi snang char/ rje nyid sku sham rkyang pa tsam
bcas phyag tu 'khar ba rtse mo gsum la ku ba sogs btags pa zhig bsnams nas sa khad yangs pa zhig tu phebs pa/ der shing lo sngon po'i spyil bu zhig 'dug pa sgor phebs
pas/ steng me tog dmar po/ 'og gzhir me tog sna tshogs bkram zhing dri zhim khor yug tu khyab pa'i dbus su grub thob sku bong mi tshad las nyis 'gyur che zhing gzi brjid
can/ ag tshom brang la sleb pa/ dbu ma dar thod/ dar gyi stod g.yogs smad g.yogs can zhig bzhugs pa'i mdun du phebs pas/ khyed kyis nga ngo i shes gsungs/ mi shes lags zhus
pas/ nga ni gnas brtan thams cad kyi gtso bo/ khyed rang thams cad kyi brgyud pa la yod cing gsol ba 'debs yul sa ra ha zhes pa de yin gsungs/ sku chas sogs la brtags
na indra bhU ti min nam dgongs pa'i skabs yang gsungs pa/ ngas ni mi dung phyur zhig la bsnyen rdzogs pa bsgrubs pa yin/ khyed nas da snga bsnyen rdzogs su la ma bsgrubs
'dug pas da ste mi lnga bcu la bsnyen rdzogs bsgrub dgos pas/ nga yis khyed la dngos su bsnyen rdzogs bsgrub gsungs/ der las grwa mi su'ang mi 'dug pas ci 'dra mdzad rgyud
yin dgongs pas/ grogs dan 'di ltar byed gsungs nas lcags kyu'i phyag rgya dang lta stangs mdzad ma thag gnam sa g.yo ba lta bu'i rol mo'i sgra dang glog 'od 'khyugs pa'i
nang du mkha' 'gro sngo sangs rus rgyan can mdzes sdug ltar mi ngom pa zhig glog zhon pa ltar byas nas der byung ste 'khod/ de nas legs sbyar sha stag gis dbang

rgyas pa zhig gnang / rjes zlos rnams kyang legs sbyar mdzad/ bum dbang skabs phyag sbyi bor bzhag /gsang dbang yab yum snyoms 'jug mdzad pa'i byang sems ljags la tshegs med
slebs/ sher dbang mkha' 'gro de gtad/ bzhi pa tshig gi ngo sprod bcas bzhi kar nyams mi 'dra bar re re skyes/ bar mtshams re bzhag /mthar/ de rnams kyis dge bsnyen/ dge
tshul/ dge slong / gnas brtan rgan po'i go 'phang grub pa yin no/ /zhes bod skad gsungs mthar gzung 'dzin rtog pa thams cad 'gags/ sngags kyi nang / tsa turnanda/ zhes gsal
bar gsan/ gzhan rnams la bod skad dang ra 'phrod pa cher ma byung gsungs/ yang shing bya zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nub/ grub chen sa ra ha pa dang indra bhU
ti bar pa la rgyal po dza:zhes grags pa de sngar dus kyi gzigs snang dang phyogs mtshungs par mjal nas khyad par 'phags pa'i thabs lam bzhi tshan bzhi bcu pa zhig gsan
par snang ba gsar rnying gi thabs lam gyi rim pa thams cad phyogs gcig tu dril ba la/ sngar med pa'i zab gnad mang pos khyad par du byas pa'i gzhung ngo mtshar ba zhig bzhugs
yod par 'dug na'ang gtan la 'bebs pa ni lta ga la zhig /zur tsam smos pa'ang bka' rgya dam por snang mod/ dbang rnon chos spyan ldan pa'i rjes 'jug mchis na bka' babs
kun las kyang ngo mtshar ba'i gnas 'di la yid ches bskyed pa'i slad du bkod pa la bla ma dang mkha' 'gros bzod cing tshangs par stsal du gsol/ shrI shrI shrI swa sti bi
dza yantu/ bsam yas bder gshegs sras bcas ye shes yon tan phrin las ji snyed kun/ /dus mtha'i

bstan dang gdul bya'i don phyir snying stobs gong bur gcig dril nas/ /'gran zlas spangs pa'i skyes bu'i khyu mchog lha mi'i bla ma'i skur snang ba/ /mtshan tsam gyis kyang
nyes pa'i mun 'joms thar lam snang mdzad de la 'dud/ /mchog bstan nor 'dzin rtsod pa'i rgya mtshor bying bar phyogs pa'i tshe/ /mkhyen stobs rus sbal stobs kyis bla na btegs
pa'i phrin las la/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing bzhugs dbang stobs rtsal ldan dpa' chen sras dang bcas/ /'jig rten dbang po rnams kyang bsngags pa'i me tog char du bsnyil/ /snyigs
lnga'i rnyogs pas shin tu snyigs gyur dmu rgod 'gror/ /shas cher brtse bas bsam mi khyab pa'i ye shes kun/ /bshes gnyen tshul bzlums thabs mkhas mdzad pa rlabs po ches/
/srid mtshor bying rnams rnam grol skam sar dbugs dbyung mdzad/ /ji snyed shes bya rang spyi'i mtshan nyid gzigs/ /gnas lugs ji lta'i dgongs pa mngon tu gyur/ /chags
dang thogs pa'i dri ma'i gzeb las grol/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes rdo rje rnon por mtshungs/ /gser zhun lta bu'i lhag bsam g.yo med pas/ /ris med bstan dang mchog dman bar ma'i
'gror/ /phyogs suu ma lhungs phan bde'i snang bas skyong / /brtse ba'i thugs rje padma dkar 'dzin dngos/ /lhan skyes grub pa'i mthu stobs rtse brgya pas/ /bdud rigs kla
klo'i dpung tshogs zil gnon pa'i/ /rdo rje'i lung gis rab bsngags lha yi dbang / /nus pa'i rtsal 'chang dpal ldan gsang ba'i bdag /phyi ru brtan mkhas yongs rdzogs 'dul ba
'dzin/ /nang du byang chub mchog spyod rgyal ba'i sras/ /gsang ba dkyil 'khor dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang / /don dam srid zhig kun

la khyab pa'i bdag /snang ba'i mu khyud rgyu skar bye ba snyed/ /kun gsal ngogs su shar la chos mtshungs kyang / /sgrol byed phreng ba ji tsam 'tshogs na yang / /nyi ma'i dkyil
'khor 'gran zlas dben pa bzhin/ /'dzin ma'i gzhi la dngos sbas tshul 'chang ba'i/ /yon tan 'od 'bar 'dren mchog ji snyed pas/ /mdo sngags nyi ma'i gnyen gyur gnyis pa
'di'i/ /rnam thar phyogs re'i char yang 'gran mi bzod/ /des na sras bcas rgyal ba'i rdo rje'i ljags/ /mgrin gcig brkyangs nas bsngags kyang mi dpog pa'i/ /dam pa'i ngang
tshul yid bzhin nor bu'i gter/ /bgrang ba'i ngal ba byis pa blun po'i mtshangs/ /nam mkha'i mtha' dang rgya mtsho'i gtir zab ltar/ /gzhal bar mi bzod zab cing rgya che
la/ /ngo mtshar rmad byung bla ma'i rnam par thar/ /shas tsam gleng ba'ang bsod nams skal ba sbom/ /stong khams ratna'i gram bur brdal 'dra ba'i/ /yon tan mdzod las sher
brtson sor mo'i rtses/ /cung zad thob pa dad blo'i gser bzang gi /skud par brgyus 'di skal ldan mgrin pa'i rgyan/ /mtshan tsam gyis kyang sangs rgyas mdzad pa sgrub/ /thos
dang dran pas rnam grol mchog sbyin pa/ /bden gsung tshad mas grub phyir phyogs mtshon tsam/ /brjod pa 'di yang don ldan 'bras bus lci/ /de phyir phul byung ngag tu ma
'khyog par/ /rang bzhin brjod par rang 'dod tshig sbyor gyi/ /dri mas ma reg sa bon tsam 'di las/ /tshig sbyor dpag bsam ljon bzang bskrun par gsol/ /de yis mos ldan dad
pa'i mig bye zhing / /des kyang skye dgu ngan 'gro'i g.yang las sgrol/ /rang gzhan thar pa'i grong du bder 'jug pa'i/ /don chen 'grub

'di thugs bskyed stobs su grub/ /spang rtogs mthar phyin rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dngos/ /mdo sngags chos sgo bsam yas 'byung ba'i gnas/ /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag
he ru ka /mnyam med dpal ldan bla mar slar yang 'dud/ /rdul snyed lus sprul de snyed bstod dbyangs sgrog /skyabs gnas gcig chog nyid du nges pa yi/ /mos pa'i blo yis zhabs
pad ze'u 'bru la/ /spyi bos gtugs te rtag tu phyag bgyi'o/ /rgyal bas rab bsngags bzang po spyod pa yi/ /mchod sprin bla bre bla na ma mchis pa/ /chos dbyings rgyas par
bres te gul phul bas/ /zag med dgongs pa mthar thug skong gyur cig /'khrul pa'i g.ya' dris chos khams gser bzang la/ /sgrib pa'i lhag ma dang bcas stobs bzhi'i chus/ /legs
par bkrus pas bdag gzhan 'gro kun rgyud/ /rnam dag tshangs pa'i bzhin ras gsal bar mdzod/ /srid rtsa zhi ba'i dbyings su gcod pa'i 'khrul/ /'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa'i
legs spyad klung / /rnam thar rgya mtshor gcig tu bzlums pa la/ /yi rang padmo 'dzum pas mdzes par bgyi/ /gang 'dul chos sgras ma rig gnyid slong zhing / /khyad par gsang
chen rdo rje na da'i dbyangs/ /gdul bya'i rna bar rgyun mi 'chad 'babs pas/ /rtsol med gdod ma'i grub mtha' snyogs par gsol/ /de bzhin nyid dbyings skye 'gag gdod nas
bral/ /rgyal rnams kun rdzob bden par rton mi mdzad/ /'gro khams mdzad pa med phyir gshis kyi skur/ /rtag brtan g.yung drung chen por bzhugs gsol 'debs/ /zag bcas zag med
yongs grub rnam dkar tshogs/ /'gro kun srid mtsho bying las myur bton

nas/ /bla ma sangs rgyas nyid 'grub phyir bsngo ba/ /rgyas sras dpa' bo rnams kyi rjes su slob/ /'di bzung byang chub snying por mchis kyi bar/ /skye kun rje btsun bla mas
rjes bzung ste/ /'bral med spyi bo'i rgyan tu bzhugs nas kyang / /gsang ba gsum gyi byin rlabs rgyud la stsol/ /rtag tu mnyes pa'i bya ba mthar phyin sgrub/ /mi mnyes log
lta skad cig mi 'byung zhing / /gsung gi mdzod 'dzin thugs kyi dgongs bcud lon/ /rnam thar phrin las yongs rdzogs 'grub par shog /byin rlabs rdzogs ldan sprin chen 'khrigs
pa las/ /phan bde nor bu'i gru char rtag 'bebs pas/ /'di gtan 'dod rgu yid bzhin 'jo mdzad pa/ /khyab bdag bla ma'i shes pas skyong gyur cig /ces khams gsum 'gro ba'i
bla ma bka' drin mnyam med thams cad mkhyen gzigs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar sa bon tsam du smos pa 'di
nyid/ rigs kyi dbon mkhyen dpyod phul byung dge blos rgyud phyug pa su bha ga badzra nas bkra shis pa'i lha reg /sa'i snying po srang 'khor gyi rten bcas bskul ba dang
/ rje nyid kyi thugs zin rim gro ba lnga rig smra ba'i dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs legs pa'i blo gros nas kyang gsung nan chen pos bskul ba ltar/ rje bla ma nyid kyi bka' drin
chen pos thun min tu bskyangs zhing ris med pa'i bstan pa la snying nas gus pa'i ku sA li blo gros mtha' yas pa'i sdes/ phyi nang gsang ba'i rnam thar gyi rtsa tshig
dang / phyi'i rnam thar rtsa tho rje rin po che nyid kyis dngos su stsal ba rnams gzhir byas/ gsan yig dang gshegs rjes dgongs rdzogs bsgrubs tshul

sogs kyi yi ge'i rigs mdor bsdus/ dag snang skor sogs zhal nas dngos su thos rim gyi zin bris btab pa rnams phyogs su bsdus te bgyis pa bgrang bya mtho zhing shes rig brtul
bas/ rjod byed kyi tshig tshogs la dpyod ldan dgyes pa'i rnam dpyod ma mchis kyang / brjod bya'i don la sgro skur gyi mtha' dang bral zhing nor 'khrul gyi rnyogs pa ma mchis
pas/ rje'i bka' slob mkhas grub rnams kyis 'di la brten nas tshigs sbyor phun sum tshogs pas gsal la rgyas par spro ba gsol ba 'debs pa lags/ 'di'ang rang lo gya gcig
tu son pa chu sprul nag pa zla bar rtsA 'dra rin chen brag gi sgrub gnas kun bzang bde chen 'od gsal gling du bkod pa'i yi ge'i ris su spel ba po gnas lnga rig pa'i blo
gros can dge ba'i bshes gnyen karma bkra shis chos 'phel gyis bgyis pa ste/ gsang ba bsgrags pa sogs nongs pa gang mchis bla ma mkha' 'gro srung ma dang bcas pa'i spyan
sngar bshags shing / dge bas mtha' yas pa'i sems can thams cad dpal ldan bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang myur du thob pa'i rgyur gyur cig /sarba thA manggal ka lyA
Ni bha wantu// // ! oM swa sti/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa dus mthar bsring pa la/ /smon lam thugs dam dus kyis sad pa las/ /phyogs dang ris med phan bde'i mchog sbyin pa/ /rje
btsun bla ma snying rje'i gter la 'dud/ /gang gi rnam thar ji bzhin 'chad pa'i bdag /ngag gi dbang phyug chen po nyid 'os phyir/ /yon tan rgya mtsho'i gter kha phye ba yi/
/gtam gyi bdud rtsi skal bzang yid kyi gsos/ /tshul 'dir shes nas dad pa'i skye bo la/ /rnam grol sgo chen dbye slad spar gyi 'phrul/ /

gtong ba'i bkraX shisaX tshe rabs kun 'phel bas/ /sde bzhis dge byas rgyal khab chen por bskrun/ /bla ma'i yon tan sgrogs pa'i bsod nams la/ /rlabs chen dge ba cis kyang mi
bskrun pa'i/ /dpal des dad can sbyin pa'i bdag po gtsos/ /'brel bcas nges par legs pas 'tsho gyur cig /thugs rje'i mkha' nas byin rlabs nyi ma'i 'od/ /skal ldan dad pa'i
pad rdzing la zhugs te/ /legs lam spyod pas dus kyi dga' ston dang / /lhan cig bstan 'gro'i phun tshogs rgyas gyur cig /ces rje btsun bla ma de nyid la kha tsam ma yin pa'i
dad gus dang ldan pa sde dge gnyer chen bkra shis tshe 'phel nas yon sbyar zhing rje nyid kyi dbon su bha ga'i mthun rkyen las brten legs par grub pa'i tshe mchog tu
dga' zhing rjes su yi rangs pa'i blo gros las byung ba dge/
